Chandogya-Upanisad (Chandogyopanisad)
with the commentary ascribed to Samkara


Input by members of the Sansknet project
(formerly: www.sansknet.org)


This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding.
Therefore, word boundaries are usually not marked by blanks.
These and other irregularities cannot be standardized at present.

The mula text has been checked against the ed. by V.P. Limaye and R.D. Vadekar
(Eighteen Principal Upanisads, vol. 1, Poona 1958), and the electronic version
available on TITUS. In cases of divergence, preference has usually been given
to the printed edition.

The text of the commentary is not proofread!


REFERENCE SYSTEM:
ChUp_n,n.n = mula text
ChUpBh_n,n.n = Samkara's Bhasya

#<...># = BOLD

#<oM>#
sAmavedIyA
#<chAndogyopaniShat>#


atha prathamo 'dhyAyaH
ApyAyantu mamAN^gAni vAkprANashcakShuH shrotramatho balamindriyANi ca sarvANi, sarvaM brahmaupaniShadaM mAhaM brahma nirAkuryAM mA mA brahma nirAkarodanirAkaraNamastvanirAkaraNaM me 'stu, tadAtmani nirate ya upaniShatsu dharmAste mayi santu te mayi santu //

oM shAntiH shAntiH shAntiH
shrImacchaN^karabhagavatpAdAcAryaviracitaM bhAShyam upodghAtaH-
"omityetadakSharam" ityAdyaShTAdhyAyI chAndogyopaniShat /
tasyAH saMkShepator'thajij~nAsubhya R^ijuvivaraNamalpagranthashrImannarendrapurIyatIndraviracitaM chAndogyopaniShadbhAShyaTippaNamidamArabhyate /
tatra sambandhaH- samastaM karmAdhigataM prANAdidevatAvij~nAnasahitamarcirAdimArgeNa brahmalokapratipattikAraNam /
kevalaM ca dhUmAdimArgeNa candralokapratipattikAraNam /
svabhAvapravR^ittAnAM ca mArgadvayaparibhraShTAnAM kaShTAdhogatiruktA /
na cobhayormArgayoranyatarasminnapi mArge AtyantikI puruShArthasiddhirityataH karmanirapekShamadvaitAtmavij~nAnaM saMsAragatitrayahetUpamardena vaktavyamityupaniShadArabhyate /
na cAdvaitAtmavij~nAnAdanyatrA'tyantikI niHshreyasaprAptiH /
vakShyati hi-"atha ye 'myathAto viduranyarAjAnaste kShayyalokA bhavanti" /
viparyaye ca"sa svarADbhavati"iti /
tathA dvaitaviShayAnR^itAbhisandhasya bandhanaM taskarasyeva taptaparashugrahaNe bandhadAhabhAvaH, saMsAraduHkhaprAptishcetyuktvAdvaitAtmasatyAbhisandhasyAtaskarasyeva taptaparashugrahaNe bandhadAhAbhAvaH saMsAraduHkhanivR^ittirmokShashceti /
ata eva na karmasahabhAv.dvaitAtmadarshanam /
kriyAkArakaphalabhedopamardena"sadekamevAdvitIyam" "AtmaivedaM sarvam" ityevamAdivAkyajanitasya bAdhakapratyayAnupapatteH /
karmavidhipratyaya iti cet /
na /
kartR^ibhoktR^isvabhAvavij~nAnavatastajjanitakarmaphalarAgadveShAdidoShavatashca karmavidhAnAt /
adhigatasakalavedArthasya karmavidhAnAdadvaitaj~nAnavato 'pi karmeti cet /
na /
karmAdhikR^itaviShayasya kartR^ibhoktrAdij~nAnasya svAbhAvikasya"sadekamevAdvitIyam""AtmaivedaM sarvam" ityanenopamarditatvAt /
tasmAdavidyAdidoShavata eva karmANi vidhIyante /
nAdvaitaj~nAnavataH /
ata eva hi vakShyati-"sarva ete puNyalokA bhavanti /
brahmasastho 'mR^itatvameti"iti /
tatraitasminnadvaitavidyAprakaraNe 'bhyudayasAdhanAnyupAsanAnyucyante kaivalyasannikR^iShTaphalAni /
cAdvaitAdIShadvIkR^itabrahmaviShayANi ityAdIni karmasamR^iddhiphalAni ca karmAN^gasambandhIni /
rahasyasAmAnyAnmanovR^ittisAmAnyAcca yathAdvaitaj~nAnaM manovR^ittimAtraM tathAnyAnyapyupAsanAni manovR^ittirUpANItyasti hi sAmAnyam /
kastarhyadvaitaj~nAnasyopAsanAnAM ca visheShaH /
ucyate /
svAbhAvikasyA'tmanyakriye 'dhyAropitasya kartrAdikArakakriyAphalabhedavij~nAnasya nivartakamadvaitavij~nAnam /
rajjvAdAviva sarpAdyadhyAropalakShaNaj~nAnasya rajjvAdisvarUpanishcayaH prakAshanimittaH /
upAsanaM tu yathAshAstrasamarpitaM kiJNcidAlambanamupAdAya tasminsamAnacittavR^ittisantAnakaraNaM tadvilakShaNapratyayAnantaritamiti visheShaH /
tAnyetAnyupAsanAni sattvashuddhikaratvena vastutattvAvabhAsakatvAdadvaitaj~nAnopakArakANyAlambanaviShayatvAt susAdhyAni ceti pUrvamupanyasyante /
tatra karmAbhyAsasya dR^iDhIkR^itatvAtkarmaparityAgenopAsana eva duHkhaM cetaH samarpaNaM kartR^imiti karmAN^gaviShayameva tAvadAdAvupAsanamupanyasyate /


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.1

#<om ity etad akSharam udgItham upAsIta |
om iti hy udgAyati |
tasyopavyAkhyAnam || ChUp_1,1.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.1 ityupodghAtabhAShyam- omityetadakSharamudgIthamupAsIta /
omityetadakSharaM paramAtmano 'bhidhAnaM nediShTham /
tasminhi prayujyamAne sa prasIdati priyanAmagrahaNa iva lokaH /
tadihetiparaM prayuktamabhidhAyakatvAdvyAvartitaM shabdasvarUpamAtraM pratIyate /
tathA cArcAdivatparasyA'tmanaH pratIkaM sampadyate /
evaM nAmatvena pratIkatvena ca paramAtmopAsanasAdhanaM shreShThamiti sarvavedAnteShvagatam /
japakarmasvAdhyAyAdyanteShu ca bahushaH prayogAtprasiddhamasya shraiShThyam /
atastadetakSharaM varNAtmakamudgIthabhaktyavayavatvAdudgIthashabdavAcyamupAsIta /
karmAN^gAvayavabhUta oN^kAre paramAtmapratIke dR^iDhAmaikAgryalakShaNAM matiM santanuyAt /
svayameva shrutiroN^kArasyodgIthashabdavAcyatve hetumAha-omiti hyudgAyati /
omityArabhya hi yasmAdudgAyatyata udgItha oN^kAra ityarthaH /
tasyopavyAkhyAnaM tasyAkSharasyopavyAkhyAnamevamupAsanamevaMvibhUtyevaMphalamityAdikathanamupavyAkhyAnam /
pravartata iti vAkyasheShaH //1 //

_______________________________________________________________________


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.2

#<eShAM bhUtAnAM pR^ithivI rasaH |
pR^ithivyA Apo rasaH |
apAm oShadhayo rasaH |
oShadhInAM puruSho rasaH |
puruShasya vAg rasaH |
vAca R^ig rasaH |
R^icaH sAma rasaH |
sAmna udgItho rasaH || ChUp_1,1.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.2 eShAM carAcarANAM bhUtAnAM pR^ithivI raso gatiH parAyaNamavaShTambhaH /
pR^ithivyA Apo raso 'psu hyotA ca protA ca pR^ithivyatastA rasaH pR^ithivyAH /
apAmoShadhayo raso 'ppariNAmatvAdoShadhInAm /
tAsAM puruSho raso 'nnapariNAmatvAt puruShasya /
tasyApi puruShasya vAgrasaH /
puruShAvayavAnAM hi vAksAriShThA /
ato vAkpuruShasya rasa ucyate /
tasyA api vAca R^igrasaH sAratarA /
R^icaH sAma rasaH sArataram /
tasyApi sAmna udgIthaH prakR^itatvAdoN^kAraH sArataraH //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.3

#<sa eSha rasAnAM rasatamaH paramaH parArdhyo 'ShTamo yadudgIthaH || ChUp_1,1.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.3 evaM sa eSha udgIthAkhya oN^kAro bhUtAdInAmuttarottararasAnAmatishayena raso rasatamaH /
paramaH paramAtmapratIkatvAt /
parArdhyor'dhaM sthAnaM, paraM ca tadardhaM ca parArdhaM tadarhatIti parArdhyaH paramAtmasthAnArhaH paramAtmavadupAsyatvAdityabhiprAyaH /
aShTamaH pR^ithivyAdirasasaMkhyAyAM yadudgItho ya udgIthaH //3 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.4

#<katamA katama rk katamat katamat sAma katamaH katama udgItha iti vimR^iShTaM bhavati || ChUp_1,1.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.4 vAca R^igrasa ityuktam /
katamA sarkkatamattatsAma katamo vA sa udgIthaH /
katamA katameti vIpsA'darArthA /
nanu"vA bahUnAM jAtipariprashne Datamac" /
na hyatra R^igjAtibahutvaM kathaM DatamacprayogaH /
naiSha doShaH /
jAtau pariprashno jAtipariprashna ityetasminvigrahe jAtAvR^igvyaktInAM bahutvopapatteH /
na tu jAteH pariprashna iti vigR^ihyate /
nanu jAteH pariprashna ityasminvigrahe katamaH kaTha ityAdyudAharaNamupapannaM jAtau pariprashna ityatra tu na yujyate /
tatrApi kaThAdijAtAveva vyaktibahitvAbhiprAyeNa pariprashna ityadoShaH /
yadi jAteH pariprashnaH syAtkatamA katamargityAdAvupasaMkhyAnaM kartavyaM syAdvimR^iShTaM bhavati vimarshaH kR^ito bhavati //4 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.5

#<vAg evark |
prANaH sAma |
om ity etad akSharam udgIthaH |
tad vA etan mithunaM yad vAk ca prANash cark ca sAma ca || ChUp_1,1.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.5 vimarshe hi kR^ite sati prativacanoktirupapannA vAgevarkprANaH sAmeti /
vAgR^icorekatve 'pi nAShTamatvavyAghAtaH pUrvasmAdvAkyAntaratvAdAptiguNasiddhaya omityetadakSharamudgItha iti /
vAkprANAvR^iksAmayonI iti vAgevarkprANaH sAmetyucyate /
yathAkramamR^iksAmayonyorvAkprANayorgrahaNe hi sarvAsAmR^icAM sarveShAM ca sAmnAmavarodhaH kR^itaH syAt /
sarvarksAmAvarodhe carksAmasAdhyAnAM ca sarvakarmaNAmavarodhaH kR^itaH syAt /
tadavarodhe ca sarve kAmA avaruddhAH syuH /
omityetadakSharamudgItha iti bhaktyAshaN^kA vinartyate /
tadvA etaditi mithunaM nirdishyate /
kiM tanmithunamityAha yadvAkca prANashca sarvaR^iksAmakAraNabhUtau mithunam /
R^ikva sAma ceti R^iksAmakAraNAvR^iksAmashabdoktAvityarthaH /
na tu svatantramR^ikca sAma ca mithunam /
anyathA hi vAkca prANashcetyekaM mithunamR^iksAma cAparaM mithunamiti dve mithune syAtAm /
tathA ca tadetanmithunamityekavacananirdeSho 'nupapannaH syAt /
tasmAdR^iksAmayonyorvAkprANayoreva mithunatvam //5 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.6

#<tad etan mithunam om ity etasminn akShare saMsR^ijyate |
yadA vai mithunau samAgacchata Apayato vai tAv anyo 'nyasya kAmam || ChUp_1,1.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.6 tadetadevaMlakShaNaM mithunamomityetasminnakShare saMsR^ijyate /
evaM sarvakAmAvAptiguNavishiShTaM mithunamoN^kAre saMsR^iShTaM vidyata ityoN^kArasya sarvakAmAvAptiguNavattvaM prasiddham /
vAÇmayatvamoN^kArasya prANaniShpAdyatvaM ca mithunena saMsR^iShTatvaM mithunasya kAmApayitR^itvaM prasiddhamiti dR^iShTAnta ucyate /
yathA loke mithunau mithunAvayavau strIpuMsau yadA samAgacchato grAmyadharmatayA saMyujyeyAnAM tadA'payataH prApayato 'nyonyasyetaretarasya tau kAmam /
tathA ca svAtmAnupraviShTena mithunena sarvakAmAptiguNavattvamoN^kArasya siddhamityabhiprAyaH //6 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.7

#<ApayitA ha vai kAmAnAM bhavati ya etad evaM vidvAn akSharam udgItham upAste || ChUp_1,1.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.7 tadupAsako 'pyudgAtA taddharmA bhavatItyAha-ApayitA ha vai kAmAnAM yajamAnasya bhavati ya etadakSharamevamAptiguNavadudgIthamupAste tasyaitadyathoktaM phalamityarthaH /
"taM yathA yathopAsate tadeva bhavati"iti shruteH //7 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.8

#<tad vA etad anuj~nAkSharam |
yad dhi kiMcAnujAnAty om ity eva tad Aha |
eSho eva samR^iddhir yad anuj~nA |
samardhayitA ha vai kAmAnAM bhavati ya etad evaM vidvAn akSharam udgItham upAste || ChUp_1,1.8 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.8 samR^iddhiguNavAMshcoN^kAraH /
katham-tadvA etatprakR^imanuj~nAkSharamanuj~nA ca sAkSharaM ca tat /
anuj~nAnumatiroN^kAra ityarthaH /
kathamanuj~netyAha shrutireva /
yaddhi kiJNca yatkiJNca loke j~nAnaM dhanaM vAnujAnAti vidvAndhanI vA tatrAnumatiM kurvannomityeva tadAha /
tathA ca vede"trayastriMshadityomiti hovAca"ityAdinA /
tathA ca loke 'pi tavedaM dhanaM gR^ihNAmItyukta omityAha /
ata eShA u evaiShaiva samR^iddhiryadanuj~nA yAnuj~nA sA samR^iddhistanmUlatvAdanuj~nAyAH /
samR^iddho hyomityanuj~nAM dadAti tasmAtsamR^iddhiguNavAnoN^kAra ityarthaH /
samR^iddhiguNopAsakatvAttaddharmA sansamardhayitA ha vai kAmAnAM yajamAnasya bhavati ya etadevaM vidvAnakSharamudgIthamupAsta ityAdi pUrvavat //8 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.9

#<teneyaM trayI vidyA vartate |
om ity AshrAvayati |
om iti shaMsati |
om ity udgAyati |
etasyaiva akSharasyApacityai mahimnA rasena || ChUp_1,1.9 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.9 athedAnImakSharaM stautyupAsyatvAtprarocanArtham /
kathaM, tenAkShareNa prakR^iteneyamR^igvedAdilakShaNA trayI vidyA trayIvidyAvihitaM karmetyarthaH /
na hi trayI vidyaivA'shrAvaNAdibhirvartate karma tu tathA pravartata iti prasiddham /
kathamomityAshrAvatyomiti shaMsatyomityudgAyatIti liN^gAcca somayAga iti gamyate /
tacca karmaitasyaivAkSharasyApacityai pUjArtham /
paramAtmapratIkaM hi tat /
tadapacitiH paramAtmana eva sA /
"svakarmaNA tamabhyarcya siddhiM vindati mAnavaH"iti smR^iteH /
mahimnA rasena /
kiJNcaitasyaivAkSharasya mahimnA mahattvena R^itvigyajamAnAdiprANairityarthaH /
tathaitasyaivAkSharasya rasena vrIhiyavAdirasanirvR^ittena haviShetyarthaH /
yAgahomAdyakShareNa kriyate /
taccA'dityamupatiShThate /
tato vR^iShTyAdikrameNa prANo 'nnaM ca jAyate /
prANairannena ca yaj~nastAyate /
ata ucyate 'kSharasya mahimnA rasnti //9 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,1.10

#<tenobhau kurutaH |
yash caitad evaM veda yash ca na veda |
nAnA tu vidyA cAvidyA ca |
yad eva vidyayA karoti shraddhayopaniShadA tad eva vIryavattaraM bhavatIti khalv etasyaivAkSharasyopavyAkhyAnaM bhavati || ChUp_1,1.10 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,1.10 tatrAkSharavij~nAnavataH karma kartavyamiti sthitamAbhipati-tenAbhareNobhau yashcaitadakSharamevaM vyAkhyAtaM veda yashca karmamAtravidakSharayAthAtmyaM na veda tAvubhau kurutaH karma /
tayoshca karmasAmarthyAdeva phalaM syAtkiM tatrAkSharayAthAtmyavij~nAneneti /
dR^iShTaM hi loke harItakIM bhakShayatostadrasAbhij~netarayorvirecanam /
naivam /
yasmAnnAnA tu vidyA cAvidyA ca bhinne hi vidyAvidye /
tushabdaH pakShavyAvR^ittyarthaH /
noN^kArasya karmAN^gatvamAtravij~nAnameva rasatamAptisamR^iddhiguNavadvij~nAnaM kiM tarhi tato 'bhyadhikam /
tasmAttadaN^gAdhikyAtphalAdhikyaM yuktamityabhiprAyaH /
dR^iShTaM hi loke vaNikshabarayoH padmarAgAdimaNivikraye vaNijo vij~nAnAdhikyAtphalAdhikyam /
tasmAdyadeva vidyayA vij~nAnena yuktaH sankaroti karmashraddhayA shraddadhAnashca sannupaniShadA yogena yuktashcetyarthaH /
tadeva karma vIryavattaramavidvatkarmaNo 'dhikaphalaM bhavatIti /
vidvatkarmaNo vIryavattara[tvaTavacanAdaviduSho 'pi karma vAryadeva bhavatItyabhiprAyaH /
na cAviduShaH karmaNyanadhikAraH /
auShastye kANDe 'viduShAmapyArvijyadarshanAt /
rasatamAptisamR^iddhiguNavadakSharamityekamupAsanam /
madhye prayatnAntarAdarshanAt /
anekairhi visheShaNairanekadhopAsyatvAtkhalvetasyaiva prakR^itasyodgIthAkhyasyAkSharasyopavyAkhyAnaM bhavati //10//

#<iti chAndogyopaniShacchAN^karabhAShye prathamAdhyAyasya prathama khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 1,2.1

#<devAsurA ha vai yatra saMyetire |
ubhaye prAjApatyAs tad dha devA udgItham Ajahrur anenainAn abhibhaviShyAma iti || ChUp_1,2.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.1 devAsurA devAshcAsurAshca /
devA dIvyaterdyetanArthasya shAstrodbhAsitA indriyavR^ittayaH /
ashirAstadvirItAH sveShvevAsuShu viShvagviShayAsu prANanakriyAsu ramaNAtsvAbhAvikyastama AtmikA indriyavR^ittaya eva /
ha vA iti pUrvavR^ittodbhAsakau nipAtau /
yatra yasminnimitta itaretaraviShayApahAralakShaNe saMyetire /
sampUrvasya yatateH saMgrAmArthatvamiti saMgrAmaM kR^itavanta utyarthaH /
shAsrIyaprakAshavR^ittayabhibhavanAya pravR^ittAH svAbhAvikyastamorUpA indriyavR^ittayo 'surAH /
tathA tadviparItAH shAsrArthaviShayavivekajyotirAtmAno devA svAbhAvikatamorUpAsurAbhibhavanAya pravR^ittA ityanyonyAbhibhavodbhavarUpaH saMgrAma iva sarvaprANiShu pratidehaM devAsurasaN^grAmo 'nAdikAlapravR^itta ityabhiprAyaH /
sa ihashrutyA'khyAyikArUpeNa dharmAdharmotpattivivekavij~nAnAya kathyate prANavishuddhivij~nAnavidhiparatayA /
ata ubhaye 'pi devAsurAH prajApaterapatyAnIti prAjApatyAH /
prajApatiH karmaj~nAnAdhikR^itaH puruShaH /
"puruSha evokthamayameva mahAnprajApatiH"iti shrutyantarAt /
tasya hi shAsrIyAH svAbhAvikyashca karaNavR^ittayo viruddhA apatyAnIva tadudbhavatvAt /
tattatrotkarShApakarShalakShaNanimitte ha devA udgIthabhaktyupalakShitamaudgAtraM karmA'jahrurAhR^itavantaH /
tasyApi kevalasyA'haraNAsambhavAjjotiShTomAdyAhR^itavanta ityabhiprAyaH /
tatkimarthamAjahrurityucyate anena karmaNainAnasurAnabhibhaviShyAma ityevamabhiprAyAH santaH //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,2.2

#<te ha nAsikyaM prANam udgItham upAsAM cakrire |
taM ha asurAH pApmanA vividhuH |
tasmAt tenobhayaM jighrati surabhi ca durgandhi ca |
pApmanA hy eSha viddhaH || ChUp_1,2.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.2 yadA ca  tadudgIthaM karmA'jihIrShavastadA-te ha devA nAsikyaM nAsikAyAM bhavaM cetanAvantaM ghrANaM prANamudgIthakartAramudgIthabhaktyopAsAMcakrirejhrupAsanaNTakR^itavanta ityarthaH /
nAsikyaprANamadR^iShTyodgIthAkhyamakSharamoN^kAramupAsAMcakrira ityarthaH /
evaM hi prakR^itArthaparityAgo 'prakR^itArthopAdAnaM ca na kR^itaM syAt /
khalvetasyaivAkSharasyetyoN^kAramupAsAMcakrira ityarthaH /
evaM hi prakR^itArthaparityAgo 'prakR^itArthopAdAnaM ca na kR^itaM syAt /
khalvetasyaivAkSharasyetyoN^kAro hyApAsyatayA prakR^itaH /
nanUdgIthopalakShitaM karmA'hR^itavanta ityavoca idAnImeva;kathaM nAsikyaprANadR^iShTyoN^kAramupAsAMcakrira ityAttha /
naiSha doShaH /
udgIthakarmaNyeva hi tatkartR^iprANadevatAdR^iShTyodgIthabhaktyavayavashcoN^kAra upAsyatvena vivakShito na svatantro 'tastAdarthyena karmA'hR^itavanta iti yuktamevoktam /
tamevaM devairvR^itamudgAtAraM hAsurAH svAbhAvikatama AtmAno jyotIrUpaM nAsikyaM prANaM devaM svotthena pApmanAdharmAsaN^garUpeNa vividhurviddhavantaH saMsarga kR^itavanta ityarthaH /
sa hi nAsikyaH prANaH kalyANagandhagrahaNAbhimAnAsaN^gAbhibhUtavivekavij~nAno babhUva /
sa tena doSheNa pApmasaMsargI babhUva /
tadidamuktamasurAH pApmanA vividhuriti /
yasmAdAsureNa pApmanA viddhastasmAttena pApmanA prerito ghrANaH prANo durgandhigrAhakaH prANinAm /
atastenobhayaM jighrati lokaH surabhi ca durgandhi ca /
pApmanA hyeSha yasmAdviddhaH /
ubhayagrahaNamavivakShitam /
yasyobhayaM havirArtimArchatIti yadvat /
yadevedamapratirUpaM jighratIti samAnaprakaraNashruteH //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,2.3-6

#<atha ha vAcam udgItham upAsAM cakrire |
tAM hAsurAH pApmanA vividhuH |
tasmAt tayobhayaM vadati satyaM cAnR^itaM ca |
pApmanA hy eShA viddhA || ChUp_1,2.3 ||>#

#<atha ha cakShur udgItham upAsAM cakrire |
tad dhAsurAH pApmanA vividhuH |
tasmAt tenobhayaM pashyati darshanIyaM cAdarshanIyaM ca |
pApmanA hy etad viddham || ChUp_1,2.4 ||>#

#<atha ha shrotram udgItham upAsAM cakrire |
tad dhAsurAH pApmanA vividhuH |
tasmAt tenobhayaM shR^iNoti shravaNIyaM cAshravaNIyaM ca |
pApmanA hy etad viddham || ChUp_1,2.5 ||>#

#<atha ha mana udgItham upAsAM cakrire |
tad dhAsurAH pApmanA vividhuH |
tasmAt tenobhayaM saMkalpayate saMkalpanIyaM ca |
pApmanA hy etad viddham || ChUp_1,2.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.3-6 mukhyaprANasyopAsyatvAya tadvishuddhatvAnubhavArtho 'yaM vicAraH shrutyA pravartitaH /
atashcakShurAdidevatAH krameNa vicAryA'sureNa pApmanA viddhA ityapohyante /
samAnamanyat, atha ha vAcaM cakShuH shrotraM mana ityAdi /
anuktA apyanyAstvagrasamAdidevatA draShTavyAH /
"evamu khalvetA devatAH pApmabhiH" iti shrutyantarAt //3-6 //

START ChUp 1,2.7

#<atha ha ya evAyaM mukhyaH prANas tam udgItham upAsAM cakrire |
taM hAsurA R^itvA vidadhvaMsur yathAshmAnam AkhaNam R^itvA vidhvaMsetaivam || ChUp_1,2.7 ||>#


__________


ChUpBh_1,2.7 AsureNa viddhatvAdghrANAdidevatA apohyAthAnantaraM ya evAyaM prasiddho mukhe bhavo mukhyaH prANastamudgIthamupAsAJNcakrire taM hAsurAH pUrvavadR^itvA prApya vidadhvaMsurvinaShTA abhiprAyamAtreNa /
akR^itvA kiJNcidapi prANasya /
kathaM vinaShTA ityatra dR^iShTAntamAha-yathA loke 'shmAnamAkhaNaM na shakyate khanituM kuddAlAdibhirapi bhettuM na shakyo 'khaNa evA'khaNastamR^itvA sAmarthyAlloShTaH pAMsupiNDaH kShutyantarAccAshmani kShipto 'shmabhedanAbhiprAyeNa tasyAshmanaH kiJNcidapyakR^itvA svayaM vidhvaMseta vidIryetaivaM vidadhvaMsurityarthaH //7 //

START ChUp 1,2.8

#<evaM yathAshmAnam AkhaNam R^itvA vidhvaMsata evaM haiva sa vidhvaMsate ya evaMvidi pApaM kAmayate yash cainam abhidAsati |
sa eSho 'shmAkhaNaH || ChUp_1,2.8 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.8 evaM vishuddho 'surairadharShitatvAtprANa iti evaMvidaH prANAtmabhUtasyedaM phalamAha-yathAshmAnamiti /
eSha eva dR^iShTAntaH /
evaM haiva sa vidhvaMsate vinashyati /
ko 'sAvityAha-ya evaMvidi yathoktaprANavidi pApaM tadanarhaM kartu kAmayata icchati yashcApyenamabhidAsati hinasti prANavidaM pratyAkroshatADanAdi prayuN^kte so 'pyevameva vidhvaMsata ityarthaH /
yasmAtsa eSha prANavitprANabhUtatvAdashmAkhaNa ivAshmAkhaNo 'dharShaNIya ityarthaH /
nanu nAsikyo 'pi prANo vAyvAtmA yathA mukhyastatra nAsikyaH prANaH pApmanA viddhaH prANa eva sanna mukhyaH katham /
naiSha doShaH /
nAsikyastu sthAnakaraNavaiguNyAdviddho vAyvAtmApi sanmukhyaH sthAnadevatAbalIyastvAnna viddha iti yuktam /
yathA vAsyAdayaH shikShAvatpuruShAshrayAH kAryavisheShaM kurvanti nAnyahastagatAstadvaddoShavadghrANasacivatvAdviddhA ghrANadevatA na mukhyaH //8 //

START ChUp 1,2.9

#<naivaitena surabhi na durgandhi vijAnAti |
apahatapApmA hy eShaH |
tena yad ashnAti yat pibati tenetarAn prANAn avati |
etam u evAntato 'vittvotkrAmati |
vyAdadAty evAntata iti || ChUp_1,2.9 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.9 yasmAnna viddho 'surairmukhyastasmAnnaivaitena surabhi durgandhi vA vijAnAti ghrANenaiva tadubhayaM vijAnAti lokaH /
atashca pApmakAryAdarshanAdapahatapApmApahato vinAshito 'panItaH pApmA yasmAtso 'yamapahatapApmA hyeSha vishuddha ityarthaH /
yasmAccA'tmambharayaH kalyANAdyAsaN^gavattvAdghrANAdayo na tathA'tmambharirmukhyaH kiM tarhi sarvArthaH /
kathamiti, ucyate-tena mukhyena yadashnAti yatpibati lokastenAshitena pItena cotarAnghrANAdInavati pAlayati /
tena hi teShAM sthitirbhavatItyarthaH /
ataH sarvambharaH prANo 'to vishuddhaH /
kathaM punarmukhyAshitapItAbhyAM sthitireShAM gamyata iti, ucyate-etaM (tamu eva) mukhyaM prANaM mukhyaprANasya vR^ittimannapAne ityarthaH /
antato 'nte maraNakAle 'vittvAlabdhvot-krAmati /
ghrANAdiprANasamudAya ityarthaH /
aprANo hi na shaknotyashituM pAtuM vA /
tena tadotkrAntiH prasiddhA ghrANAdikalApasya /
dR^ishyate hyutkrAntau prANasyAshishiShA /
ato vyAdadAtyevA'syavidAraNaM karotItyarthaH /
taddhyannAlAbha utkrAntasya liN^gam //9 //

START ChUp 1,2.10

#<taM hAN^girA udgItham upAsAM cakre |

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.10 taM hAN^girAstaM mukhyaM prANaM hAN^girA ityevaN^guNamudgIthamuyAsAJNcakre baka ityeva sambandhaM kR^itavantaH kecit /
etamu evA'N^girasaM bR^ihaspatimayAsyaM prANaM manyanta iti canAt /
bhavatyevaM yathAshrutAsambhave, sambhavati tu yathAshrutamR^iShicodanAyAmapi shrutyantaravat /
tasmAcchatarcina ityAcakShata etameva santamR^iShimapi /

AsyAd yad ayate || ChUp_1,2.12 ||>#

ChUpBh_1,2.11,12 tathA vAco bR^ihatyAH patistenAsau bR^ihaspatiH /

START ChUp 1,2.13

#<tena taM ha bako dAlbhyo vidAM cakAra |

__________


ChUpBh_1,2.13 na kevalamaN^giraHprabhR^itayaH upAsAJNcakrire /

ChUpBh_1,2.14 tathAnyo 'pyudgAtA'gAtA ha vai kAmAnAM bhavati evaM vidvAnyathoktaguNaM prANamakSharamudgIthamupAste tasyaitaddR^iShTaM phalamuktam /

START ChUp 1,3.1

#<athAdhidaivatam |
ya evAsau tapati tam udgItham upAsIta |
udyan vA eSha prajAbhya udgAyati |
udyaMs tamo bhayam apahanti |
apahantA ha vai bhayasya tamaso bhavati ya evaM veda || ChUp_1,3.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,3.1 athAnantaramadhidaivataM devatAviShayamudgIthopAsanaM prastutamutyartho 'nekadhopAsyatvAdudgIthasya /
ya evAsAvAdityastapati samudgIthamupAsItA'dityadR^iShTyodgIthamupAsItetyarthaH /
tamudgIthamityudgIthashabdo 'kSharavAcI sankathamAditye vartata iti?ucyate /
udyannudgacchanvA eSha prajAbhyaH prajArthamudgAyati prajAnAmannotpattyartham /
na hyanudyati tasminvrIhyAdeH paktiH syAdata udgAyatIvodgAyati, yathaivodgAtAnnArthamata udgIthaH savitetyarthaH /
kiJNcodyannaishaM tamastajjaM ca bhayaM praNinAmapahanti tamevaN^guNaM savitAraM yo veda so 'pahantA nAshayitA ha vai bhayasya janmamaraNAdilakShaNasyA'tmanastamasashca tatkAraNasyAj~nAnalakShaNasya bhavati //1 //

START ChUp 1,3.2

#<samAna u evAyaM cAsau ca |

tasmAd vA etam imam amuM ca udgItham upAsIta || ChUp_1,3.2 ||>#

ChUpBh_1,3.2 yadyapi sthAnabhedAtprANAdityau bhinnAviva lakShyete tathApi na sa tattvabhedastayoH /

ataH satattvAbhedAdetaM prANamimamamuM cA'dityamudgIthamupAsIta //2 //

START ChUp 1,3.3

#<atha khalu vyAnam evodgItham upAsIta |
yad vai prANiti sa prANaH |
yad apAniti so 'pAnaH |
atha yaH prANApAnayoH saMdhiH sa vyAnaH |
yo vyAnaH sA vAk |

__________


ChUpBh_1,3.3 atha khalviti prakArAntareNopAsanamudgIthasyocyate-vyAnameva vakShyamANalakShaNaM prANasyaiva vR^ittivisheShamudgIthamupAsIta /

tataH kimiti, ucyate-atha ya uktalakShaNayoH prANApAnayoH sandhistayorantarA vR^ittivisheShaH sa vyAnaH, yaH sAN^khyAdishAsraprasiddhiH shrutyA visheShanirUpaNAnnAsau vyAna ityabhiprAyaH /
kasmAtpunaH prANApAnau hitvA mahatA'yAsena vyAnasyaivopAsanamucyate /
vIryavatkarmahetutvamityAha-yo vyAnaH sA vAk /
vyAnakAryatvAdvAcaH /
yasmAdvyAnanirvartyA vAktasmAdaprANannanapAnanprANApAnavyApArAvakurvanvAcamabhivyAharatyuccArayati lokaH //3 //

ChUpBh_1,3.5 na kevalaM vAgAdyabhivyAharaNamevAto 'smAdanyAnyapi yAni vIryavanti karmANi prayatnAdhikyanirvartyAni yathAgnermanthanamAjermaryAdAyAH saraNaM dhAvanaM dR^iDhasya dhanuSha AyamanamAkarShaNamaprANannanapAnaMstAni karoti /

#<atha khalUdgIthAkSharANy upAsIta ud-gI-tha iti |

anne hIdaM sarvaM sthitam || ChUp_1,3.6 ||>#

ChUpBh_1,3.12 AtmAnamudgAtA svaM rUpaM gotranAmAdibhiH sAmAdInkrameNa svaM cA'tmAnamantato 'nta upasR^itya stuvIta /

START ChUp 1,4.1

#<om ity etad akSharam udgItham upAsIta |
om iti hy udgAyati |
tasyopavyAkhyAnam || ChUp_1,4.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,4.1 omityetadityAdiprakR^itasyAkSharasya punarupAdAnamudgIthAkSharAdyupAsanAntaritatvAdanyatra prasaN^go mA bhUdityevamartham /
prakR^itasyaivAkSharasyAmR^itAbhayaguNavishiShTasyopAsanaM vidhAtavyamityArambhaH /
omityAdi vyAkhyAtam //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,4.2

#<devA vai mR^ityor bibhyatas trayIM vidyAM prAvishan |
te chandobhir acchAdayan |
yad ebhir acchAdayaMs tac chandasAM chandastvam || ChUp_1,4.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,4.2 devA vai mR^ityormArakAdvibhyataH kiM kR^itavanta ityucyate /
trayIM vidyAM trayIvihitaM karma prAvishanpraviShTavanto vaidikaM karma prArabdhavanta ityarthaH /
tanmR^ityosrANaM manyamAnAH /
kiJNca te karmaNyaviniyuktaishchandobhirmantrairjapahomAdi kurvanta AtmAnaM karmAntareShvacchAdayaMshchAditavantaH /
yadyasmAdebhirmantrairacchAdayaMstattasmAcchandasAM mantrANAM chAdanAcchandastvaM prasiddhameva //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,4.3

#<tAn u tatra mR^ityur yathA matsyam udake paripashyed evaM paryapashyad R^ici sAmni yajuShi |
te nu vittvordhvA R^icaH sAmno yajuShaH svaram eva prAvishan || ChUp_1,4.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,4.3 tAMstatra devAnkarmaparAnmR^ityuryathA loke matsyaghAtako matsyamudake nAtigambhIre paripashyedbaDishodakasrAvopAyasAdhyaM manyamAna evaM paryapashyaddR^iShTavAnmR^ityuH karmakShayopAyena sAdhyAndevAnmena ityarthaH /
kvAsau devAndadarshetyucyate-R^ici sAmni yajuShi /
R^igyajuHsAmasambandhikarmaNItyarthaH /
te nu devA vaidikena karmaNA saMskR^itAH shuddhAtmAnaH santo mR^ityoshcikIrShitaM viditavantaH /
viditvA ca ta UrdhvA vyAvR^ittAH karmabhya R^icaH sAmno yajuSha R^igyajuHsAmasambaddhAtkarmaNo 'bhyutthAyetyarthaH /
tena karmaNA mR^ityubhayApagamaM prati nirAshAstadapAsyAmR^itAbhayaguNamakSharaM svaraM svarashabditaM prAvishanneva praviShTavantaH /
oN^kAropAsanaparAH saMvR^ittAH /
evashabdo 'vadhAraNArthaH sansamuccayapratiShedhArthaH /
tadupAsanaparAH saMvR^ittA ityarthaH //3 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,4.4

#<yadA vA R^icam Apnoty om ity evAtisvarati evaM sAmaivaM yajuH |
eSha u svaro yad etad akSharam etad amR^itam abhayam |
tat pravishya devA amR^itA abhavan || ChUp_1,4.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,4.4 kathaM punaH svarashabdavAcyatvamakSharasyetyucyate-yadA vA R^icamApnotyomityevAtisvaratyevaM sAmaivaM yajuH /
eSha u svaraH /
ko 'sau yadetadakSharametadamR^itamabhayaM tatpravishya yathAguNamevAmR^itA abhayAshcAbhavandevAH //4 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,4.5

#<sa ya etad evaM vidvAn akSharaM praNauty etad evAkSharaM svaram amR^itam abhayaM pravishati |
tat pravishya yad amR^itA devAs tad amR^ito bhavati || ChUp_1,4.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,4.5 sa yo 'nyo 'pi devavadevaitadakSharamevamamR^itamabhayaguNaM vidvAnpraNauti stauti /
upAsanamevAtra stutirabhipretA /
sa tathaivaitadevAkSharaM svaramamR^itamabhayaM pravishati /
tatpravishya ca rAjakulaM praviShTAnAmiva rAj~no 'ntaraN^gabahiraN^gatAvanna vishiShTastadamR^ito bhavati na nyUnatA nApyadhikatAmR^itatva ityarthaH //5//

#<iti chAndogyopaniShacchAN^karabhAShye prathamAdhyAyasya caturthaH khaNDaH>#

=======================================================================

START ChUp 1,5.1

#<atha khalu ya udgIthaH sa praNavo yaH praNavaH sa udgItha iti |
asau vA Aditya udgItha eSha praNavaH |
om iti hy eSha svarann eti || ChUp_1,5.1 ||>#


__________


ChUpBh_1,5.1 prANAdityadR^iShTivishiShTasyodgIthasyopAsanamuktamevAnUdya praNavodgIthayorekatvaM kR^itvA tasminprANarashmibhedaguNavishiShTadR^iShTyAkSharasyopAsanamanekaputraphalamidAnIM vaktavyamityArabhyate-atha khalu ya udgIthaH sa praNavo bahvR^icAnAM yashca praNavasteShAM sa eva cchAndogya udgIthashabdavAcyaH /
asau vA Aditya udgItha eSha praNavashabdavAcyo 'pi sa eva bahvR^icAnAM nAnyaH /
udgItha AdityaH katham /
udgIthAkhyamakSharamomityetadeSha hi yasmAtsvarannuccArayannanekArthatvAddhAtUnAm /
athavA svarangacchannaiti /
ato 'sAvudgIthaH savitA //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,5.2

#<etam u evAham abhyagAsiShaM tasmAn mama tvam eko 'sIti ha kauShItakiH putram uvAca |
rashmIMs tvaM paryAvartayAt |
bahavo vai te bhaviShyanti |
ity adhidaivatam || ChUp_1,5.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,5.2 tametamu evAhamabhyagAsiShamAbhimukhyena gItavAnasmyAdityarashmyabhedaM kR^itvA dhyAnaM kR^itavAnasmItyarthaH /
tena tasmAtkAraNAnmama tvameko 'si putra iti ha kauShItakiH kuShItakasyApatyaM kauShItakiH putramuvAcoktavAn /
ato rashmInAdityaM ca bhedena tvaM paryAvartayAtparyAvartayetyarthaH /
tvaMyogAt /
evaM bahavo vai te tava putrA bhaviShyantItyadhi daivatam //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,5.3

#<athAdhyAtmam |
ya evAyaM mukhyaH prANas tam udgItham upAsita |
om iti hy eSha svarann eti || ChUp_1,5.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,5.3 athAnantaramadhyAtmamucyate /
ya evAyaM mukhyaH prANastamudgIthamupAsItetyAdi pUrvavat /
tathomiti hyeSha prANo 'pi svarannetyomiti hyanuj~nAM kurvanniva vAgAdipravR^ittyarthametotyarthaH /
na hi maraNakAle mumUrShoH samIpasthAH prANasyoN^kAraNaM shR^iNvantIti /
etatsAmAnyAdAditye 'pyoN^karaNamanuj~nAmAtraM draShTavyam //3 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,5.4

#<etam u evAham abhyagAsiShaM tasmAn mama tvam eko 'sIti ha kauShItakiH putram uvAca |
prANAMs tvaM bhUmAnam abhigAyatAd bahavo vai me bhaviShyantIti || ChUp_1,5.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,5.4 etamu evAhamabhyagAsiShityAdi pUrvavadeva /
ato vAgAdInmukhyaM ca prANaM bhedaguNavishiShTagudgIthaM pashyanbhUmAnaM manasAbhigAyatAt /
pUrvavadAvartayetyarthaH /
bahavo vai me mama putrA bhaviShyantItyevamabhiprAyaH sannityarthaH /
prANAdityaikatvodgIthadR^iShTerekaputratvaphaladoSheNApoditatvAdrashmiprANabhedadR^iShTeH kartavyatA codyate 'sminkANDe bahuputraphalatvArtham //4 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,5.5

#<atha khalu ya udgIthaH sa praNavo yaH praNavaH sa udgItha iti |
hotR^iShadanAd dha evApi durudgItham anusamAharatIty anusamAharatIti || ChUp_1,5.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,5.5 atha khalu ya udgItha ityAdipraNavodgIthaikatvadarshanamapaktaM tasyaitatphalamAhartuM shakyam /
kiM taddhaivApi durudgItaM duShTamudgItamudgAnaM kR^itamudgAtrA svakarmaNi kShataM kR^itamityarthaH /
tadanusamAharatyanusandhatta ityarthaH /
cikitsayeva dhAtuvaiShamyasamIkaraNamiti //5//

#<iti chAndogyopaniShacchAN^karabhAShye prathamAdhyAyasya paJNcamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 1,6.1

#<iyam evark |
agniH sAma |
tad etad etasyAm R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma |
tasmAd R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma gIyate |
iyam eva sA |
agnir amaH |
tat sAma || ChUp_1,6.1 ||>#


__________


ChUpBh_1,6.1 athedAnIM sarvaphalasampattyarthamudgIthasyopAsanAntaraM vidhitsyate-iyameva pR^ithivyR^ik /
R^ici pR^ithivIdR^iShTiH kAryA /
tathAgniH sAma /
sAmnyagnidR^iShTiH /
kathaM pR^ithivyagnyor R^iksAmatvamiti /
ucyate /
tadetattadetadagnyAkhyaM sAmaitasyAM pR^ithivyAmR^icyadhyUDhamadhigatamuparibhAvena sthitamityarthaH /
R^icIva sAma /
tasmAdata eva kAraNAdR^icyadhyUDhameva sAma gIyata idAnImapi sAmagaiH /
yathA ca R^iksAmanI nAtyantaM bhinne anyonyaM tathaitau pR^ithivyagnidvayaM sAmaikashabdAbhidheyatvamApannaM sAma /
tasmAnnAnyonyaM bhinnaM pR^ithivyagnidvayaM nityasaMshliShTamR^iksAmanI iva /
tasmAcca pR^ithivyagnyor R^iksAmatvamityarthaH /
sAmAkSharayoH pR^ithivyagnidR^iShTividhAnArthamiyameva sAgnirama iti kecit //1 //

START ChUp 1,6.2-3

#<antarikSham evark |
vAyuH sAma |
tad etad etasyAm R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma |

antarikSham eva sA |
vAyur amaH |
tat sAma || ChUp_1,6.2 ||>#

#<dyaur evark |

dyaur eva sA |
Adityo 'maH |

ChUpBh_1,6.2,3 antarikShamevargvAyuH sAmetyAdi pUrvavat //2-3 //

START ChUp 1,6.4

#<nakShatrAny evark |
candramAH sAma |

nakShatrANy eva sA |
candramA amaH |
tat sAma || ChUp_1,6.4 ||>#

ChUpBh_1,6.4 nakShatrANAmadhipatishcandramA ataH sa sAma //4 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,6.5

#<atha yad etad Adityasya shuklaM bhAH saivark |
atha yan nIlaM paraHkR^iShNaM tat sAma |
tad etad etasyAm R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma |
tasmad R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma gIyate || ChUp_1,6.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,6.5 atha yadetadAdityasya shuklaM bhAH shuklA dIptiH saivarka /
atha yadAditye nIlaM paraH kR^iShNaM paro 'tishayena kArShNyaM tatsAma /
taddhyekAntasamAhitadR^iShTerdR^ishyate //5 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,6.6

#<atha yad evaitad Adityasya shuklaM bhAH saiva sA |
atha yan nIlaM paraHkR^iShNaM tad amaH |
tat sAma |
atha ya eSho 'ntarAditye hiraNmayaH puruSho dR^ishyate hiraNyashmashrur hiraNyakesha A praNakhAt sarva eva suvarnaH || ChUp_1,6.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,6.6 te evaite bhAH shuklakR^iShNatve sA cAmashca sAma /
atha ya eSho 'ntarAditye AdityasyAntarmadhye hiraNmayo hiraNmaya iva hiraNmayaH /
na hi suvarNavikAratvaM devasya sambhavati /
R^iksAmageShNatvApahatapApmatvAsambhavAt /
na hi sauvarNe 'cetane pApmAdiprAptirasti yena pratiShidhyeta /
cAkShuShe cAgrahaNAt /
ato luptopama eva hiraNmayashabdo jyotirmaya ityarthaH /
uttareShavapi samAnA yojanA /
puruShaH puri shayanAtpUrayati vA svenA'tmanA jagaditi /
dR^ishyate nivR^ittacakShurbhiH samAhitacetobhirbrahmacaryAdisAdhanApekSham /
tejasvino 'pi shmashrukeshAdayaH kR^iShNAH syurityato vishinaShTi-hiraNyashmashrurhiraNyakesha iti /
jyotirmayAnyevAsya shmashrUNi keshAshcetyarthaH /
ApraNakhAtpraNakho nakhAgraM nakhAgreNa saha sarvaH suvarNa iva bhArUpa ityarthaH //6 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,6.7

#<tasya yathA kapyAsaM puNDarIkam evam akShiNI |
tasyod iti nAma |
sa eSha sarvebhyaH pApmabhya uditaH |
udeti ha vai sarvebhyaH pApmabhyo ya evaM veda || ChUp_1,6.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,6.7 tasyaivaM sarvataH suvarNavarNasyApyakShNorvasheShaH /
kathaM?tasya yathA kapermarkaTasyA'saH kapyAsaH /
AserupaveshanArthasya karaNe gha¤ /
kapipR^iShThAnto yenopavishati /
kapyAsa iva puNDarIkamatyantatejasvyevamasya devasyAkShiNI /
upamitopamAnatvAnna hInopamA /
tasyaivaN^guNavishiShTasya gauNamidaM nAmoditi /
kathaM gauNatvam /
sa eSha devaH sarvebhyaH pApmabhyaH pApmanA saha tatkAryebhya ityarthaH /
ya AtmApahatapApmetyAdi vakShyati /
udita ud ita udgata ityarthaH /
ato 'sAvunnAmA /
tamevaN^guNasampannamunnAmAnaM yathoktena prakAreNa yo veda so 'pyevamevodetyudgacchati sarvebhyaH pApmabhyaH /
ha vA ityavadhAraNArthau nipAtau /
udetyevetyarthaH //7 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,6.8

#<tasyark ca sAma ca geShNau |
tasmAd udgIthaH |
tasmAt tv eva udgAtA |
etasya hi gAtA |
sa eSha ye cAmuShmAt parAJNco lokAs teShAM ceShTa devakAmAnAM ca |
ity adhidaivatam || ChUp_1,6.8 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,6.8 tasyodgIthatvaM devasyA'dityAdInAmiva vivakShitatvAdAha-tasyarkca sAma ca geShNau pR^ithivyAdyuktalakShaNe parvaNI /
sarvAtmA hi devaH /
parAparalokakAmeshitR^itvAdupapadyate pR^ithivyagnyR^iksAmageShNatvam /
sarvayonitvAcca /
yata evamunnAmAcAsAvR^iksAmageShNashca tasmAdR^iksAmageShNatvaprAptamudgIthatvamucyate parokSheNa parokShapriyatvAddevasya tasmAdudgItha iti /
tasmAttaveva hetorudaM gAyatItyudgAtA /
yasmAddhyetasya yathoktasyonnAmno gAtAsAvato yuktodgAteti nAmaprasiddhirudgAtuH /
sa eSha deva unnAmA ye cAmuShmAdAdityAtparAJNcaH parAgaJNcanAdUrdhvA lokAsteShAM lokAnAM ceShTe na kevalamIshitR^itvameva cashabdAddhArayati ca /
"sa dAdhAra pR^ithivIM dyAmutemAm"ityAdimantravarNAt /
kiJNca devakAmAnAmIShTa ityetadadhidaivataM devatAviShayaM devasyodgIthasya svarUpamuktam //8//

#<iti chAndogyopaniShacchAN^karabhAShye prathamodhyAyasya ShaShThaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 1,7.1

#<athAdhyAtmam |
vAg evark |
prANaH sAma |
tad etad etasyAm R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma |
tasmAd R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma gIyate |
vAg eva sA |
prANo 'maH |
tat sAma || ChUp_1,7.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.1 athAdhunAdhyAtmamucyate /
vAgevarkprANaH sAma /
adharoparisthAnatvasAmAnyAt /
prANo ghrANamucyate saha vAyunA, vAgeva sA prANo 'ma ityAdi pUrvavat //1 //

START ChUp 1,7.2

#<cakShur evark |
AtmA sAma |

AtmAmaH |

ChUpBh_1,7.2 cakShurevargAtmA sAma /
Atmeti cchAyAtmA tatsthatvAtsAma //2 //

START ChUp 1,7.3

#<shrotram evark |
manaH sAma |

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.3 shrotramevarÇmanaH sAma, shrotrasyAdhiShThAtR^itvAnmanasaH sAmatvam //3 //

START ChUp 1,7.4

#<atha yad etad akShnaH shuklaM bhAH saivark |
atha yan nIlaM paraHkR^iShNaM tat sAma |
tad etad etasyAm R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma |
tasmAd R^icy adhyUDhaM sAma gIyate |

atha yan nIlaM paraHkR^iShNaM tad amaH |
tat sAma || ChUp_1,7.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.4 atha yadetadakShNaH shuklaM bhAH saivarka /
atha yannIlaM paraH kR^iShNamAditya iva dR^ikshaktyadhiShThAnaM tatsAma //4 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,7.5

#<atha ya eSho 'ntar akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate saivark |
tat sAma |
tad uktham |
tad yajuH |
tad brahma |
tasya etasya tad eva rUpaM yad amuShya rUpam |
yAv amuShya geShNau tau tau goShNau |
yan nAma tan nAma || ChUp_1,7.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.5 atha ya eSho 'ntarakShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate /
pUrvavat /
saivargadhyAtmaM vAgAdyA pR^ithivyAdyA cAdhidaivatam /
prasiddhA ca R^ikpAdabaddhAkSharAtmikA /
tathA sAma /
ukthasAhacaryAdvA stotraM sAmokthaM shastram /
ukthAdanyat tathA yajuH svAhAsvadhAvaShaDAdi sarvameva vAgyajustatsa eva /
sarvAtmakatvAtsarvayonitvAcceti hyavocAma /
R^igAdiprakaraNAttadbrahmeti trayo vedAH /
tasyaitasya cAkShuShasya puruShasya tadeva rUpamatidishyate /
kiM tadyadamuShyA'dityapuruShasya /
hiraNmaya ityAdi yadadhidaivatamuktam /
yAvamuShya geShNau parvaNI tAvevAsyApi cAkShuShasya geShNau /
yaccAmuShya nAmodityudgItha iti ca tadevAsya nAma /
sthAnabhedAdrUpagiNanAmAtideshAdIshitR^itvaviShayabhedavyapadeshAccA'dityacAkShuShayorbheda iti cet /
na /
amunAnenaivetyekasyobhayAtmaprAptyanupapatteH /
dvidhAbhAvenopapadyata iti cet /
vakShyati hi sa ekadhA bhavati tridhA bhavatItyAdi /
na /
cetanasyaikasya niravayavatvAddvidhAbhAvAnupapatteH /
tasmAdadhyAtmAdhidaivatayorekatvameva /
yattu rUpAdyatidesho bhedakAraNamavoco na tadbhedAvagamAya /
kiM tarhi sthAnabhedAdbhedAshaN^kA mA bhUdityevamartham //5 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,7.6

#<sa eSha ye caitasmAd arvAJNco lokAs teShAM ceShTe manuShyakAmAnAM ceti |
tad ya ime vINAyAM gAyanty etaM te gAyanti |
tasmAt te dhanasanayaH || ChUp_1,7.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.6 sa eSha cAkShuShaH puruSho ye caitasmAdAdhyAtmikAdAtmanor'vAJNcor'vAggatA lokAsteShAM ceShTe manuShyasambandhinAM ca kAmAnAm /
tatsmAdya ime vINAyAM gAyanti gAyakasta etameva gAyanti /
yasmAdIshvaraM gAyanti tasmAtte dhanasanayo dhanalAbhayuktA dhanavanta utyarthaH //6 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,7.7

#<atha ya etad evaM vidvAn sAma gAyaty ubhau sa gAyati |
so 'munaiva sa eSha ye cAmuShmAt parAJNco lokAs tAMsh cApnoti devakAmAMsh ca || ChUp_1,7.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.7 atha ya etadevaM vidvAnyathoktaM devamudgIthaM vidvAnsAma gAyatyubhau sa gAyati cAkShuShamAdityaM ca /
tasyaivaMvidaH phalamucyateso 'munaivA'dityena sa eSha ye cAmuShmAtparAJNco lokAstAMshcA'pnoti AdityAntargatadevo bhUtvetyartho devakAmAMshca //7 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 1,7.8-9

#<athAnenaiva ye caitasmAd arvAJNco lokAs tAMsh cApnoti manuShyakAmAMsh ca |
tasmAd u haivaMvid udgAtA brUyAt || ChUp_1,7.8 ||>#

#<kaM te kAmam AgAyAnIti |
eSha hy eva kAmAgAnasyeShTe ya evaM vidvAn sAma gAyati sAma gAyati || ChUp_1,7.9 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_1,7.8 athAnenaiva cAkShuSheNaiva ye caitasmAdarvAJNco lokAstAMshcA'pnoti manuShyakAmAMshca cAkShuSho bhUtvetyarthaH /
tasmAdu haivaMvidudgAtA brUyAdyajamAnaM kamiShTaM te tava kAmamAgAyAnIti /
eSha hi yasmAdudgAtA kAmAgAnasyodgAnena kAmaM sampAdayitumIShTe samartha ityarthaH /
ko 'sau?ya evaM vidvAnsAma gAyati sAma gAyati /

atha tarhy eta eva samatisR^iShTAH stuvatAm |

ChUpBh_1,11.3 adyApi bhagavAMstveva me mama sarvairArtvijyairR^itvikkarmArthamastvityuktastathetyAhoShast iH /

START ChUp 2,12.1

ChUpBh_2,12.1 abhimanthati sa hiN^kAraH prAthamyAt /
agnerdhUmo jAyate sa prastAva AnantaryAt /

ChUpBh_2,23.1 oN^kArasyopAsanavidhyarthaM trayo dharmaskandhA ityAdyArabhyate /

ke ta ityAha -yaj~no 'gnihotrAdiH /

gR^ihasthasamavetatvAttannirvartakena gR^ihasthena nirdishyate prathama eka ityartho dvitIyatR^itIyashravaNAnnA'dyArthaH /
tapa eva dvitIyastapa iti kR^icchracAndrAyaNAdi tadvAMstApasaH parivrADvA na brahmasaMstha AshramadharmamAtrasaMstho;brahmasaMsthasya tvamR^itatvashravaNAt /
dvitIyo dharmaskandhaH /
brahmacAryAcAryakule vastuM shIlamasyetyAcAryakulavAsI /
atyantaM yAvajjIvamAtmAnaM niyamairAcAryakule 'vasAdayankShapayandehaM tR^itIyo dharmaskandhaH /
atyantamityAdivisheShaNAnnaiShThika iti gamyate /
upakurvANasya svAdhyAyagrahaNArthatvAnna puNyalokatvaM brahmacaryeNa /
sarva ete trayo 'pyAshramiNo yathoktairdharmaiH puNyalokA bhavanti /
puNyo loko yeShAM ta ime puNyalokA AshramiNo bhavanti /
avashiShTastvanuktaH parivrADbrahmasaMstho brahmaNi samyaksthitaH so 'mR^itatvaM puNyalokavilakShaNamamaraNabhAvamAtyantikameti nA'pekShikaM devAdyamR^itatvavat /
puNyalokAtpR^iyagamR^itatvasya vibhAgakaraNAt /
yadi ca pumyalokAtishayamAtramamR^itatvamabhaviShyattataH puNyalokatvAdvibhaktaM nAvakShyat /
vibhaktepadeshAccA'tyantikamamR^itatvamiti gamyate /
atra cA'shramadharmaphalopanyAsaH praNavasevAstutyarthaM na tatphalavidhyartham /
stutaye ca pravamasevAyA Ashramadharmaphalavidhaye ceti hi bhidyeta vAkyam /
tasmAtsmR^itisiddhAshramaphalAnuvAdena praNavasevAphalamamR^itatvaM bruvanpraNavasevAM stauti /
yathA pUrNavarmaNaH sevA bhaktaparidhAnamAtraphalA rAjavarmaNastu sevA rAjyatulyaphaleti tadvat /
praNavashca tatsatyaM paraM brahma tatpratIkatvAt /
"etaddhyevAkSharaM brahma etaddhyevAkSharaM param" ityAdyAmnAyAtkAThake yuktaM tatsevAto 'mR^itatvam /
caturNAmadhikR^itatvAvisheShAt /
brahmasaMsthatve 'pratiShedhAcca /
svakarmacchidre ca brahmasaMsthatAyAM sAmardhyopapatteH /
na ca yavavarAhAdishabdavadbrahmasaMsthashabdaH parivrAjake rUDhaH /
brahmaNi saMsthitinimittamupAdAya pravR^ittatvAt /
na hi rUDhishabdA nimittamupAdadate /
sarveShAM ca brahmaNi sthitirupapadyate /
yatra yatra nimittamasti brahmaNi saMsthitistasya tasya nimittavato vAcakaM santaM brahmasaMsthashabdaM parivrADekaviShaye saMkoca kAraNAbhAvAnniroddhuma yuktam /
na ca pArivrAjyAshramadharmamAtreNAmR^itatvam /
j~nAnAnarthakyaprasaN^gAt /
pArivrAjyadharmayuktameva j~nAnamamR^itatvasAdhanamiti cenna /
AshramadharmatvAvisheShAt /
dharmo vA j~nAnavishiShTo 'mR^itatvasAdhanamityedapi sarvAshramadharmANAmavishiShTam /
na ca vacanamasti parivrAjakasyaiva brahmasaMsthasya mokSho nAnyeShAmiti /
j~nAnAnmokSha iti ca sarvopaniShadAM siddhAntaH tasmAdya eva brahmasaMsthaH svAshramavihitakarmavatAM so 'mR^itatvametIti /
kurvidaM mA kArShIriti karmavidhayaH pravR^ittAH /
tacca nimittaM na shAsrakR^itam /
sarvaprANiShu darshanAt /
"sadekamevAdvitIyaM" "AtmaivedaM sarvaM" "brahmaivedaM sarvam" itishAsrajanyaH pratyayo vidyArUpaH svAbhAvikaM kriyAkArakaphalabhedapratyayaM karmavidhinimittamanupamR^idya na jAyate /
bhedAbhedapratyayayorvirodhAt /
na hi taimirikadvicandrAdibhedapratyayamanupamR^idya timirApagame candrAdyekatvapratyaya upajAyate /
vidyAvidyApratyayayorvirodhAt /
tatraivaM sati yaM bhedapratyayamupAdAya karmavidhayaH pravR^itAH sa yasyopamarditaH sadekamevAdvitIyaM tatsatyaM vikArabhedo 'nR^itamityetadvAkyapramANajanitenaikatvapratyayena sa sarvakarmabhyo nivR^itto nimittanivR^itte:,sa ca nivR^ittakarmA brahmasaMstha ucyate, sa ca parivrADevAnyasyAsambhavAt /
anyo hyanivR^ittabhedapratyayaH so 'nyatpashya¤shR^iNvanmanvAno vijAnannidaM kR^itvedaM prApnuyAmiti hi manyate /
tasyaivaM kurvato na brahmasaMsthatA /
vAcArambhaNamAtravikArAnR^itAbhisandhipratyayatvAt /
na cAsatyamityupardite bhedapratyaye satyamidamanena kartavyaM mayeti pramANaprameyabuddhirupapadyate /
AkAsha iva talamalabuddhirvivekinaH /
upamardite 'pi bhedapratyaye karmabhyo na nivartate cetprAgiva bhedapratyayopamardanAdekatvapratyayavidhAyakaM vAkyamapramANIkR^itaM syAt /
abhakShyabhakShaNAdipratiShedhavAkyAnAM prAmANyavadyuktamekatvavAkyasyApi prAmANyam /
sarvopaniShadAM tatparatvAt /
karmavidhInAmaprAmANa ayaprasaN^ga iti cet /
na /
anupamarditabhedapratyayavatpuruShaviShaye prAmANyopapatteH svapnAdipratyaya iva prAkprabodhAt /
vivekinAmakaraNAtkarmavidhiprAmANyoccheda iti cet /
na /
kAmyavidhyanucchedadarshanAt /
na hi kAmAtmatA na prashastetyevaMvij~nAnavadbhiH kAmyAni karmANi nAnuShThIyanta iti kAmyakarmavidhaya ucchidyante 'nuShThIyanta eva kAmibhiriti /
tathA brahmasaMsthairbrahmavidbhirnAnuShThIyante karmANIti na tadvidhaya ucchidyante 'brahmavidbhiranuShThIyanta eveti /
parivrAdakAnAM bhikShAcaraNAdivadutpannaikatvapratyayAnAmapi gR^ihasthAdInAmagnihotrAdikarmAnivR^ittiriti cenna /
prAmANyacintAyAM puruShapravR^itteradR^iShTAntatvAt /
na hi nAbhicarediti pratiShiddhamapyabhicaramaM kashcitkurvandR^iShTa iti shatrau dveSharahitenApi vivekinAbhicaraNaM kriyate /
na ca karmavidhipravR^ittinimitte bhedapratyaye bAdhite 'gnihotrAdau pravartakaM nimittamasti, parivrAjakasyeva bhikShAcaraNAdau bubhukShAdi pravartakam /
ihApyakaraNe pratyavAyabhayaM pravartakamiti cet /
na /
bhedapratyayavato 'dhikR^itatvAt /
bhedapratyayavAnanupamarditabhedabuddhirvidyayA yaH sa karmaNyadhikR^ita ityavocAma /
yo hyadhikR^itaH karmaNi tasya tadakarame pratyavAyo na nivR^ittAdhikArasya gR^ihasthasyeva brahmacAriNo visheShadharmAnanuShThAne /
evaM tarhi sarvaH svAshramastha utpannekatvapratyayaH parivrADiti cet  /
na /
svasvAmitvabhedabuddhyanivR^itteH /
karmArthatvAccetarAshramANAm /
"atha karma kurvIya"iti shruteH /
tasmAtsvasvAmitvAbhAvAdbhikShureka eva parivrAT /
na gR^ihasthAdiH /
ekatvapratyayavidhijanitena pratyayena vidhinimittabhedapratyayasyopamarditatvAdyamaniyamAdyanupapattiH parivrAjakasyeti cet /
na /
bubhukShAdinaikatvapratyayAtprAcyAvitasyopapatternivR^ittyarthatvAt /
na ca pratiShiddhasevAprAptiH /
ekatvapratyayotpatteH prAgeva pratiShiddhatvAt /
na hi rAtrau kUpe kaNTake vA patita udite 'pi savitari patati tasminneva /
tasmAtsiddhaM nivR^ittakarmA bhikShuka eva brahmasaMstha iti /
yatpunaruktaM sarveShAM j~nAnavarjitAnAM puNyalokateti /
satyametat /
yaccoktaM tapaHshabdena parivrADapyukta iti /
etadasat /
kasmAt /
parivrAjakasyaiva brahmasaMsthatAsambhavAt /
sa eva hyavasheShita ityavocAma /
ekatvavij~nAnavato 'gnihotrAdivattaponivR^itteshca /
bhedabuddhimata eva hi tapaHkartavyatA syAt /
etena karmacchidre brahmasaMsthatAsAmarthyaM apratiShedhashca pratyuktaH /
tathA j~nAnavAneva nivR^ittakarmA parivrADiti j~nAnavaiyarthyaM pratyuktam /
yatpunaruktaM yavavarAhAdishabdavatparivrAjake na rUDho brahmasaMsthashabda iti tatparihR^itam /
tasyaiva brahmasaMsthatAsambhavAnnAnyasyeti /
yatpunaruktaM rUDhashabdA nimittaM nopAdadata iti /
tanna /
gR^ihasthatakShaparivrAjakAdishabdadarshanAt /
gR^ihasthitipArivrAjyatakShaNAdinimittopAdAnA api gR^ihasthaparivrAjakAshramivisheShe vishiShTajAtimati ca takSheti rUDhA dR^ishyante shabdAH /
na yatra yatra tAni nimittAni tatra tatra vartante /
prasiddhyabhAvAt /
tathehApi brahmasaMsthashabdo nivR^ittasarvakarmatatsAdhanaparivrADekaviShaye 'tyAshramiNi paramahaMsAkhye vR^itta iha bhavitumarhati /
mukhyAmR^itatvaphalashravaNAt /
atashcedamevaikaM vedoktaM pArivrAjyam /
na yaj~nopavItatridaNDakamaNDalvAdiparigraha iti /
"muNDo 'parigraho 'saN^ga"iti shrutiH"atyAkShamibyaH paramaM pavitram" ityAdi ca shvetAshvatarIye /
"niHstutirnirnamaskAra"ityAdismR^itibhyashca /
"tasmAtkarma na kurvanti yatayaH pAradarshinaH" /
"tasmAdaliN^go dharmaj~no 'vyaktaliN^ga"ityAdismR^itibhyashca /
yattu sAMkhyaiH karmatyAgo 'bhyupagamyate /
kriyAkArakaphalabhedabuddheH satyatvAbhyupagamAt tanmR^iShA /
yacca bauddhaiH shUnyatAbhyupagamAdakartR^itvamabhyupagamyate /
tadapyasat /
tadabhyupagantuH sattvAbhyupagamAt /

tasmAdvedAntapramANajanitaikatvapratyayavata eva karmanivR^ittilakShaNaM pArivrAjyaM brahmasaMsthatvaM ceti siddham /

nanvagnyutsAdanadoShabhAksyAtparivrajan /

#<tasya ye prAJNco rashmayas tA evAsya prAcyo madhunADyaH |
R^ica eva madhukR^itaH |
R^igveda eva puShpam |
tA amR^itA ApaH |
tA vA etA R^icaH || ChUp_3,1.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,1.2 tasya saviturmadhvAshrayasya madhuno ye prAJNcaH prAcyAM dishi gatA rashmayastA evAsya prAcyaH prAgaJNcanAnmadhuno nADyo madhunADya iva madhvAdhAracchidrANItyarthaH /
tatra R^ica eva madhukR^ito lohitarUpaM savitrAshrayaM madhu kurvantIti madhukR^ito bhramarA iva yato rasAnAdAya madhu kurvanti /
tatpuShpamiva puShpamR^igveda eva /
tatra R^igbrAhmaNasamudAyasya R^igvedAkhyatvAcchabdamAtrAcca bhogyarUparasanisrAvAsambhavAdR^igvedashabdenAtra R^igvedavihitaM karma /
tato hi karmaphalabhUtamadhurasanisrAvasambhavAt /
madhukarairiva puShpasthAnIyAdR^igvedavihitAtkarmaNo 'pa AdAya R^igbhirmadhu nirvartyate /
kAstA Apa ityAha-tAH karmaNi prayuktAH somAjyapayorUpA agnau prakShiptAstatpAkAbhinirvR^ittA amR^itA amR^itArthatvAdatyanta rasavatya Apo bhavanti /
tadrasAnAdAya tA vA etA ÌcaH puShpebhyo rasamAdadAnA eva bhramarAH R^icaH //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 3,1.3

#<etam R^igvedam abhyatapan |
tasyAbhitaptasya yashas teja indriyaM vIryam annAdyaM raso 'jAyata || ChUp_3,1.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,1.3 etamR^igvedamR^igvedavihitaM karma puShpasthAnIyamabhyatapannabhitApaM kR^itavatya ivaitA R^icaH karmaNi prayuktAH /
Ìgbhirhi mantraiH shasrAdyaN^gabhAvamupagataiH kriyamANaM karma madhunirvartakaM rasaM muJNcatItyupapadyate puShpANIva bhramarairAcUShyamANAni /
tadetadAha-tasyargvedasyAbhitaptasya /
ko 'sau raso ya R^iÇmadhukarAbhitApaniHsR^ita ityucyate /
yasho vishrutatvaM tejo dehagatA dIptirindriyaM sAmarthyopetairindriyairavaikalyaM vIryaM sAmarthyaM balamityarthaH /
annAdyamannaM ca tadAdyaM ca yenopayujyamAnenAhanyahani devAnAM sthitiH syAttadannAdyameSha raso 'jAyata yAgAdilakShaNAtkarmaNaH //3 //

ChUpBh_3.8.1-4, 9.1-4, 10.1-4 tathA pashcAduttarata UrdhvamudetA viparyayeNAstametA /
pUrvasmAtpUrvasmAddviguNottarottareNa kAlenetyapaurANaM darshanam /

atroktaH parihAra AcAryaiH /
amarAvatyAdInAM purINAM dviguNottarottareNa kAlenodvAsaH syAt /

tannivAsinAM ca prANinAmabhAve tAnprati tenaiva mArgeNa gacchannapi naivodetA nAstameteti cakShurgocarApattestadatyayasya cAbhAvAt /
tathAmarAvatyAH sakAshAddviguNaM kAlaM saMyamanI purI vasatyatastannivAsinaH prANinaH prati dakShiNata ivodetyuttarato 'stametItyucyate 'smadbuddhiM cApekShya /
tathottarAsvapi purIShu yojanA /
sarveShAM ca meruruttarato bhavati /
yadAmarAvatyAM madhyAhnagataH savitA tadA saMyamanyAmudyandR^ishyate tatra madhyAhnagato vAruNyAmudyandR^ishyate, tathottarasyAM, pradakShiNAvR^ittestulyatvAt /
ilAvR^itavAsinAM sarvataH parvataprAkAranivAritAdityarashmInAM savitordhva ivodetAvagistametA dR^ishyate /
parvatordhvacchidrapraveshAtsavitR^iprakAshasya /
tathargAdyamR^itopajIvinAmamR^itAnAM ca dviguNottarottaravIryavattvamanumIyate bhogakAladvaiguNyaliN^gena /
udyamanasaMveshanAdi devAnAM rudrAdInAM viduShashca samAnam //1-4 //

START ChUp 3,11.1

__________


ChUpBh_3,11.1 kR^itvaivamudayAstamanena prANinAM svakarmaphalabhoganimittamanugrahaM tatkarmaphalopabhogakShaye tAni prANijAtAnyAtmani saMhR^ityAtha tatastasmAdanantaraM prANyanugrahakAlAdUrdhvaH sannAtmanyudetyodgamya yAnpratyudeti teShAM prANinAmabhAvAtsvAtmastho naivodetA nAstametaikalo 'dvitIyo 'navayavo madhye svAtmanyeva sthAtA /
tatra kashcidvidvAnvasvAdisamAnacaraNo rohitAdyamR^itabhogabhAgI yathoktakrameNa svAtmAnaM savitAramAtmatvenopetya samAhitaH sannetaM mantraM dR^iShTvotthito 'nyasmai pR^iShTavate jagAda /

START ChUp 3,11.2

#<na vai tatra na nimloca |
nodiyAya kadAcana |
devAs tenAhaM satyena |
mA virAdhiShi brahmaNeti || ChUp_3,11.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,11.2 na vai tatra yato 'haM brahmalokAdAgatastasminna vai tatraitadasti yatpR^icchasi /
na hi tatra nimloco 'stamagamatsavitA na codiyAyodgataH kutashcitkadAcana kasmiMshcidapi kAla iti /
udayAstamayavarjito brahmaloka ityanupapannamityuktaH shuthamiva pratipede /
he devAH sAkShiNo yUyaM shR^iNuta yathA mayoktaM satyaM vacastena steyanAhaM brahmaNA brahmasvarUpeNa mA virAdhiShi mA virudhyeyamaprAptirbrahmaNA mama mA bhUdityarthaH //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 3,11.3

#<na ha vA asmA udeti na nimlocati |
sakR^id divA haivAsmai bhavati |
ya etAm evaM brahmopaniShadaM veda || ChUp_3,11.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,11.3 satyaM tenoktamityAha shrutiH-na ha vA asmai yathoktabrahmavide nodeti na nimlocati nAstameti kiM tu brahmavide 'smai sakR^iddivA haiva sadaivAharbhavati svayaJNjyotiShTvAdya etAM yathoktAM brahmopaniShadaM vedaguhyaM veda /
evaM tantreNa vaMshAditrayaM pratyamR^itasambandhaM ca yaccAnyadavocAmaivaM jAnAtItyarthaH /
vidvAnudayAstamayakAlAparicchedyaM nityamajaM brahma bhavatItyarthaH //3 //

START ChUp 3,11.4

#<tad dhaitad brahmA prajApataya uvAca |
prajApatir manave |

__________


ChUpBh_3,11.4 taddhaitanmadhuj~nAnaM brahmA hiraNyagarbho virAje prajApataya uvAca /

kiM ca taddhaitanmadhuj~nAnamuddAlakAyA'ruNaye pitA

START ChUp 3,14.1

#<sarvaM khalv idaM brahma tajjalAn iti shAnta upAsIta |

__________


ChUpBh_3,14.1 punastasyaiva tripAdamR^itasya brahmaNo 'nantaguNavato 'nantashakteranekabhedopAsyasya vishiShTaguNashaktimatvenopAsanaM vidhitsannAha-sarvaM samastaM;khalviti vAkyAlaN^kArArtho nipAtaH /

tasmAdbrahmaNo jAtaM tejobannAdikrameNa sarvam /
atastajjam /
tathA tenaiva jananakrameNa pratilomatayA tasminneva brahmaNi lIyate tadAtmatayA shliShyata iti tallam /
tathA tasminneva sthitikAle 'niti prANiti ceShTata iti /
evaM brahmAtmatayA triShu kAleShvavishiShTaM tadvyatirekeNAgrahaNAt /
atastadevedaM jagat /
yathA cedaM tadevaikamadvitIyaM tathA ShaShThe vistareNa vakShyAmaH /
yasmAcca sarvamidaM brahma, ataH shAnto rAgadveShAdidoSharahitaH saMyataH sanyattatsarvaM brahma tadvakShyamANairguNairupAsIta /
kathamupAsIta /
kratuM kurvIta kraturnishcayo 'dhyavasAya evameva nAnyathetyavicalaH pratyayastaM kratuM kurvItopAsItetyanena vyavahitena sambandhaH /
kiM punaH kratukaraNena kartavyaM prayojanam /
kathaM vA kratuH kartavyaH kratukaraNaM cAbhipretArthasiddhisAdhanaM kathamityasyArthasya pratipAdanArthamathetyAdigranthaH /
atha khalviti hetvarthaH /
yasmAtkratumayaH kratuprAyo 'dhyavasAyAtmakaH puruSho jIvaH /
yathAkraturyAdR^ishaH kraturasya so 'yaM yathAkraturyathAdhyavasAyo yAdR^iÇnishcayo 'smiMlloke jIvanniha puruSho bhavati tatheto 'smAddehAtpretya mR^itvA bhavati /
kratvanurUpaphalAtmako bhavatItyarthaH /
evaM hyetacchAsrato dR^iShTam /
"yaM yaM vApi smaranbhAvaM tyajatyante kalevaram"ityAdi /
yata evaM vyavasthA shAsradR^iShTAtaH sa evaM jAnankatuM kurvIta yAdR^ishaM kratuM vakShyAmastam /
yata evaM shAsraprAmANyAdupapadyate kratvanurUpaM phalamataH sa kartavyaH kratuH //1 //

START ChUp 3,14.2

#<manomayaH prANasharIro bhArUpaH satyasaMkalpa AkAshAtmA sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH sarvagandhaH sarvarasaH sarvam idam abhyatto 'vAky anAdaraH || ChUp_3,14.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,14.2 katham /
manomayo manaHprAyaH /
manute 'neneti manastatsvavR^ittyA viShayeShu pravR^ittaM bhavati tena manasA tanmayaH, tathA pravR^itta iva tatprAyo nivR^itta iva ca /
ata eva prANasharIraH prANo liN^gAtmA vij~nAnakriyAshaktidvayasaMmIrchitaH /
"yo vai prANaH sA praj~nA yA vA praj~nA sa prANaH"iti shruteH /
sa sharIraM yasya sa prANasharIraH /
"manomayaH £ANasharIranetA"iti ca shrutyantarAt /
bhArUpaH /
bhA dIptishcaitanyalakShaNaM rUpaM yasya sa bhArUpaH /
satyasaN^kalpaH /
satyA avitathAH saN^kalpA yasya so 'yaM satyasaN^kalpaH /
na yathA saMsAriNa ivAnaikAntikaphalaH saN^kalpa IshvarasyetyarthaH /
anR^itena mithyAphalatvahetunA pratyUDhatvAtsaN^kalpasya mithyAphalatvam /
vakShyatyanR^itena hi pratyUDhA iti /
AkAshAtmA /
AkAsha ivA'tmA svarUpaM yasya sa AkAshAtmA /
sarvagatatvaM sUkShmatvaM rUpadihInatvaM cA'kAshatulyateshvarasya /
sarvakarmA /
sarvaM vishvaM teneshvareNa kriyata iti jagatsarvaM karmAsya sa sarvakarmA /
"sa hi sarvasya kartA"iti shruteH /
sarvakAmaH /
sarve kAmA doSharahitA asyeti sarvakAmaH /
"dharmaviruddho bhUteShu kAmo 'smi"iti smR^iteH /
nanu kAmo 'smIti vacanAdiha bahuvrIhistathA kAmo 'smItismR^ityartho vAcyaH /
sarvagandhaH /
sarve gandhAH sukhakarA asya so 'yaM sarvagandhaH /
"puNyo gandhaH pR^ithivyAm"iti smR^iteH /
tathA rasA api vij~neyAH. apuNyagandharasagrahaNasya pApmasambandhanimittatvashravaNAt /
"tasmAttenobhayaM jighrati surabhi ca durgandhi ca /
pApmanA hyeShu viddhaH"iti shruteH /
na ca pApmasaMsarga Ishvarasya, avidyAdidoShasyAnupapatteH /
sarvamidaM jagadabhyAtto 'bhivyAptaH /
atatervyAptyarthasya kartari niShThA /
tathAvAkyucyate 'nayeti vAgvAgeva vAkaH /
dvA vacergha¤antasya karaNe vAk /
sa yasya vidyate sa vAkI na vAkyavAkI /
vAkpratiShedhashcAtropalakShaNArthaH /
gandharasAdishravaNAdIshvarasya prAptAnighrANAdIni karaNAni gandhAdigrahaNAya /
ato vAkpratiShedhena pratiShidhyante tAni /
"apANipAdo javano grahItA pashyatyacakShuH sa shR^iNotyakarNaH"ityAdimantravarNAt /
anAdaro 'saMbhramaH /
aprAptaprAptau hi saMbhramaH syAdanAptakAmasya /
na tvAptakAmatvAnnityatR^iptasyeshvarasya saMbhramo 'sti kvacit //2 //

START ChUp 3,14.3

#<eSha ma AtmA antarhR^idaye 'NIyAn vrIher vA yavAd vA sarShapAd vA shyAmAkAd vA shyAmAkataNDulAd vA |
eSha ma AtmA antarhR^idaye jyAyAn pR^ithivyA jyAyAn antarikShAj jyAyAn divo jyAyAn ebhyo lokebhyaH || ChUp_3,14.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,14.3 eSha yathoktaguNo me mamA'tmAntarhR^idaye hR^idayapuNDarIkasyAntarmadhye 'NIyAnaNutaro vrIhervA yavAdvetyAdyatyantasUkShmatvapradarshanArtham /

jyAyaHparimANAcca jyAyastvaM darshayannanantaparimANatvaM darshayati //3 //

START ChUp 3,14.4

#<sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH sarvagandhaH sarvarasaH sarvam idam abhyatto 'vAkyanAdaraH |
eSha ma AtmA antarhR^idaye |
etad brahma |
etam itaH pretyAbhisaMbhavitA asmIti yasya syAd addhA na vicikitsA asti |
iti ha smAha shANDilyaH shANDilyaH || ChUp_3,14.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,14.4 manomaya ityAdinA jyAyAnebhyo lokebhya ityantena yathoktaguNalakShaNa Ishvaro dhyeyo na tu tadguNavishiShTa eva yathA rAjapuruShamAnaya citraguM vetyukte na visheShaNashyApyAnayane vyApriyate tadvadihApIti prAptamatastannivR^ittyartha sarvakarmetyAdi punarvacanam /

ata eva ShaShThasaptamayoriva tattvamasyAtmaivedaM sarvamiti neha svArAjye 'bhiShiJNcati /
eSha ma AtmaitadbrahmaitamitaH pratyAbhisambhavitAsmIti liN^gAnna tvAtmashabdena pratyagAtmaivocyate /
mameti ShaShThyAH sambandhArthapratyAyakatvAdetamabhisambhavitAsmIti ca karmakartR^itvanirdeshAt /
nanu ShaShThe 'pyatha sampatsya iti satsampatteH kAlAntaritatvaM darshayati /
na, ArabdhasaMskArasheShasthityarthaparatvAt na kAlAntaritArthatA /
anyathA tattvamasItyetasyArthasya bAdhaprasaN^gAt /
yadyapyAtmashabdasya pratyagarthatvaM sarvaM khalvidaM brahmeti ca prakR^itameSha ma AtmAntarhR^idaya etadbrahmetyucyate tathApyantardhAnamIShadaparityajyaivaitamAtmAnamito 'smAccharIrAtpretyAbhisambhavitAsmItyuktam /
yathAkraturUpasyA'tmanaH pratipattAsmIti yasyaivaMvidaH syAdbhavedaddhA satyamevaM syAmahaM pretya evaM na syAmiti na ca vicikitsAstItyetasminnarthe kratuphalasambandhe sa tathaiveshvarabhAvaM pratipadyate vidvAnityetadAha smoktavAnkila shANDalyo nAmarShiH /
dvirabhyAsa AdarArthaH //4//

START ChUp 3,15.1

#<antarikShodaraH kosho bhUmibudhno na jIryati |

START ChUp 3,15.2

#<tasya prAcI dig juhUr nAma |

subhUtA nAmodIcI |
tAsAM vAyur vatsaH |

mA putrarodaM rudam || ChUp_3,15.2 ||>#

START ChUp 3,16.1

#<puruSho vAva yaj~naH |
tasya yAni caturviMshativarShANi tat prAtaHsavanam |

ChUpBh_3,16.1 putrAyuSha upAsanamuktaM japashca /
athedAnImAtmano dIrghajIvanAyedamupAsanaM japaM ca vidadhadAha /
jIvanhi svayaM putrAdiphalena yujyate nAnyathA ityata AtmAnaM yaj~naM sampAdayati-puraShaH puruSho jIvanavishiShTaH kAryakaraNasaN^ghAto yathAprasiddha eva /

START ChUp 3,17.5

#<tasmAd AhuH soShyaty asoShTeti |
punar utpAdanam evAsya tat |
maraNam evAvabhR^ithaH || ChUp_3,17.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,17.5 yasmAcca yaj~naH puraShastasmAttaM janayiShyati mAtA yadA tadA'huranye soShyatIti tasya mAtaraM yadA ca prasUtA bhavati tadAsoShTa pUrNiketi vidhiyaj~na iva soShyati somaM devadatto 'soShTa somaM yaj~nadatta iti, ataH shabdasAmAnyAdvA puruSho yaj~naH /
punarutpAdanamevAsya tatpuruShAkhyasya yaj~nasya yatsoShyatyasoShTeti shabdasambandhitvaM vidhiyaj~nasyeva /
kiJNca tanmaraNamevAsya puruShayaj~nasyAvabhR^ithaH samAptisAmAnyAt //5 //

START ChUp 3,17.6

#<tad dhaitad ghora AN^girasaH kR^iShNAya devakIputrAyoktvovAca |
apipAsa eva sa babhUva |
so 'ntavelAyAm etat trayaM pratipadyetAkShitam asy acyutam asi prANasaMshitam asIti |
tatraite dve R^icau bhavataH || ChUp_3,17.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,17.6 taddhaitadyaj~nadarshanaM ghoro nAmata AN^giraso gotrataH kR^iShNAya devakIputrAya shiShyAyokatvovAca tadetattrayamityAdivyavahitena sambandhaH /
sa caitaddarshanaM shrutvApipAsa evAmyAbhyo vidyAbhyo babhUva /
itthaM ca vishiShTeyaM vidyA yatkR^iShNasya devakIputrasyAnyAM vidyAM prati tR^iDvicchedakarIti puruShayaj~navidyAM stauti /
ghora AN^girasaH kR^iShNAyoktvemAM vidyAM kimuvAceti tadAha-sa evaM yathoktayaj~navidantavelAyAM maraNakAla etanmantratrayaM pratipadyeta japedityarthaH /
kiM tadakShitamakShINamakShataM vAsItyekaM yajuH sAmarthyAdAdityasthaM prANaM caikIkR^ityA'ha /
tathA tamevA'hAcyutaM svarUpAdapracyutamasIti dvitIyaM yajuH /
prANasaMshitaM prANashca sa saMshitaM samyaktanUkR^itaM ca sUkShmaM tattvamasIti tR^itIyaM yajuH /
tatraitasminnarthe vidyAstutipare dve R^icau mantrau bhavato na japArthe /
trayaM pratipadyeteti tritvasaMkhyAbAdhanAt /
paJNcasaMkhyA hi tadA syAt //6 //

START ChUp 3,17.7

#<Adit pratnasya retasaH |
ud vayaM tamasaspari |
jyotiH pashyanta uttaram |
svaH pashyanta uttaram |
devaM devatrA sUryam aganma jyotir uttamam iti jyotir uttamam iti || ChUp_3,17.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,17.7 AdidityatrA'kArasyAnubandhastakAro 'narthaka icchabdashca /
pratnasya cirantanasya purANasyetyarthaH /
retasaH kAraNasya bIjabhUtasya jagataH sadAkhyasya jyotiH prakAshaM pashyanti /
Ashabda utsR^iShTAnubandhaH pashyantItyanena sambadhyate /
kiM tajjayotiH pashyanti /
vAsaramaharahariva tatsarvato vyAptaM brahmaNo jyotiH /
nivR^ittacakShuSho brahmavido brahmacaryAdinivR^ittisAdhanaiH shuddhAntaHkaraNA A samantato jyotiH pashyantItyarthaH /
paraH paramiti liN^gavyatyayena, jyotiShparatvAt /
yadidhyate dIpyate divi dyotanavati pasminbrahmaNi vartamAnam /
yena jyotiSheddhaH savitA tapati candramA bhAti vidyudvidyotate grahatArAgaNA vibhAsante /
kiJNcAnyo mantradR^igAha yathoktaM jyotiH pashyan /
udvayaM tamaso 'j~nAnalakShaNAtpari parastAditi sheShaH /
tamaso vApanetR^i yajjayotiruttaramAdityasthaM paripashyanto vayamudaganmeti vyavahitena sambandhaH /
tajjyotiH svaH svamAtmIyamasmaddhR^idi sthitam /
AdityasthaM ca tadekaM jyotiH /
yaduttaramutkR^iShTataramUrdhvataraM vAparaM jyotirapekShya pashyanta udaganma vayam /
kamudaganmetyAha /
devaM dyotanavantaM devatrA deveShu sarveShu sUryaM rasAnAM rashmInAM prANAnAM ca jagata IraNAtsUryastamudaganma gatavanto jyotiruttamaM sarvajyotirbhya utkR^iShTatamamaho prAptA vayamityarthaH /
idaM tajjyotiryadR^igbhyAM stutaM yadyajustrayeNa prakAshitam /
dvirabhyAso yaj~nakalpanAparisamAptyarthaH //7//

START ChUp 3,18.1

#<mano brahmety upAsIta |
ity adhyAtmam |

__________


ChUpBh_3,18.1 manomaya Ishvara ukta AkAshAtmeti ca brahmaNo guNaikadeshatvena /
athedAnIM mana AkAshayoH samastabrahmadR^iShTividhAnArtha Arambho mano brahmetyAdi /

START ChUp 3,18.2

#<tad etac catuShpAd brahma |

athAdhidaivatam |

__________


ChUpBh_3,18.2 tadetanmana AkhyaM catuShpAdbrahma, catvAraH pAdA asyeti /

START ChUp 3,18.3

#<vAg eva brahmaNash caturthaH pAdaH |

__________


ChUpBh_3,18.3 tatra vAgeva manaso brahmaNashcaturthaH pAda itarapAdatrayApekShayA /

ato manasaH pAda iva vAk /

athavA tailaghR^itAdyAgneyAshaneneddhA vAgbhAti ca tapati ca vadanAyotsAhavatI syAdityarthaH /

#<shrotram eva brahmaNash caturthaH pAdaH |

START ChUp 3,19.1

#<Adityo brahmety AdeshaH |
tasyopavyAkhyAnam |
asad evedam agra AsIt |
tat sad AsIt |
tat samabhavat |
tad ANDaM niravartata |
tat saMvatsarasya mAtrAm ashayata |
tan nirabhidyata |
te ANDakapAle rajataM ca suvarNaM cAbhavatAm || ChUp_3,19.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,19.1 Adityo brahmaNaH pAda ukta iti tasminsakalabrahmadR^iShTyarthamidamArabhyate-Adityo brahmetyAdesha upadeshastasyopavyAkhyAnaM kriyate stutyartham /
asadavyakR^itanAmarUpamidaM jagadasheShamagre prAgavasthAyAmutpatterAsInna tvasadeva /
kathamasataH sajjAyetetyasatkAryatvasya pratiShedhAt /
nanvihAsadeveti vidhAnAdvikalpaH syAt /
na, kriyAsviva vastuni vikalpAnupapatteH /
kathaM tarhIdamasadeveti /
nanvavocAmAvyAkR^itanAmarUpatvAdasadivAsaditi /
nanvevashabdo 'vadhAraNArthaH /
satyamevaM, na tu sattvAbhAvamavadhArayati /
kiM tarhi?vyAkR^itanAmarUpAbhAvamavadhArayati nAmarUpavyAkR^itaviShaye sacchabdaprayogo dR^iShTaH /
tacca nAmarUpavyAkaraNamAdityAyattaM prAyasho jagataH tadabhAve hyandhaM tama idaM na praj~nAyeta kiJNcanetyatastatstutipare vAkye sadapIdaM rAj~naH kulaM sarvaguNasampanne pUrNavarmaNi rAjanyasatIti tadvat /
na ca sattvamasattvaM veha jagataH pratipipAdayiShitamAdityo brahmetyAdeshaparatvAt /
upasaMhariShyatyanta AdityaM brahmetyupAsta iti /
tatsadAsIttadasacchabdavAcyaM prAgutpatteH stimitamanispandamasadiva satkAryAbhimukhamIShadupajAtapravR^itti sadAsIttato labdhaparispandaM tatsamabhavadalpataranAmarUpavyAkaraNenAN^kurIbhUtami va bIjam /
tato 'pi krameNa sthUlIbhavattadadbhya ANDaM samavartata saMvR^ittam /
ANDamiti dairdhyaM chAndasam /
tadaNDaM saMvatsarasya kAlasya prasiddhasya mAtrAM parimANamabhinnasvarUpamevAshayata sthitaM babhUva /
tattataH saMvatsaraparimANAtkAlAdUrdhvaM nirabhidyata nirbhinnaM vayasAmivANDam /
tasya nirbhinnasyANDasya kapAle dve rajataM ca suvarNaM cAbhavatAM saMvR^itte //1 //

START ChUp 3,19.2

#<tad yad rajataM seyaM pR^ithivI |
yat suvarNaM sA dyauH |
yaj jarAyu te parvatAH |
yad ulbaM (sa) samegho nIhAraH |
yA dhamanayas tA nadyaH |
yad vAsteyam udakaM sa samudraH || ChUp_3,19.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,19.2 tattayoH kapAlayoryadrajataM kapAlamAsItseyaM pR^ithivI pR^ithivyupalakShitamadho 'NDakapAlamityarthaH /
yatsuvarNaM kapAlaM sA dyaurdyulokopalakShitamUrdhvaM kapAlamityarthaH /

yA garbhasya jAtasya dehe dhamanayaH shirAstA nadyo babhUvuH /
yattasya bastau bhavaM vAsteyamudakaM sa samudraH //2 //

START ChUp 3,19.3

#<atha yat tad ajAyata so 'sAv AdityaH |
taM jAyamAnaM ghoShA ulUlavo 'nUdatiShThant sarvANi ca bhUtAni sarve ca kAmAH |
tasmAt tasyodayaM prati pratyAyanaM prati ghoShA ulUlavo 'nUttiShThanti sarvANi ca bhUtAni sarve ca kAmAH || ChUp_3,19.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_3,19.3 atha yattadajAyata garbharUpaM tasminnaNDe so 'sAvAdityastamAdityaM jAyamAnaM ghoShAH shabdA ulUlava urUravo vistIrNaravA udatiShThannutthitavanta Ishvarasyeveha prathamaputrajanmani sarvANi ca sthAvarajaN^gamAni bhUtAni sarve ca teShAM bhUtAnAM kAmAH kAmyanta iti viShayAH strIvasrAnnAdayaH /
yasmAdAdityajanmanimittA bhUtakAmotpattistasmAdadyatve 'pi tasyA'dityasyodayaM prati pratyAyanaM pratyastagamanaM ca pratyathavA punaH punaH pratyAgamanaM pratyAyanaM tatprati tannimittIkR^ityetyarthaH /
sarvANi ca bhUtAni sarve ca kAmA ghoShA ulUlavashcAnUttiShThanti /
prasiddhaM hyetadudayAdau savituH //3 //

START ChUp 3,19.4

#<sa ya etam evaM vidvAn AdityaM brahmety upAste |

__________


ChUpBh_3,19.4 sa yaH kashcidetamevaM yathoktamahimAnaM vidvAnsannAdityaM brahmetyupAste sa tadbhAvaM pratipadyata ityarthaH /
kiJNca dR^iShTaM phalamabhyAshaH kShipraM tadvido yaditi kriyAvisheShaNamenamevaMvidaM sAdhavaH /
shobhanA ghoShAH /

START ChUp 4,1.1

#<jAnashrutir ha pautrAyaNaH shraddhAdeyo bahudAyI bahupAkya Asa |
sa ha sarvata AvasathAn mApayAM cakre sarvata eva me 'nnam atsyantIti || ChUp_4,1.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.1 vAyuprANayorbrahmaNaH pAdadR^iShTyadhyAsaH purastAdvarNitaH /
athedAnIM tayoH sAkShAdbrahmatvenopAsyatvAyottaramArabhyate /
sukhAvabodhArthA'khyAyikA, vidyAdAnagrahaNavidhipradarshanArthA ca shraddhAnnadAnAnuddhatatvAdInAM ca vidyAprApti sAdhanatvaM pradarshyata AkhyAyikayA /
jAnashrutirjanashrutasyApatyam /
haH aitihyArthaH /
putrasya pautraH pautrAyaNaH sa eva shraddhAdeyaH shraddhApuraHsarameva brAhmaNAdibhyo deyamasyeti shraddhAdeyaH /

evaN^guNasampanno 'sau jAnashrutiH pautrAyaNo vishiShTe deshe kAle ca kasmiMshcidAsa babhUva /

START ChUp 4,1.2

#<atha ha haMsA nishAyAm atipetuH |
tad dhaivaM haMso haMsam abhyuvAda |
ho ho 'yi bhallAkSha bhallAkSha jAnashruteH pautrAyaNasya samaM divA jyotir AtataM tan mA prasAN^kShIs tat tvAM mA pradhAkShIr iti || ChUp_4,1.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.2 tatraivaM sati rAjani tasmindharmakAle harmyatalasthe 'tha ha haMsA nishAyAM rAtrAvatipetuH /
R^iShayo devatA vA rAj~no 'nnadAnaguNaistoShitAH santo haMsArUpA bhUtvA rAj~no darshanagocare 'tipetuH /
tattasminkAle teShAM patatAM haMsAnAmekaH pR^iShThataH patannagrataH patantaM haMsamabhyuvAdAbhyuktavAnho ho 'yIti bho bho iti sambodhya bhallAkSha bhallAkShetyAdaraM darshayan yathA pashya pashyA'shcaryamiti tadvat /
bhallAkSheti mandadR^iShTitvaM sUcayannAha /
athavA samyagbrahmadarshanAbhimAnavattvAttasyAsakR^idupAlabdhastena pIDyamAno 'marShitayA tatsUcayati bhallAkSheti /
jAnashruteH pautrAyaNasya samaM tulyaM divA dyulokena jyotiH prabhAsvaramannadAnAdijanitaprabhAvajamAtataM vyAptaM dyulokaspR^igityarthaH /
divAhnA vA samaM jyotirityetat /

START ChUp 4,1.3

#<tam u ha paraH pratyuvAca kam v ara enam etat santaM sayugvAnam iva raikvam Attha iti |

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.3 tamevamuktavantaM para itaro 'gragAmI pratyuvAcAre nikR^iShTo 'yaM rAjA varAkastaM kamu enaM santaM kena mAhAtmyena yuktaM santamiti kutsayatyenamevaM sabahumAnametadvacanamAttha raikvamiva, sayugvAnaM saha yugvanA gantryA vartata iti sayugvA raikvaH /

ananurUpamasminnayuktamIdR^ishaM vaktuM raikva ivetyabhiprAyaH /

START ChUp 4,1.4

#<yathA kR^itAya vijitAyAdhareyAH saMyanty evam enaM sarvaM tad abhisameti yat kiMca prajAH sAdhu kurvanti |
yas tad veda yat sa veda sa mayaitad ukta iti || ChUp_4,1.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.4 yathA loke kR^itAyaH kR^ito nAmAyo dyUtasamaye prasiddhashcaturaN^kaH sa yadA jayati dyUte pravR^ittAnAM tasmai vijitAya tadarthamitare tridvyekAN^kA adhare 'yAstretAdvAparakalinAmAnaH saMyanti saMgacchante 'ntarbhavanti /
caturaN^ke kR^itAye tridvyekAN^kAnAM vidyamAnatvAttadantarbhavantItyarthaH /
yathAyaM dR^iShTAnta evamenaM raikvaM kR^itAyasthAnIyaM tretAdyAyasthAnIyaM sarvaM tadabhisametyantarbhavati raikve /
kiM tadyatkiJNca loke sarvAH prajAH sAdhu shobhanaM dharmajAtaM kurvanti tatsarvaM raikvasya dharme 'ntarbhavati /
tasya ca phale sarvaprANidharmaphalamantarbhavatItyarthaH /
tathAnyo 'pi kashcidyastadvedyaM veda /
kiM tadyadvedyaM sa raikvo veda /
tadvedyamanyo 'pi yo veda tamapi sarvaprANidharmajAtaM tatphalaM ca raikvamivAbhisametItyanuvartate /

START ChUp 4,1.5-6

#<tad u ha jAnashrutiH pautrAyaNa upashushrAva |
sa ha saMjihAna eva kShattAram uvAcAN^gAre ha sayugvAnam iva raikvam Attheti |
yo nu kathaM sayugvA raikva iti || ChUp_4,1.5 ||>#

#<yathA kR^itAya vijitAyAdhareyAH saMyanty evam enaM sarvaM tad abhisameti yat kiMca prajAH sAdhu kurvanti |
yas tad veda yat sa veda sa mayaitad ukta iti || ChUp_4,1.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.5,6 tadu ha tadetadIdR^ishaM haMsavAkyamAtmanaH kutsArUpamanyasya viduSho raikvAdeH prashaMsArUpamupashushrAva shrutavAnharmyatalastho rAjA jAnashrutiH pautrAyaNaH /
tacca haMsavAkyaM smaranneva paunaH punyena rAtrisheShamativAhayAmAsa /
tataH sa bandibhI rAjA stutiyuktAbhirvAgbhiH pratibodhyamAna uvAca kShattAraM saMjihAna eva shayanaM nidrAM vA parityajanneva he 'N^ga vatsAre sa sayugvAnamiva raikvamAttha kiM mAm /
sa eva stutyarhe nAhamityabhiprAyaH /
athavA sayugvAnaM raikvamAttha gatvA mama taddidR^ikShA;tadevashabdo 'vadhAraNArtho 'narthako vA vAcyaH /
sa ca kShattA pratyuvAca raikvAnayanakAmo rAj~no 'bhiprAyaj~no yo nu kathaM sayugvA raikva iti, rAj~naivaM cokta AnetuM taccihnaM j~natumicchanyo nu kathaM sayugvA raikva ityavocat /
sa ca bhallAkShavacanamevAvocat //5-6 //

START ChUp 4,1.7

#<sa ha kShattAnviShya nAvidam iti pratyeyAya |
taM hovAca yatrAre brAhmaNasyAnveShaNA tad enam arccheti || ChUp_4,1.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.7 tasya smaransa ha kShattA nagaraM grAmaM vA gatvAnviShya raikvaM nAvidaM na vyaj~nAsiShamiti pratyeyAya pratyAgatavAn /
taM hovAca kShattaramare yatra brAhmaNasya brahmavida ekAnte 'raNye nadIpulinAdau vivikte deshe 'nveShaNAnumArgaNaM bhavati tattatrainaM raikvamarcha R^iccha gaccha tatra mArgaNaM kurvityarthaH //7 //

START ChUp 4,1.8

#<so 'dhastAc chakaTasya pAmAnaM kaShamANam upopavivesha |

ahaM hy arA 3 iti ha pratijaj~ne |
sa ha kShattAvidam iti pratyeyAya || ChUp_4,1.8 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,1.8 ityuktaH kShattAnviShya taM vijane deshe 'dhastAcchakaTasya gantryAH pAmAnaM kharjUM kaShamANaM kaNDUyamAnaM dR^iShTvAyaM nUnaM sayugvA raikva ityupa samIpa upavivesha vinayenopaviShTavAn /

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi caturthAdhyAyasya prathamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 4,2.1

#<tad u ha jAnashrutiH pautrAyaNaH ShaT shatAni gavAM niShkam ashvatarIrathaM tad AdAya praticakrame |

__________


ChUpBh_4,2.1 tattatra R^iShergArhasthyaM pratyabhiprayaM buddhvA dhanArthitAM co ha, eva jAnashrutiH pautrAyaNaH ShaTshatAni gavAM niShkaM kaNThahAramashvatarIrathamashvatarIbhyAM yuktaM rathaM tadAdAya dhanaM gR^ihItvA praticakrame raikvaM prati gatavAn /
taM ca gatvAbhyuvAda hAbhyuktavAn //1 //

START ChUp 4,2.2

#<raikvemAni ShaT shatAni gavAm ayaM niShko 'yam ashvatarIrathaH |
anu ma etAM bhagavo devatAM shAdhi yAM devatAm upAssa iti || ChUp_4,2.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,2.2 he raikva gavAM ShaTshatAnImAni tubhyaM mayA'nItAnyayaM niShko 'shvatarIrathashcAyametaddhanamAdatsva bhagavo 'nushAdhi ca me mAmetAM yAM ca devatAM tvamupAHse taddevatopadeshena mAmanushAdhItyarthaH //2 //

START ChUp 4,2.3

#<tam u ha paraH pratyuvAcAha hAretvA shUdra tavaiva saha gobhir astv iti |

__________


ChUpBh_4,2.3 tamevamuktavantaM rAjAnaM pratyuvAca paro raikvaH /
ahetyayaM nipAto vinigrahArthIyo 'nyatreha tvanarthakaH /
evashabdasya pR^ithakprayogAt /
hAretvA hAreNa yuktetvA gantrI seyaM hAretvA gobhiH saha tavaivAstu tiShThatu na mamAparyAptena karmArthamanena prayojanamityabhiprAyo he shUdreti /
nanu rAjAsau kShattR^isambandhAtsa ha kShattAramuvAcetyuktam /
vidyAgrahaNAya ca brAhmaNasamIpopagamAcchUdrasya cAnadhikArAtkathamidamananurUpaM raikveNocyate he shUdreti /
tatrA'hurAcAryAH-haMsavacanashravaNAcchugenamAvivesha /
tenAsau shucA shrutvA raikvasya mahimAnaM vA AdravatIti R^iShirAtmanaH parokShaj~natAM darshaya¤shUdretyAheti /

na tu jAtyaiva shUdra iti /
apare punarAhuralpaM dhanamAhR^itamiti ruShaivainamuktavAJNchUdreti /

START ChUp 4,2.4-5

#<taM hAbhyuvAda |

#<tasyA ha mukham upodgR^ihNann uvAcAjahAremAH shUdrAnenaiva mukhenAlApayiShyathA iti |

tasmai hovAca || ChUp_4,2.5 ||>#


__________


ChUpBh_4,2.4,5 raikvedaM gavAM sahasramayaM niShko 'yamashvatarIratha iyaM jAyArthaM mama duhitA'nItAyaM ca grAmo yasminnAHse tiShThasi sa ca tvadarthe mayA kalpitaH tadetatsarvamAdAyAnushAdhyeva mA mAM he bhagava ityuktastasyA jAyArthamAnItAyA rAj~no duhiturhaiva mukhaM dvAraM vidyAyA dAne tIrthamupodgR^ihNaJNjAnannityarthaH /
brahmacArI dhanadAyI medhAvI shrotriyaH priyaH /
vidyayA vA vidyA prAha tAni tIrthAni ShaNmama //
iti vidyAyA vacanaM vij~nAyate hi /
evaM jAnannupodgR^ihNannuvAcoktavAn /
AjahArA'hR^itavAnbhavAnyadimA gA yaccAnyaddhanaM tatsAdhviti vAkyasheShaH /

tasmai rAj~ne dhanaM dattavate ha kilovAca vidyAM sa raikvaH //4-5 //

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi caturthAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 4,3.1

#<vAyur vAva saMvargaH |

ChUpBh_4,3.1 vAyurvAva saMvargo vAyurbAhyo vAvetyavadhAraNArthaH /

naiSha doShaH /

ChUpBh_4,3.2 tathA yadA'pa ucchuShyantyucchoShamApnuvanti tadA vAyumevApiyanti /

#<atha ha shaunakaM ca kApeyam abhipratAriNaM ca kAkShaseniM pariviShyamANau brahmacArI bibhikShe |

ChUpBh_4,3.5 athaitayoH stutyarthamiyamAkhyAyikA'rabhyate /

START ChUp 4,3.6

#<sa hovAca |
mahAtmanash caturo deva ekaH kaH sa jagAra bhuvanasya gopAH |

__________


ChUpBh_4,3.6 sa hovAca brahmacArI mahAtmanashcatura iti dvitIyAbahuvacanam /

START ChUp 4,3.7

#<tad u ha shaunakaH kApeyaH pratimanvAnaH pratyeyAya |
AtmA devAnAM janitA prajAnAM hiraÇyadaMShTro babhaso 'nasUriH |
mahAntam asya mahimAnam Ahur anadyamAno yad anannam atti |
iti vai vayam brahmacArin nedam upAsmahe dattAsmai bhikShAm iti || ChUp_4,3.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,3.7 tadu ha brahmacAriNo vacanaM shaunakaH kApeyaH pratimanvAno manasA'locayanbrahmacAriNaM pratyeyAyA'jagAma /
gatvA cA'ha-yaM tvamavoco na pashyanti martyA iti taM vayaM pashyAmaH /
katham?AtmA sarvasya sthAvarajaN^gamasya /
kiJNca devAnAmagnyAdInAmAtmani saMhR^itya grasitvA punarjanitotpAdayitA vAyurUpeNAdhidaivatamagnyAdInAm /
adhyAtmaM ca prANarUpeNa vAgAdInAM prajAnAM ca danitA /
atha vA'tmA devAnAmagnivAgAdInAM janitA prajAnAM sthAvarajaN^gamAnAm /
hiraNyadaMShTro 'bhagnadaMShTra iti yAvat /
babhaso bhakShaNashIlaH /
anasUriH sUrirmedhAvI na sUrirasUristatpratiShedho 'nasUriH sUrirevetyarthaH /
mahAntamatipramANamaprameyamasya prajApatermahimAnaM vibhUtimAhurbrahmavidaH /
yasmAtsvayamanyairanadyamAno 'bhakShyamANo yadanannamagnivAgAdidevatArUpamatti bhakShayatIti /
vA iti nirarthakaH /
vayaM he brahmacArin, A, idamevaM yathoktalakShaNaM brahma vayamA upAsmahe /
vayamiti vyavahitena sambandhaH /
anye na vayamidamupAsmahe /
kiM tarhi parameva brahmopAsmaha iti varNayanti /
dattAsmai bhikShAmityavocadbhR^ityAn //7 //
