START ChUp 4,3.8

#<tasmai u ha daduH |
te vA ete paJNcAnye paJNcAnye dasha santas tat kR^itam |
tasmAt sarvAsu dikShv annam eva dasha kR^itam |
saiShA virAD annAdI |
tayedaM sarvaM dR^iShTam |
sarvam asya idaM dR^iShTaM bhavaty annAdo bhavati ya evaM veda ya evaM veda || ChUp_4,3.8 ||>#

__________

tasmA u ha daduste hi bhikShAm /
te vai ye grasyante 'gnyAdayo yashca teShAM grasitA vAyuH paJNcAnye vAgAdibhyaH, tathAnye tebhyaH paJNcAdhyAtmaM vAgAdayaH prANashca, te sarve dasha santastatkR^itaM bhavati, te caturaN^ka ekAya evaM catvAraH tryaN^kAyaH evaM trayo 'pare dvyaN^kAyaH evaM dvAvanyAvekAN^kAya evameko 'nya, ityevaM desha santastatkR^itaM bhavati /
yata evaM tasmAtsarvAsu dikShu dashasvapyagnyAdyA vAgAdyAshca dashasaMkhyAsAmAnyAdannameva"dashAkSharA virAD virADannam" iti hi shrutiH /

ato 'nnameva dashasaMkhyatvAt /
tata eva dasha kR^itaM kR^ite 'ntarbhAvAccaturAyatvenetyavocAma /
saiShA virADdashasaMkhyA satyannaM cAnnAdyannAdinI ca kR^itatvena dashasaMkhyayAnnaM kR^itasaMkhyayAnnAdI tayA annAnnAdinyA idaM sarvaM jagaddashadiksaMsthaM dR^iShTaM kR^itasaMkhyAbhUtayopalabdham /
evaMvido 'sya sarvaM kR^itasaMkhyAbhUtasya dashadiksaMbaddhaM dR^iShTamupalabdhaM bhavati /
kiJNcAnnAdashca bhavati ya evaM veda yathoktadarshI /
dvirabhyAsa upAsanamAptyarthaH //8//

START ChUp 4,4.1

#<satyakAmo ha jAbAlo jabAlAM mAtaram AmantrayAM cakre |

__________

ChUpBh_4,4.1 sarvaM vAgAdyagnyAdi cAnnAnnAdatvasaMstutaM jagadekIkR^itya ShoDashadhA pravibhajya tasminbrahmadR^iShTirvidhAtavyetyArabhyate /
shraddhAtapasorbrahmopAsanAN^gatvapradarshanAyA'khyAyikA /

START ChUp 4,4.2

#<sA hainam uvAca |
nAham etad veda tAta yadgotras tvam asi |

sAham etan na veda yadgotras tvam asi |

sa satyakAma eva jAbAlo bruvIthA iti || ChUp_4,4.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,4.2 evaM pR^iShTA jabAlA sA hainaM putramuvAca-nAhametattava gotraM veda he tAta yadgotrastvamasi /
kasmAnna vetsItyuktA'ha-bahu bhartR^igR^ihe paricaryAjAtamatithyabhyAgatAdi carantyahaM paricAriNI paricarantIti paricaraNashIlaivAhaM paricaraNacittatayA gotrAdismaraNe mama mano nAbhUt /

START ChUp 4,4.3-4

#<sa ha hAridrumataM gautamam etyovAca |

#<taM hovAca kiMgotro nu somyAsIti |
sa hovAca |
nAham etad veda bho yadgotro 'ham asmi |
apR^icchaM mAtaram |
sA mA pratyabravId bahv aham carantI paricariNI yauvane tvAm alabhe |

ChUpBh_4,4.4 sa ha satyakAmo hAridrumataM haridrumato 'patyaM hAridrumataM gautamaM gotrata etya gatvovAca brahmacaryaM bhagavati pUjAvati tvayi vatsyAmyata upeyAmupagaccheyaM shiShyatayA bhagavantamityuktavantaM taM hovAca gautamaH /

START ChUp 4,4.5

#<taM hovAca |
naitad abrahmaNo vivaktum arhati |

upa tvA neShye na satyAd agA iti |
tam upanIya kR^ishAnAm abalAnAM catuHshatA gA nirAkR^itya uvAcemAH somyAnusaMvrajeti |
tA abhiprasthApayann uvAca |

sa ha varShagaNaM provAsa |

ChUpBh_4,4.5 taM hovAca gautamo naitadvaco 'brAhmaNo visheSheNa vaktumarhatyArjavArthasaMyuktam /

tAH samyaggAvo rakShitA yadA yasminkAle sahasraM saMpeduH saMpannA babhUvuH //5//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi caturthAdhyAyasya caturthaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 4,5.1

#<atha hainam R^iShabho 'bhyuvAda satyakAma 3 iti |
bhagava iti ha pratishushrAva |
prAptAH somya sahasraM smaH |
prApaya na AcAryakulam || ChUp_4,5.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,5.1 tametaM shraddhAtapobhyAM siddhaM vAyudevatA diksaMbandhinI tuShTA satyR^iShabhamanupravishyarShabhApannAnugrahAyAtha hainamR^iShabho 'bhyuvAdAbhyuktavAnsatyakAma 3 iti saMbodhya, tamasau satyakAmo bhagava iti ha pratishushrAva prativacanaM dadau /
praptAH somya sahasraM smaH pUrNA tava pratij~nAtaH prApaya no 'smAnAcAryakulam //1 //

START ChUp 4,5.2

#<brahmaNash ca te pAdaM bravANi iti |
bravItu me bhagavAn iti |
tasmai hovAca |
prAcI dik kalA |
praticI dik kalA |
dakShiNA dik kalA |
udIcI dik kalA |

ya eSha vidyuti puruSho dR^ishyate so 'ham asmi sa evAham asmIti || ChUp_4,13.1 ||>#

#<sa ya etam evaM vidvAn upAste |

nAsyAvarapuruShAH kShIyante |

ChUpBh_4,14.2,3 bhagava iti ha pratishushrAva /

ko nu mAnushiShyAdanushAsanaM kuryAdbho bhagavaMstvayi proShita itIhApeva nihnute 'panihnuta iveti vyavahitena sambandho na cApanihnute na ca yatAvadagnibhiruktaM bravItItyabhiprAyaH /
kathamime 'gnayo mayA paricaritA uktavanto nUnaM yatastvAM dR^iShTvA vepamAnA ivedR^ishA dR^ishyante pUrvamanyAdR^ishAH santa itIhAgnInabhyUde 'bhyuktavAnkAkvAgnIndarshayan /
kiM nu somya kila te tubhyamavocannagnaya iti pR^iShTa ityevamidamuktavanta ityevaM ha pratijaj~ne pratij~nAtavAnpratIkamAtraM kiJNcinna sarvaM yathoktamagnibhiruktamavocat /

ahaM tu te tubhyaM tadbrahma yadicchasi tvaM shrotuM vakShyAmi, shR^iNu tasya mayocyamAnasya brahmaNo j~nAnamAhAtmyaM yathA puShkarapalAshe padmapatra Apo na shilaShyanta evaM yatA vakShyAmi brahmaivaMvidi pApaM karma na shilaShyate na sambadhyata ityevamuktavatyAcArya Ahopakosalo bravItu me bhagavAniti tasmai hovAcA'cAryaH //2-3 //

START ChUp 4,15.1

#<ya eSho 'kShiNi puruSho dR^ishyata eSha Atmeti hovAca |

ChUpBh_4,15.1 ya eSho 'kShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate nivR^ittacakShurbhirbrahmacaryAdisAdhanasampannaiH shAntairvivekibhirdR^iShTerdraShTA"cakShuShashcakShuH"ityAdishrutyantarAt /

START ChUp 4,15.5

#<atha yad u caivAsmi¤ chavyaM kurvanti yadi ca nArciSham evAbhisaMbhavanti |

ChUpBh_4,15.5 athedAnIM yathoktabrahmavido gatirucyate /
yadyadi u caivAsminnevaMvidi shavyaM shavakarma mR^ite kurvanti yadi ca na kurvanti R^itvijaH sarvathApyevaMvittena shavakarmaNAkR^itenApi pratibaddho na brahma[dmaTaprApnoti /
na ca kR^itena shavakarmaNAsya kashcanAbhyadhiko lokaH /
"na karmaNA vardhate no kanIyAn"iti shrutyantarAt /
shavakarmaNyanAdaraM darshayanvidyAM stauti na punaH shavakarmaivaMvido na kartavyamiti /
akriyamANe hi shavakarmaNi karmaNA phalArambhe pratibandhaH kashcidanumIyate 'nyatra /
yata iha vidyAphalArambhakAle shavakarma syAdvA na veti vidyAvato 'pratibandhena phalArambhaM darshayati /
ye sukhAkAshamakShisthaM saMyadvAmo vAmanIrbhAmanIrityevaN^guNamupAsate prANasahitAmagnividyAM ca teShAmanyatkarma bhavatu mA vA bhUtsarvathApi te 'rciShamevAbhisambhavantyarcirabhimAninIM devatAmabhisambhavanti pratipadyanta ityarthaH /
arciSho 'rcirdevatAyA aharaharabhimAninIM devatAmahna ApUryamANapakShaM shuklapakShadevatAmApUryamANapakShAdyAnShaNmAsAnudaÇÇuttarAM dishameti savitA tAnmAsAnuttarAyaNadevatAM tebhyo mAsebhyaH saMvatsaraM saMvatsaradevatAM tataH saMvatsarAdAdidityamAdityAccandramasaM candramaso vidyutaM tattatrasthAMstAnpuruShaH kashcidbrahmalokAdetyAmAnavo mAnavyAM sR^iShTau bhavo mAnavo na mAnavo 'mAnavaH sa puruSha enAnbrahma satyalokasthaM gamayati gantR^igantavyagamayitR^itvavyapadeshebhyaH /
sanmAtrabrahmaprAptau tadanupapatteH /
brahmaiva sanbrahmApyetIti hi tatra vaktuM nyAyyam /
sarvabhedanirAsena sanmAtrapratipattiM vakShyati /
na cAdR^iShTo mArgo 'gamanAyopatiShThate /
"sa enamavidito na bhunakti"iti shrutyantarAt /
eSha devapathaH devairarcirAdibhiH gamayitR^itvenAdhikR^itaiH upalakShitaH panthA devapatha ucyate /
brahma gantavyaM tena copalakShita iti brahmapathaH /
etena pratipadyamAnA gacchanto brahmemaM mAnavaM manusambandhinaM manoH sR^iShTilakShaNamAvata nA'vartanta Avartante 'smiJNjananamaraNaprabandhacakrArUDhA ghaTIyantravatpunaH punarityArvatastaM na pratipadyante /
nAvartante nA'vartante iti dviruktiH saphalAyA vidyAyAH parisamAptipradarshanArthA //5//

START ChUp 4,16.1

#<eSha ha vai yaj~no yo 'yaM pavate |

ChUpBh_4,16.1 rahasyaprakaraNe prasaN^gAdAraNyakatvasAmAnyAcca yaj~ne kShata utpanne vyAhR^itayaH prAyashcittArthA vidhAtavyAstadabhij~nasya cartvijo brahmaNo maunamityata idamArabhyate-eSha ha vA eSha vAyuryo 'yaM pavate 'yaM yaj~naH /

" "ayaM vai yaj~no yo 'yaM pavate"ityAdishrutibhyaH /

na hyacalataH shuddhirasti /

#<anyatarAm eva vartanIM saMskaroti |

ChUpBh_4,16.3 tayorvartanyoranyatarAM vartanIM manasA vivekaj~nAnavatA saMskaroti brahmartvigvAcA vartanyA hotAdhvaryurudgAtetyete trayo 'pyR^itvijo 'nyatarAM vAglakShaNAM vartanIM vAcaiva saMskurvanti /

atha sa brahmA yatra yasminkAla upAkR^ite prArabdhe prAtaranuvAke shasre purA pUrvaM paridhAnIyAyA R^ico brahmaitasminnantare kAle vyavavadati maunaM parityajati yadi tadAnyatarAmeva vA#agvartanIM saMskaroti brahmaNAsaMskriyamANA manovartanI hIyate vinashyati cchidrIbhavatyanyatarA /
sa yaj~no vAgvartanyaivAnyatarayA vartitumashaknuvanriShyati /

#<sa yathobhayapAd vrajan ratho vobhAbhyAM cakrAbhyAM vartamAnaH pratitiShThaty evam asya yaj~naH pratitiShThati yaj~naM pratitiShThantaM yajamAno 'nu pratitiShThati |

START ChUp 4,17.10

#<mAnavo brahmaivaika R^itvikkurUnashvAbhirakShatyevaMviddha vai brahmA yaj~naM yajamAnaM sarvAMsh># #<cartvijo 'bhirakShati tasmAdevaMvidameva brahmANaM kurvIta nAnevaMvidaM nAnevaMvidam //10//>#

#<mAnavaH |
brahmaivaika R^itvik kurUn ashvAbhirakShati |
evaMvid dha vai brahmA yaj~naM yajamAnaM sarvAMsh cartvijo 'bhirakShati |
tasmAd evaMvidam eva brahmANaM kurvIta nAnevaMvidaM nAnevaMvidam || ChUp_4,17.10 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_4,17.10 mAnavo bhrahmA maunAcaraNAnmananAdvA j~nAvanattvAttato brahmaivaikartvikkurUnkartÌn /
yoddhÌnArUDhAnashvA vaDavA yathAbhirakShatyevaMviddha vai brahmA yaj~naM yajamAnaM sarvAMshcartvijo 'bhirakShati tatkR^itadoShApanayanAt /
yata evaMvishiShTo brahmA vidvAMstasmAdevaMvidameva yathoktavyAhR^ityAdividaM brahmANaM kurvIta nAnevaMvidaM kadAcaneti /
dvirabhyAso 'dhyAyaparisamAptyarthaH //10 //

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi caturthAdhyAyasya saptadashaH khaNDaH>#
#<iti shrImadgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyaparamahaMsapar ivrAjakAcAryashrImacchaN^karabhagavatpAdakR^itau cchAndogyopaniShadvivaraNe caturtho 'dhyAyaH>#

#<atha paJNcamo 'dhyAyaH>#

START ChUp 5,1.1

#<yo ha vai jyeShThaM ca shreShThaM ca veda jyeShThash ca ha vai shreShThash ca bhavati |

__________


ChUpBh_5,1.1
saguNa brahmavidyAyA uttarA gatiruktA /
athedAnIM paJNcame 'dhyAye paJNcAgnivido gR^ihasthasyordhvaretasAM ca shraddhAlUnAM vidyAntarashIlinAM tAmeva gatimanUdyAnyA dakShiNadiksambandhinI kevalakarmiNAM dhUmAdilakShaNA punarAvR^ittirUpA tR^itIyA ca tataH kaShTatarA saMsAragatirvairAgyahetorvaktavyetyArabhyate /
prANaH shreShTho vAgAdibhyaH prANo vAva saMvarga ityAdi ca bahusho 'tIte granthe prANagrahaNaM kR^itam /
sa kathaM shreShTho vAgAdiShu sarvaiH saMhatyakAritvAvisheShe?kathaM ca tasyopAsanamiti tasya shreShThatvAdiguNavidhitsayedamanantaramArabhyate-yo ha vai kashcijjyeShThaM ca prathamaM vayasA vAva jyeShThashca vayasA vAgAdibhyaH /
garbhasthe hi puruShe prANasya vR^ittirvAgAdibhyaH pUrvaM labdhAtmikA bhavati yayA garbho vivardhate cakShurAdisthAnAvayavaniShpattau satyAM pashcAdvAgAdInAM vR^ittilAbha iti prANo jyeShTho vayasA bhavati /
shreShThatvaM tu pratipAdayiShyati suhaya ityAdinidarshanena /
ataH prANa eva jyeShThashca shreShThashcAsminkAryakaraNasaN^ghAte //1 //

__________


ChUpBh_5,1.2 yo ha vai vasiShThaM vasitR^itamamAcchAdayitR^itamaM vasumattamaM vA yo veda sa tathaiva vasiShTho ha bhavati svAnAM j~nAtInAm /
kastarhi vasiShTha ityAha /

#<te ha prANAH prajApatiM pitaram etyocuH bhagavan ko naH shreShTha iti |

__________


ChUpBh_5,1.7 te ha - tai haivaM vivadamAnA AtmanaH shreShThatvavij~nAnAya prajApatiM pitaraM janayitAraM kaJNcidetyocuruktavanto he bhagavanko no 'smAkaM madhye shreShTho 'bhyadhiko guNairityevaM pR^iShTavantaH /

START ChUp 5,1.8-11

#<sA ha vAg uccakrAma |

#<mano hoccakrAma |

__________


ChUpBh_5,1.8,9,10,11 tathokteShu pitrA prANeShu sA ha vAguccakrAmotkrAntavatI /
sA cotkramya saMvatsaramAtraM proShya svavyApArAnnivR^ittA satI punaH paryetyetarAnprANAnuvAca kathaM kena prakAreNAshakata shaktavanto yUyaM madR^ite mAM vinA jIvituM dhArayitumAtmAnamiti te hocuryathAkalA ityAdi /
akalA mUkA yathA loke 'vadanto vAcA jIvanti /
katham?prANantaH prANena pashyantashcakShuShA shR^iNvantaH shrotreNa dhyAyanto manasaivaM sarvakaraNaceShTAM kurvanta ityarthaH /
evaM vayamajIviShmetyarthaH /
Atmano 'shreShThatAM prANeShu buddhvA pravivesha ha vAkpunaH svavyApAre pravR^ittA babhUvetyarthaH /
samAnamanyaccakShurheccakrAma shrotraM hoccakrAma mano hoccakrAmetyAdi /

START ChUp 5,1.15

#<na vai vAco na cakShUMShi na shrotrANi na manAMsIty AcakShate |
prANA ity evAcakShate |
prANo hy evaitAni sarvANi bhavati || ChUp_5,1.15 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_5,1.15 shruteridaM vaco yuktamidaM vAgAdibhirmukhyaM prANaM pratyabhihitaM yasmAnna vai loke vAco na cakShUMShi na shrotrANi na manAMsIti vAgAdIni karaNAnyAcakShate laukikA Agamaj~nA vA /
kiM tarhi?prANA ityevA'cakShate kathayanti yasmAtprANo hyevaitAni sarvANi vAgAdIni karaNajAtAni bhavatyato mukhyaM prAmaM pratyanurUpameva vAgAdibhiruktamiti prakaraNArthamupasaJNjihIrShati /
nanu kathamidaM yuktaM cetanAvanta iva puruShA ahaMshreShThatAyai vivadanto 'nyonyaM spardheranniti /
na hi cakShurAdInAM vAcaM pratyAkhyAya pratyekaM vadanaM sambhavati /
tathApagamo dehAtpunaH pravesho brahmagamanaM prANastutirvopapadyate /
tatrAgnyAdicetanAvaddevatAdhiShThitatvAdvAgAdInAM cetanAvattvaM tAvatsiddhamAgamataH. tArkikasamayavirodha iti ceddeha ekasminnanekacetanAvattve /
na /
Ishvarasya nimittakAramatvAbhyupagamAt /
ye tAvadIshvaramabhyupagacchanti tArkikAste mana AdikAryakaramAnAmAdhyAtmikAnAM bAhyAnAM ca pR^ithivyAdInAmIshvarAdhiShThitAnAmeva niyamena pravR^ittimicchanti rathAdivat /
na cAsmAbhiragnyAdyAshcetanAvatyo 'pi devatA adhyAtmaM bhoktryo 'bhyupagamyante, kiM tarhi,kAryakaraNavatInAM hi tAsAM prANaikadevatAbhedAnAmadhyAtmAdhibhUtAdhidaivabhedakoTivikalpAnAmadhyakShatAmAtreNa niyanteshvaro 'bhyupagamyate /
sa hyakaraNaH /
"hiraNyagarbhaM janayAmAna pUrvam"ityAdi ca shvetAshvatarIyAH paThanti /
bhoktA karmaphalasambandhI dehe tadvilakShaNo jIva iti vakShyAmaH /
vAgAdInAM ceha saMvAdaH kalpito viduSho 'nvayavyatirekAbhyAM prANashreShThatAnirdhAraNArtham /
yathA loke puruShA anyonyamAtmanaH shreShThatAyai vivadamAnAH kaJNcidguNavisheShAbhij~naM pR^icchanti ko naH shreShTho guNairiti /
tenoktA ekaikashyenAdaH kAryaM sAdhayitumudyacchata yenAdaH kAryaM sAdhyate sa vaH shreShTha ityuktAstathaivodyacchanta Atmano 'nyasya vA shreShThavAM nirdhArayanti /
tatemaM saMvyavahAraM vAgAdiShu kalpitavatI shrutiH /
kathaM nAma vidvAnvAgAdInAmekaikasyAbhAve 'pi jIvanaM dR^iShTaM na tu prANasyeti prANashreShThatAM pratipadyateti /
tathAca shrutiH kauShItakinAm -"jIvati vAgapeto mUkAnhi pasyAmo jIvati cakShurapeto 'ndhAnhi pashyAmo jIvati shrotrApeto badhirAnhi pashyAmo jIvati manopeto bAlAnhi pashyAmo jIvati bAhucchinno jIvatyUrucchinnaH"ityAdyA //15//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi paJNcamAdhyAyasya prathamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 5,2.1

#<sa hovAca kiM me 'nnaM bhaviShyatIti |
yat kiMcid idam A shvabhya A shakunibhya iti hocuH |
tad vA etad anasyAnnam |
ano ha vai nAma pratyakSham |
na ha vA evaMvidi kiMcanAnannaM bhavatIti || ChUp_5,2.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_5,2.1 sa hovAca mukhyaH prANaH kiM me 'nnaM bhaviShyatIti /
mukhyaM prANaM praShTAramiva kalpayitvA vAgAdInprativaktÌniva kalpayantI shrutirAha-yadidaM loke 'nnajAtaM prasiddhamA shvabhiH sahA'shakunibhyaH saha shakunibhiH sarvaprANinAM yadannaM tattavAnnamiti hocurvAgAdaya iti /
prANasya sarvamannaM prANo 'ttA sarvasyAnnasyetyevaM pratipattaye kalpitAkhyAyikArUpAdvyAvR^itya svena shrutirUpeNA'ha-tadvA etadyatkiJNcilloke prANibhirannamadyate 'nasya prANasya tadannaM prANenaiva tadadyata ityarthaH /
sarvaprakAraceShTAvyAptiguNapradarshanArthamana iti prANasya pratyakShaM nAma /
prAdyupasargapUrvatve hi visheShagatireva syAt /
tathAca sarvAnnAnAmatturnAmagrahaNamitIdaM pratyakShaM nAmAna iti sarvAnnAnAmattuH sAkShAdabhidhAnam /
na ha vA evaMvidi yathoktaprANavidi prANo 'hamasmi sarvabhUtasthaH sarvAnnAnAmatteti tasminnevaMvidi ha vai kiJNcana kiJNcidapi prANibhirAdyaM sarvairanannamannAdyaM na bhavati sarvamevaMvidyannaM bhavatItyarthaH /

prANabhUtatvAdviduShaH /
"prANAdvA eSha udeti prANe 'stameti"ityupakramya-"evaMvido ha vA udeti sUrya evaMvidyastameti"iti shrutyantarAt //1 //

START ChUp 5,2.2

#<sa hovAca kiM me vAso bhaviShyatIti |
Apa iti hocuH |
tasmAd vA etad ashiShyantaH purastAc copariShTAc cAdbhiH paridadhati |
lambhuko ha vAso bhavati |
anagno ha bhavati || ChUp_5,2.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_5,2.2 sa hovAca punaH prANaH /
pUrvavadeva kalpanA /
kiM me vAso bhaviShyatItyApa iti hocurvAgAdayaH /
yasmAtprANasya vAsa ApastasmAdvA etadashiShyanto bhoktavantashca brAhmaNA vidvAMsa etatkurvanti /
kim /
adbhirvAsasthAnIyAbhiH purastAdbhojanAtpUrvamupariShTAcca bhojanAdUrdhvaM ca paridadhati paridhAnaM kurvanti mukhyasya prANasya lambhuko sambhanashIlo vAso ha bhavati /
vAsaso labdhaiva bhavatItyarthaH /
anagno ha bhavati /
vAsaso lambhukatvenArthasiddhaivAnagnatetyanagno ha bhavatItyuttarIyavAnbhavatItyetat /
bhokShyamANasya bhuktavatashca yadAcamanaM shuddhyarthaM vij~nAtaM tasminprANasya vAsa iti darshanamAtramiha vidhIyate /
adbhiH paridadhatIti nA'camanAntaram /
yathA laukikaiH prAmibhiradyamAnamannaM prANasyeti darshanamAtraM tadvatkiM me 'nnaM kiM me vAsa ityAdiprashnaprativacanayostulyatvAt /
yadyAcamanamapUrvaM tAdarthyena kriyate tadA kR^imyAdyannamapi prANasya bhakShyatvena vihitaM syAt /
tulyayorvij~nAnArthayoH prasnaprativacanayoH prakaraNasya vij~nAnArthatvAdardhajaratIyo nyAyo na yuktaH kalpayitum /
yattu prasiddhamAcamanaM prAyatyArthaM prANasyAnagnatArthaM ca na bhavatItyucyate na tathA vayamAcamanamubhayArthaM brUmaH /
kiM tarhi prAyatyArthAcamanasAdhanabhUtA ApaH prANasya vAsa iti darshanaM codyata iti brUmaH /
tatrA'camanasyobhayArthatvaprasaN^gadoShacodanAnupapannA /
vAsortha evA'camane taddarshanaM syAditi cet /
na /
vAsoj~nAnArthavAkye vAsorthApUrvAcamanavidhAne tatrAnagnatArthatvadR^iShTividhAne ca vAkyabhedaH Acamanasya tadarthatvamanyArthatvaM ceti /
pramANAbhAvAt //2 //

START ChUp 5,2.3

#<tad dhaitat satyakAmo jAbAlo goshrutaye vaiyAghrapadyAyoktvovAca |

__________


ChUpBh_5,2.3 tadetatprANadarshanaM stUyate /
katham /
taddhaitatprANadarshanaM satyakAmo jAbAlo goshrutaye nAmnA vaiyAghrapadyAya vyAghrapado 'patyaM vaiyAghrapadyastasmai goshrutyAkhyAyoktvovAcAnyadapi vakShyamANaM vacaH /

START ChUp 5,2.4

#<atha yadi mahaj jigamiShet, amAvAsyAyAm dIkShitvA paurNamAsyAM rAtrau sarvauShadhasya mantham dadhimadhunor upamathya jyeShThAya shreShThAya svAhety agnAv Ajyasya hutvA manthe saMpAtam avanayet || ChUp_5,2.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_5,2.4 athAnantaraM yadi mahanmahattvaM jigamiShedgantumicchenmahattvaM prAptuM yadikAmayetetyarthaH /
tasyedaM karma vidhIyate /
mahattve hi sati shrIrupanamate /
shrImato hyarthaprAptaM dhanaM tataH karmAnuShThAnaM tatashca devayAnaM pitR^iyANaM vA panthAnaM pratipatsyata ityetatprayojanamurarIkR^itya mahattvaprepsoridaM karma na viShayopabhogakAmasya /

START ChUp 5,2.5

#<vasiShThAya svAhety agnAv Ajyasya hutvA manthe saMpAtam avanayet |

AyatanAya svAhety agnAv Ajyasya hutvA manthe saMpAtam avanayet || ChUp_5,2.5 ||>#

ChUpBh_5,2.5 samAnamanyat /
vasiShThAya pratiShThAyai saMpada AyatanAya svAheti pratyekaM tathaiva saMpAtamavanayeddhutvA //5 //

START ChUp 5,2.6

#<atha pratisR^ipyAJNjalau mantham AdhAya japati |
amo nAmAsi |
amA hi te sarvam idam |
sa hi jyeShThaH shreShTho rAjAdhipatiH |
sa mA jyaiShThyaM shraiShThyaM rAjyam AdhipatyaM gamayatu |
aham evedaM sarvam asAnIti || ChUp_5,2.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_5,2.6 atha pratisR^ipyAgnerIShadapasR^ipyAJNjalau manthamAdhAya japatImaM mantram /
amo nAmAsyamA hi te /
ama iti prANasya nAma /
annena hi prANaH prANiti deha ityato manthadravyaM prANasyAnnatvAtprANatvena stUyate 'mo nAmAsIti /
kutaH /
yato 'mA saha hi yasmAtte tava prANabhUtasya sarvaM samastaM jagadidamataH /
sa hi prANabhUto mantho jyeShThaH shreShThashca /
ata eva ca rAjA dIptimAnadhipatishcAdhiShThAya pAlayitA sarvasya /
samA mAmapi manthaH prANo jyaiShThyAdiguNapUgamAtmano gamayatvahamevedaM sarvaM jagadasAni bhavani prANavat /
itishabdo mantraparisamAptyarthaH //6 //

START ChUp 5,2.7

#<atha khalv etayarcA paccha AcAmati |

shreShThaM sarvadhAtamam ity AcAmati |

nirNijya kaMsaM camasaM vA pashcAd agneH saMvishati |

__________


ChUpBh_5,2.7 athAnantaraM khalvetayA vakShyamANayarcA pacchaH pAdasha AcAmati bhakShayati, mantrasyaikaikena pAdenaikaikaM grAsaM bhakShayati /
tadbhojanaM savituH sarvasya prasavituH /
prANamAdityaM caikIkR^ityocyate /
Adityasya vR^iNImahe prArthayemahi mantharUpam /
yenAnnena sAvitreNa bhojanenopabhuktena vayaM savitR^isvarUpApannA bhavemetyabhiprAyaH /
devasya savituriti pUrveNa sambandhaH /
shreShThaM prashasyatamaM sarvAnnebhyaH sarvadhAtamaM sarvasya jagato dhArayitR^itamamatishayena vidhAtR^itamamiti vA /
sarvathA bhojanavisheShaNam /
turaM tvaraM tUrNaM shIghramityatat /
bhagasya devasya savituH svarUpamiti sheShaH /
dhImahi cintayemahi vishiShTabhojanena saMskR^itAH shuddhAtmAnaH santa ityabhiprAyaH /
athavA bhagasya shriyaH kAraNaM mahattvaM prAptuM karma kR^itavanto vayaM taddhomahi cintayemahIti sarvaM ca manthalepaM pibati nirNijya prakShAlya kaMsaM kaMsAkAraM camasaM camasAkAraM vaudumbaraM pAtram /
pItvA'camya pashcAdagneH prAkshirAH saMvishati carmaNi vAjine sthaNDile kevalAyAM vA bhUmau /
vAcaMyamo vAgyataH sannityarthaH /
aprasAho na prasahyate nAbhibhUyate stryAdyaniShTasvapnadarshanena yathA tathA saMyatacittaH sannityarthaH /
sa evaMbhUto yadi sriyaM pashyetsvapneShu tadA vidyAtsamR^iddhaM mamedaM karmeti //7 //

ChUpBh_5,3.1 brahmAdistambaparyantAH saMsAragatayo vaktavyA vairAgyahetormumukShUNAmityata AkhyAyikA'rabhyate-shvetaketunamito ha, ityaitihyArthaH /

START ChUp 5,3.2

ChUpBh_5,3.2 taM hovAca yadyanushiShTo 'si vettha yadito 'smAllokAdadhyUrdhvaM yatprajAH prayanti yadgacchanti tatkiM jAnISha ityarthaH /

ChUpBh_5,3.3 vetthA yathAsau lokaH pitR^isambandhI yaM prApya punarAvartante bahubhiH prayadbhirapi yena kAramena na sampUryata iti /

START ChUp 5,3.5-6

#<paJNca mA rAjanyabandhuH prashnAn aprAkShIt |

#<sa ha gautamo rAj~no 'rdham eyAya |

ChUpBh_5,3.5,6 yataH paJNca paJNcasaMkhyAkAnprashnAnrAjanyabandhU rAjAnyA bandhavo 'syeti rAjanyabandhuH svayaM durvR^itta ityarthaH /
aprAkShItpR^iShTavAMsteShAM prashnAnAM naikaJNcanaikamapi nAshakaM na shaktavAnahaM vivaktuM visheSheNArthato nirNetumityarthaH /
sa hovAca pitA yathA mA mAM vatsa tvaM tadA'gatamAtra evaitAnprashnAnavada uktavAnasi teShAM naikaJNcanAshakaM vivaktumiti tathA mAM jAnIhi, tvadIyAj~nAnena liN^gena mama tadviShayamaj~nAnaM jAnIhItyarthaH /
kathaM, yathAhameShAM prashnAnAmekaJNcanaikamapi na veda na jAna iti yathA tvamevAN^gaitAnprashnAnna jAnIShe tathAhamapyetAnna jAna ityarthaH /
ato mayyanyathAbhAvo na kartavyaH /
kuta etadevaM yato na jAne yadyahamimAnprashnAnavediShyaM viditavAnasmi kathaM te tubhyaM priyAya putrAya samAvartanakAle purA nAvakShyaM noktavAnasmItyuktvA sa ha gotrato rAj~no jaivalerardhaM sthAnameyAya gatavAn /
tasmai ha gautamAya prAptAyArhAmarhUNAM cakAra kR^itavAn /
sa ca gautamaH kR^itAtithya uShitvA paredyuH prAtaHkAle sabhAge sabhAM gate rAj~nyudeyAya /
bhajanaM bhAgaH pUjA sevA saha bhAgena vartamAno vA sabhAgaH pUjyamAno 'nyaiH svayaM gautama udeyAya rAjAnamudgatavAn /
taM hovAca gautamaM rAjA mAnuShasya bhagavangautama manuShyasambandhino vittasya grAmAdervaraM varaNIyaM kAmaM vR^iNIthAH prArthayethAH /
sa hovAca gautamastavaiva tiShThatu rAjanmAnuShaM vittam /
yAmeva kumArasya mama putrasyAnte samIpe vAcaM paJNcaprashnalakShaNAmabhAShathA uktavAnasi tAmeva vAcaM me mahyaM brUhi kathayetyukto gautamena rAjA sa ha kR^icchrI duHkhI babhUva /
kathaM tvidamiti //5-6 //

START ChUp 5,3.7

#<taM ha ciraM vasety Aj~nApayAM cakAra |

ChUpBh_5,3.7 sa ha kR^icchrIbhUto 'pratyAkhyeyaM brAhmaNaM manvAno nyAyena vidyA vaktavyeti matvA taM ha gautamaM ciraM dIrghakAlaM vasetyevamAj~nApayAJNcakArA'j~naptavAn /
yatpUrvaM pratyAkhyAtavAnrAjA vidyAM yacca pashcAcciraM vasetyAj~naptavAn, tannimittaM brAhmamaM kShamApayati hetuvacanoktyA-taM hovAca rAjA sarvavidyo brahmaNo 'pi sanyathA yena prakAreNa mA mAM he gautamAvadastvaM tAmeva vidyAlakShaNAM vAcaM me brUhItyaj~nAnAttena tvaM jAnIhi /
tatrAsti vaktavyaM yathA yena prakAreNeyaM vidyA prAktvatto brAhmaNAnna gacchati na gatavatI, na ca brAhmaNA anayA vidyayAnushAsitavantaH, tathaitatprasiddhaM loke yatastasmAdu purA pUrvaM sarveShu lokeShu kShattrasyaiva kShattrajAterevAnayA vidyayA prashAsanaM prashAstR^itvaM shiShyAmAmabhUdbabhUva /
kShattriyaparamparayaiveyaM vidyatAvantaM kAlamAgatA /

ato mayA yaduktaM tatkShantumarhasItyuktvA tasmai hovAca vidyAM rAjA //7//

ChUpBh_5,4.1 paJNcamyAmAhutAvApa ityayaM prashnaH prAthamyenApAkriyate /

teShAM cApAkaraNamuktaM tatraiva-"te vA ete AhutI hute utkrAmataste antarikShamAvishataste antarikShamevA'havanIyaM kurvAte vAyuM samidhaM marIcIreva shuklAmAhutiM te antarikShaM tarpayataste tata utkrAmata ityAdyevameva pUrvavaddivaM tarpayataste tata Avartete /
imAmAvishya tarpayitvA puruShamAvishataH /
tataH sriyamAvishya lokaM pratyutthAyA bhavati"iti /

iha tu taM kAryArambhamagni hotrApUrvavipariNAmalakShaNaM paJNcadhA pravibhajyAgnitvenopAsanamuttaramArgapratipattisAdhanaM vidhitsannAha-asau vAva loko gautamAgnirityAdi /
iha sAyaMprAtaragnihotrAhutI hute paya AdisAdhane shraddhApuraHsare AhavanIyAgnisamiddhUmArciraN^gAravisphuliN^gabhAvite kartrAdikArakabhAvite cAntarikShakrameNotkramya dyulokaM pravishantyau sUkShmabhUte apsamavAyitvAdapshabdavAcye shraddhAhetutvAcca shraddhAshabdavAcye tayoradhikaraNo 'gniranyacca tatsambandhaM samidAdItyucyate /
yA cAsAvagnyAdibhAvanA'hutyoH sApi tathaiva nirdishyate /
asau vAva loko 'gnirhe gautama yathAgnihotrAdhikaraNamAhavanIya iha /
tasyAgnerghulokAkhyasyA'ditya eva samittena hIddho 'sau loko dIpyate /
ataH samindhanAtsamidAdityaH /
rashmayo dhUmastadutthAnAt, samidho hi dhUma uttiShThati /

ahaHprashame 'bhivyakteH /

tatrApAmAhutisamavAyitvAtprAdhAnyavivakShA'paH paJNcamyAmAhutau puruShavacaso bhavantIti /
na tvApa eva kevalAH somAdikAryamArabhante /
na cA'po 'trivR^itkR^itAH santIti /
trivR^itkR^itatve 'pi visheShasaMj~nAlAbho dR^iShTaH pR^ithivIyamimA Apo 'yamagnirityanyatamabAhulyanimittaH /
tasmAtsamuditAnyeva bhUtAnyabbAhulyAtkarmasamavAyIni somAdikAryArambhakANyApa ityucyante /
dR^ishyate ca dravabAhulyaM somavR^iShTyannaretodeheShu /
bahudravaM ca sharIraM yadyapi pArthivam /
tatra paJNcamyAmAhutau hutAyAM retorUpA Apo garbhIbhUtAH //2//

START ChUp 5,9.1

#<iti tu paJNcamyAm AhutAv ApaH puruShavacaso bhavantIti |

__________


ChUpBh_5,9.1 iti tvevaM tu paJNcamyAmAhutAvApaH puruShavacaso bhavantIti vyAkhyAta ekaH prashnaH /

kaShTaM hi mAtuH kukShau mUtrapurIShavAtapittashleShmAdipUrNe tadanuliptasya garbhasyolbAshucipaTAvR^itasya lohitareto 'shucibIjasya mAturashitapItarasAnupraveshena vivardhamAnasya niruddhashaktibalavIryatejaHpraj~nAceShTasya shayanam /

ChUpBh_5,9.2 sa evaM jAto yAvadAyuShaM punaH punarghaTIyantravadgamanAgamanAya karma kurvankulAlacakravadvA tiryagbhramaNAya yAvatkarmaNopAttamAyustAvajjIvati /

START ChUp 5,10.1-2

#<tad ya itthaM viduH |

ChUpBh_5,10.1,2 vettha yadito 'dhi prajAH prayantItyayaM prashnaH pratyupasthito 'pAkartavyatayA /
tattatra lokaM pratyutthitAnAmadhikR^itAnAM gR^ihamedhinAM ya itthamevaM yathoktaM paJNcAgnidarshanaM dyulokAdyagnibhyo vayaM krameNa jAtA agnisvarUpAH paJNcAgnyAtmAna ityevaM vidurjAnIyuH /

na /
gR^ihasthAnpratyarthavattvAt /
ye gR^ihasthA anitthaMvidasteShAM svabhAvato dakShiNo dhUmAdiH panthAH prasiddhasteShAM yaM itthaM viduH saguNaM vAnyadbrahma viduH /
"atha yadu caivAsmi¤shavyaM kurvanti yadi nArciShameva"iti liN^gAduttareNa te gacchanti /
nanUrdhvaretasAM gR^ihasthAnAM ca samAna Ashramitva UrdhvaretasAmevottareNa pathA gamanaM na gR^ihasthAnAmiti na yuktamagnihotrAdivaidikakarmabAhulye ca sati /
naiSha doShaH /
apUtA hi te /
shatrumitrasaMyoganimittaM hi teShAM rAgadveShau /

hiMsAnR^itamAyAbrahmacaryAdi ca bahvashuddhikAraNamaparihAryaM teShAm /
ato 'pUtAH /
apUtatvAnnottareNa pathA gamanam /
hiMsAnR^itamAyAbrahmacaryAdiparihArAcca shuddhAtmAno hItare shatrumitrarAgadveShAdiparihArAcca virajasasteShAM yukta uttaraH panthAH /
tathAca paurANikAH - "ye prajAmIShire 'dhIrAste shmashAnAni bhejire /
ye prajAM neShire dhIrAste 'mR^itatvaM hi bhejire" /
ityAhuH /
itthaMvidAM gR^ihasthAnAmaraNyavAsinAM ca samAnamArgatve 'mR^itatvaphale ca satyaraNyavAsinAM vidyAnarthakyaM prAptam /
tathAca shrutivirodhaH /
"na tatra dakShiNA yanti nAvidvAMsastapasvinaH"iti /
"sa enamavidito na bhunakti"iti ca viruddham /
na /
AbhUtasaMplavasthAnasyAmR^itatvena vivakShitatvAt /

yaccA'tyantikamamR^itatvaM tadapekShayA"na tatra dakShiNA yanti" "sa enamavidito na bhunaktI"-tyAdyAH shrutaya ityato na virodhaH /
"na ca punarAvartanta"iti"maM mAnavamAvartaM nA'vartanta"ityAdishrutivirodha iti cet /
na /
imaM mAnavamiti visheShaNAtteShAmiha na punarAvR^ittirastIti ca /
yadi hyekAntenaiva nA'varterannimaM mAnavamiheti ca visheShaNamanarthakaM syAt /
imamihetyAkR^itimAtramucyata iti cet /
na /
anAvR^ittishabdenaiva nityAnAvR^ittyarthasya pratItatvAdAkR^itikalpanAnarthikA /
ata imamiheti ca visheShaNArthavattvAyAnyatrA'vR^ittiH kalpanIyA /
na ca sadekamevAdvitIyamityevaMpratyayavatAM mUrdhanyayA nADyArcirAdimArgeNa gamanam /
"brahmaiva sanbrahmApyati" /
"tasmAttatsarvamabhavat" /
"na tasya prANA utkrAmanti /
atraiva samavanIyante"ityAdishrutishatebhyaH /
nanu tasmAjjIvAduccikramiShoH prANA notkrAmanti sahaiva gacchantItyayamarthaH kalpyata iti cet /
na /
atraiva samavanIyanta iti visheShaNAnarthakyAt /
sarve prANA anUtkrAmantIti ca prANairgamanasya prAptatvAt /
tasmAdutkrAmantItyanAshaN^kaivaiShA /
yadApi mokShasya saMsAragativailakShaNyAtprANAnAM jIvena sahAgamAshN^kya tasmAnnotkrAmantItyucyate tadApyatraiva samavanIyanta iti visheShaNamanarthakaM syAt /
na ca prANairviyuktasya gatirupapadyate jIvatvaM vA /
sarvagatatvAtsadAtmano niravayavatvAtprANasambandhamAtrameva hyagnivisphuliN^gavajjIvatvabhedakAraNamityatastadviyoge jIvatvaM gatirvA na shakyA parikalpayituM shrutayashcetpramANam /
na sato 'NuravayavaH sphuTito jIvAkhyaH sadrUpaM chidrIkurvangacchatIti shakyaM kalpayitum /

START ChUp 5,10.3

#<atha ya ime grAma iShTApUrte dattam ity upAsate |

ChUpBh_5,10.4 mAsebhyaH pitR^ilokaM pitR^ilokAdAkAshamAkAshAccandramasam /

ChUpBh_5,10.5 yAvattadupabhoganimittasya karmaNaH kShayaH sampatanti yeneti sampAtaH karmaNaH kShayo yAvatsampAtaM yAvatkarmaNaH kShaya ityarthaH /

yadi hi sarvAH pUrvajanmAnubhavavAsanA upamR^idyeranmarkaTajanmanimittena karmaNA markaTajanmanyArabdhe markaTasya jAtamAtrasya mAtuH shAkhAyAH shAkhAntaragamane mAturudarasaMlagnatvAdikaushalaM na prApnoti /
iha janmanyanabhyastatvAt /
na cAtItAnantarajanmani markaTatvamevA'sIttasyeti shakyaM vaktum /

tasmAdvAsanAvannAsheShakarmopamarda iti sheShakarmasambhavaH /
yata evaM tasmAccheSheNopabhuktAtkarmaNaH saMsAra upapadyata iti na kashcidvirodhaH /
ko 'sAvadhvA yaM prati nivartanta ityucyate /
yathetaM yathAgataM nivartante /

START ChUp 5,10.6

#<abhraM bhUtvA megho bhavati |

ChUpBh_5,10.6 abhraM bhUtvA tataH secanasamartho megho bhavati megho bhUtvonnateShu pradesheShvatha pravarShati /

kadAcitkAkatAlIyavR^ittyA retaHsigbhirbhakShyante yadA tadA retaH sigbhAvaM gatAnAM karmaNo vR^ittilAbhaH /
katham /
yo yo hyannamattyanushayibhiH saMshliShTaM retaH siJNcatyR^itukAle yoShiti tadbhUya eva tadAkR^itireva bhavati /
tadavayavAkR^itibhUyastvaM bhUya ityucyate retorUpeNa yoShito garbhashaye 'ntaH praviShTo 'nushayI /
retaso retaHsigAkR^itibhAvitatvAt /
"sarvebhyo 'N^gebhyastejaH saMbhUtam"iti hi shrutyantarAt /
ato retaHsigAkR^itireva bhavatItyarthaH /
tathA hi /
puruShAtpuruSho jAyate gorgavAkR^itireva na jAtyantarAkR^itistasmAdyuktaM tadbhUya eva bhavatIti /
ye tvanye 'nushayibhyashcandramaNDalamanAruhyehaiva pApakarmabhirghoraivrIhiyavAdibhAvaM pratipadyante punarmanuShyAdibhAvaM teShAM nAnushayinAmiva durniShprataram /
kasmAt /
karmaNA hi tairvrIhiyavAdideha upAtta iti tadupabhoganimittakShaye vrIhyAdistambadehavinAshe yathAkarmArjitaM dehAntaraM navaM navaM jalUkAvatsaMkramante savij~nAnA eva"savij~nAno bhavati savij~nAnamevAnvavakrAmati"iti shrutyantarAt /
yadyapyusaMhR^itakaraNAH santo dehAntaraM gacchanti tathApi svapnavaddehAntaraprAptinimittakarmodbhAvitavAsanAj~nAnena savij~nAnA eva dehAntaraM gacchanti /
shrutiprAmANyAt /
tathArcirAdinA dhUmAdinA ca gamanaM svapta ivodbhUtavij~nAnena /
labdhavR^ittikarmanimittatvAdgamanasya /
na tathAnushayinAM vrIhyAdibhAvena jAtAnAM savij~nAnameva retaH-sigyoShiddehasambandha upapadyate /
na hi vrIhyAdilavanakaNDanapeShaNAdau ca savij~nAnAnAM sthitirasti /
nanu candramaNDalAdapyavarohatAM dehAntaragamanasya tulyatvAjjalUkAvatsavij~nAnataiva yuktA /
tathA sati ghoro narakAnubhava iShTApUrtAdikAriNAM candramaNDalAdArabhya prApto yAvadbrAhmaNAdijanma /
tathA ca satyanarthAyaiveShTApUrtAdyupAsanaM vihitaM syAt /
shruteshcAprAmANyaM prAptaM vaidikAnAM karmaNAmanarthAnubandhitvAt /
na, vR^ikShArohaNapatanavadvisheShasambhavAt /
dehAddehAntaraM pratipitsoH karmaNo labdhavR^ittitvAkarmaNodbhAvitena vij~nAnena savij~nAnatvaM yuktam /
vR^ikShAgramArohata iva phalaM jighR^ikShoH /
tathArcirAdinA gacchatAM savij~nAnatvaM bhavet /
dhUmAdinA ca candramaNDalamArurukShatAm /
na tathA candramaNDalAdavarurukShatAM vR^ikShAgrAdiva patatAM sacetanatvam /
yathA ca mudgarAdyabhihatAnAM tadabhighAtavedanAnimittasaMmUrchitapratibaddhakaraNAnAM svadehenaiva deshAddeshAntaraM nIyamAnAnAM vij~nAnashUnyatA dR^iShTA tathA candramaNDalAnmAnuShAdidehAntaraM pratyavarurukShatAM svargabhoganimittakarmakShayAnmR^iditAbdehAnAM pratibaddhakaraNAnAm /
ataste 'parityaktadehabIjabhUtAbhiradbhirmUrchitA ivA'kAshAdikrameNemAmavaruhya karmanimittajAtisthAvaradehaiH saMshliShyante pratibaddhakaraNatayAnudbhUtavij~nAnA eva /
tathA lavanakaNDanapeShaNasaMskArabhakShaNarasAdipariNAmaretaHsekakAleShu mUrchitavadeva /
dehAntarArambhakasya karmaNo 'labdhavR^ittitvAt /
dehabIjabhUtApsambandhAparityAgenaiva sarvAsvavasthAsu vartanta iti jalUkAvaccetanAvattvaM na virudhyate /
antarAle tvavij~nAnaM mUrchitavadevetyadoShaH /
na ca vaidikAnAM karmaNAM hiMsAyuktatvenobhayahetutvaM shakyamanumAtum /
hiMsAyAH shAstracoditatvAt /
"ahiMsansarvabhUtAnyanyatra tIrthebhyaH"iti shruteH shAstracoditAyA hiMsAyA nAdharmahetutvamabhyupagamyate /
abhyupagate 'pyadharmahetutve mantrairviShAdivattadapanayopapatterna duHkhakAryArambhakatvopapattirvaidikAnAM karmaNAM mantreNeva viShabhakShaNasyeti //6 //

START ChUp 5,10.7

START ChUp 5,10.8

#<athaitayoH pathor na katareNacana tAnImAni kShudrANy asakR^idAvartIni bhUtAni bhavanti jAyasva mriyasveti |

START ChUp 5,11.1

ChUpBh_5,14.1 atha hovAcendradyumnaM bhAllaveyaM vaiyAghrapadya kaM tvamAtmAnamupAHsa ityAdi samAnam /

START ChUp 5,18.1

#<tAn hovAca |

ChUpBh_5,18.1 tAnyathoktavaishvAnaradarshanavato hovAca /

START ChUp 6,1.1

#<shvetaketur hAruNeya Asa |
taM ha pitovAca shvetaketo vasa brahmacaryam |
na vai somyAsmat kulIno 'nanUcya brahmabandhur iva bhavatIti || ChUp_6,1.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,1.1
shvetaketurhA'ruNeya AsetyAdyadhyAyasambandhaH /
sarvaM khalvidaM brahma tajjalAnityuktaM kathaM tasmAjjagadidaM jAyate tasminneva ca lIyate 'niti ca tenaivetyetadvaktavyam /
anantaraM caikasminbhukte viduShi sarvaM jagattR^iptaM bhavatItyuktaM tadekatve satyAtmanaH sarvabhUtasthasyopapadyate nA'tmabhede /
kathaM ca tadekatvamiti tadartho 'yaM ShaShTho 'dhyAya Arabhyate /
pitAputrAkhyAyikA vidyAyAH sAriShThatvapradarshanArthA /
shvetaketuriti nAmato hetyaitihyArthaH AruNeyo 'ruNasya pautra Asa babhUva /
taM putraM hA'ruNiH pitA yogyaM vidyAbhAjanaM manvAnastasyopanayanakAlAtyayaM ca pashyannuvAca he shvetaketo 'nurUpaM guruM kulasya no gatvA vasa brahmacaryam /
na caitadyuktaM yadasmatkulIno he somyAnanUcyAnadhItya brahmabandhuriva bhavatIti brAhmaNAnbandhUnvyapadishati na svayaM brAhmaNavR^itta iti //1 //

START ChUp 6,1.2

#<sa ha dvAdashavarSha upetya caturviMshativarShaH sarvAn vedAn adhItya mahAmanA anUcAnamAnI stabdha eyAya |
taM ha pitovAca || ChUp_6,1.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,1.2 tasyAtaH pravAso 'numIyate pituH /
yena svayaM guNavAnsanputraM nopaneShyati /
sa pitroktaH shvetaketurha dvAdashavarShaH sannupetyA'cAryaM yAvaccatuviMshativarSho babhUva tAvatsarvAnvedAMshcaturo 'pyadhItya tadarthaM ca buddhvA mahAmanA mahadgambhIraM mano yasyAsamamAtmAnamanyairmanyamAnaM mano yasya so 'yaM mahAmanAH anUcAnamAnyanUcAnamAtmAnaM manyata ityevaMshIlo yaH so 'nUcAnamAnI stabdho 'praNatasvabhAva eyAya gR^iham /
tamevaMbhUtaM hA'tmano 'nanurUpashIlaM stabdhaM mAninaM putraM dR^iShTvA pitovAca saddharmAvatAracikIrShayA /
shvetaketo yannivadaM mahAmanA anUcAnamAnI stabdhashcAsi kaste 'tishayaH prApta upAdhyAyAt?utApi tamAdeshamAdishyata ityAdeshaH kevalashAsrAcAryopadeshagamyamityetadyena vA paraM brahmA'dishyate sa AdeshastamaprAkShyaH pR^iShTavAnasyAcAryam //2 //

START ChUp 6,1.3

#<shvetaketo yan nu somyedaM mahAmanA anUcAnamAnI stabdho 'si |
uta tam Adesham aprAkShyaH yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavaty amataM matam avij~nAtaM vij~nAtam iti |
kathaM nu bhagavaH sa Adesho bhavatIti || ChUp_6,1.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,1.3 tamAdeshaM vishinaShTi-yenA'deshena shrutenAshrutamapyanyacchataM bhavatyamataM matamatarkitaM tarkitaM bhavatyavij~nAnaM vij~nAtamanishcitaM nishcitaM bhavatIti /
sarvAnapi vedAnadhAtya sarvaM cAnyadvedyamadhigamyApyakR^itArtha eva bhavati yAvadAtmatattvaM na jAnAtItyAkhyAyikAto 'vagamyate /
tadetadadbhutaM shrutvA'ha-kathaM nvetadaprasiddhamanyavij~nAnenAnyadvij~nAtaM bhavatItyevaM manvAnaH pR^icchati kathaM nu kena prakAreNa he bhagavaH sa Adesho bhavatIti //3 //

START ChUp 6,1.4

#<yathA somyaikena mR^itpiNDena sarvaM mR^inmayaM vij~nAtaM syAt |
vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittikety eva satyam || ChUp_6,1.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,1.4 yathA sa Adesho bhavati tacchR^iNu he somya /
yathA loka ekena mR^itpiNDena ghaTasharAvAdikAraNabhUtena vij~nAtena sarvamanyadvikArajAtaM mR^inmayaM mR^idvikArajAtaM vij~nAtaM syAt /
kathaM mR^itpiNDe kAraNe vij~nAte kAryamanyadvij~nAtaM syAt /
naiSha doShaH /
kAraNenAnanyatvAtkAryasya /
yanmanyase 'nyasminvij~nAte 'nyanna j~nAyata iti /
satyamevaM syAt /
yadyanyatkAraNAtkAryaM syAnna tvevamanyatkAraNAtkAryam /
kathaM tarhidaM loka idaM kAraNamayasya vikAra iti /
shR^iNu /
vAcA'rambhaNaM vAgArambhaNaM vAgAlambanamityetat /
ko 'sau vikAro nAmadheyaM nAmaiva nAmadheyaM svArthe dheyapratyayaH /
vAgAlambanamAtraM nAmaiva kevalaM na vikAro nAma vastvasti paramArthato mR^ittiketyeva tu mR^ittiketyeva tu mR^ittikaiva satyaM vastvasti //4 //

#<sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam |

ChUpBh_6,2.1 sadeva sadityastitAmAtraM vastu sUkShmaM nirvisheShaM sarvagatamekaM niraJNjanaM niravayavaM vij~nAnaM yadavagamyate sarvavedAntebhyaH /

naiSha doShaH /

START ChUp 6,2.2

#<kutas tu khalu somyaivaM syAd iti hovAca |

ChUpBh_6,2.2 tadetadviparItagrahaNaM mahAvainAshikapakShaM darshayitvA pratiShedhati-kutastu pramANAtkhalu he somyaivaM syAdasataH sajjAyatetyevaM kuto bhavenna kutashcitpramANAdevaM sambhavatItyarthaH /
yadapi bIjopamarde 'N^kuro jAyamAno dR^iShTo 'bhAvadeveti tadapyabhyupagamaviruddhaM teShAm /
katham /
ye tAvadbIjAvayavA bIjasaMsthAnavishiShTAste 'N^kure 'pyanuvartanta eva na teShAmupamarde 'N^kurajanmani /

atha saMvR^ityAbhyupagataM bIjasaMsthAnarUpamupamR^idyata iti cet /

avayavA apyupamR^idyanta iti cet /
na /
tadavayaveShu tulyatvAt /
yathA vainAshikAnAM bIjasaMsthAnarUpo 'vayavI nAsti tathAvayavA apIti teShAmapyupamardAnupapattiH /
bIjAvayavAnAmapi sUkShmAvayavAstadavayavAnAmapyanye sUkShmatarAvayavA ityevaM prasaN^gasyAnivR^itteH sarvatropamardAnupapattiH /
sadbuddhyanuvR^itteH sattvAnivR^ittishceti sadvAdinAM sata eva sadutpattiH setsyati /
na tvasadvAdinAM dR^iShTAnto 'styasataH sadutpatteH /
mR^itpiNDAdghaTotpattirdR^ishyate sadvAdinAM tadbhAve bhAvAttadabhAve cAbhAvAt /
yadyabhAvAdeva ghaTa utpadyeta ghaTArthinA mR^itpiNDo nopAdIyeta /
abhAvashabdabuddhyanuvR^ittishca ghaTAdau prasajyeta /
na tvetadastyato nAsataH sadutpattiH /
yadapyAhurmR^idbuddhirghaTabuddhernimittamiti mR^idbuddhirghaTabuddheH kAraNamucyate na tu paramArthata eva mR^idghaTo vAstIti tadapi mR^idbuddhirvidyamAnA vidyamAnAyA eva ghaTabuddheH kAraNamiti nAsataH sadutpattiH /
mR^idghaTabuddhyornimittanaimittikatayA'nantaryamAtraM na tu kAryakAraNatvamiti cet /
na /
buddhInAM nairantarye gamyamAne vainAshikAnAM bahirdR^iShTAntAbhAvAt /
ataH kutastu khalu somyaivaM syAditi hovAca kathaM kena prakAreNAsataH sajjAyeteti /
asataH sadutpattau na kashcidapi dR^iShTAntaprakAro 'stItyabhiprAyaH /
evamasadvAdipakShamunmadhyopasaMharati sattveva somyedamagra AsIditi svapakShasiddhim /
nanu sadvAdino 'pi sataH sadutpadyata iti naiva dR^iShTAnto 'sti /
ghaTAdghaTAntarotpattyadarshanAt /
satyamevaM na sataH sadantaramutpadyate kiM tarhi sadeva saMsthAnAntareNAvatiShThate /
yathA sarpaH kuNDalI bhavati /
yathA ca mR^iccUrNapiNDaghaTakapAlAdiprabhedaiH /
yadyevaM sadeva sarvaprakAravasthaM kataM prAgutpatteridamAsIditi /
ucyate /
nanu na shrutaM tvayA sadevetyava dhAraNamidaMshabdavAcyasya kAryasya /
prAptaM tarhi prAgutpatterasadevA'sInnedaMshabdavAcyamidAnImidaM jAtamiti /
na /
sata evedaMshabdabuddhiviShayatayAvasthAnAdyathA mR^ideva piNDaghaTAdishabdabuddhiviShayatvenAvatiShThate tadvat /
nanu yathA mR^idvastvevaM piNDaghaTAdyapi tadvatsadbuddheranyabuddhiviShayatvAtkAryasya sato 'nyadvastvantaraM syAtkAryajAtaM yathAshvAdgauH /
na /
piNDaghaTAdInAmitaretaravyabhicAre 'pi mR^ittvAvyabhicArAt /
yadyapi ghaTaH piNDaM vyabhicarati piNDashca ghaTaM tathApi mR^ittavaM na vyabhicaratastasmAnmR^inmAtraM piNDaghaTau /
(vyabhicarati tvashvaM gaurashvo vA gAm) /
tasmAnmR^idAdisaMsthAnamAtraM ghaTAdayaH /
evaM satsaMsthAnamAtramidaM sarvamiti yuktaM prAgutpatteH /

vAcArambhaNamAtratvAdvikArasaMsthAnamAtrasya /
nanu niravayavaM sat"niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntaM niravadyaM niraJNjanaM" "divyo hyamUrtaH puruShaH sabAhyAbhyantaro hyaja"ityAdishrutibhyo niravayavasya sataH kathaM vikArasaMsthAnamupapadyate /
naiSha doShaH /
rajjvAdyavayavebhyaH sarpAdisaMsthAnavadbuddhipArikalpitebhyaH sadavayavebyo vikArasaMsthAnopapatteH /
vAcA'rambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyamevaM sadeva satyamiti shruteH /
ekamevAdvitIyaM paramArthata idaMbuddhikAle 'pi //2 //

#<tad aikShata |

ChUpBh_6,2.3 tatsadaikShatekShAM darshanaM kR^itavat /
atashca na pradhAnaM sAMkhyaparikalpitaM jagatkAraNam /

asadeva tarhi sarvaM yadgR^ihyate rajjuriva sarpAdyAkareNa /

naiSha doShaH /
AkAshavAyusargAnantaraM tatsattejo 'sR^ijatetikalpanopapatteH /

mR^idAdidR^iShTAntAt /
athavA trivR^itkaraNasya vivakShitatvAttejobannAnAmeva sR^iShTimAcaShTe /
teja iti prasiddhaM loke dagdhR^i paktR^i prakAshakaM rohitaM ceti /
tatsatsR^iShTaM teja aikShata tejorUpasaMsthitaM sadaikShatetyarthaH /
bahu syAM prajAyeyeti pUrvavat /
tadapo 'sR^ijata /
Apo dravAH snigdhAH syandinyaH shuklAshceti prasiddhA loke /

6.2.4 #<tA Apa aikShanta bahvayaH syAma prajAyemahIti tA annamasR^ijanta tasmAdyatra># #<kva ca varShati tadeva bhUyiShThamannaM bhavatyadbhya eva tadadhyannAdyaM jAyate //4//>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,2.4 tA Apa aikShanta pUrvavadevAbAkArasaMsthitaM sadaikShatetyarthaH /
bahvayaH prabhUtAH syAma bhavema prajAyemahi utpadyemahoti /
tA annamasR^ijanta pR^ithivIlakShaNam /
pArthivaM hyannaM yasmAdapkAryamannaM tasmAdyatra kva ca varShati deshe tattatraiva bhUyiShThaM prabUtamannaM bhavati /
ato 'dbhya eva tadannAdyamadhijAyate /
tA annamasR^ijanteti pR^ithivyuktA pUrvamiha tu dR^iShTAnte 'nnaM ca tadAdyaM ceti visheShaNAdvrIhiyavAdyA ucyante /
annaM ca guru sthiraM dhAraNaM kR^iShNaM ca rUpataH prasiddham /
nanu tejaH prabhR^itiShvIkShaNaM na gamyate hiMsAdipratiShedhAbhAvAttrAsAdikAryAnupalambhAcca tatra kathaM tatteja aikShatetyAdi /
neSha doShaH /
IkShitR^ikAraNapariNAmatvAttejaH prabhR^itInAM sata ivekShiturniyatakramavishiShTakAryotpAdakatvAt tejaH prabhR^itIkShata ivekShata ityucyate bhUtam /
nanu sato 'pyupacaritamevekShitR^itvam /
na /
sadIkShaNasya kevalashabdagamyatvAnna shakyamupacaritaM kalpayitum /
tejaH prabhR^itInAM tvanumIyate mukhyekShaNAbhAva iti yuktamupacaritaM kalpayitum /
nanu sato 'pi mR^idvatkAraNatvAdacetanatvaM shakyamanumAtum /
ataH pradhAnasyaivAcetanasya satashcetanArthatvAnniyatakAlakramavishiShTakAryotpAdakatvAccaikShatevaikShateti shakyamanumAtumupacaritamevekShaNam /
dR^iShTashca loke 'cetane cetanavadupacAraH /
yathA kUlaM pipatiShatIti tadvatsato 'pi syAt /
na /
tatsatyaM sa Atmeti tasminnAtmopadeshAt /
Atmopadesho 'pyupacarita iti cedyathA mamA'tmA bhadrasena iti AtmanaH sarvArthakAriNyanAtmanyAtmopacArastadvat /
na /
sadasmIti satsatyAbhisandhasya"tasya tAvadeva ciram" iti mokShopadeshAt /
so 'pyupacAra iti cet /
pradhAnAtmAbhisandhasya mokShasAmIpyaM vartata iti mokShopadesho 'pyupacarita eva /
yathA loke grAmaM gantuM prasthitaH prAptavAnahaM grAmamiti brUyAt tvarApekShayA tadvat /
na /
yena vij~nAtenAvij~nAtaM vij~nAtaM bhavatItyupakramAt /
satyetasminvij~nAte sarvaM vij~nAtaM bhavati tadananyatvAtsarvasyAdvitIyavacanAcca /
na cAnyadvij~nAtavyamavashiShTaM shrAvitaM shrutyAnumeyaM vA liN^gato 'sti yena mokShopadesha upacaritaH syAt /
sarvasya ca prapAThakArthasyopacaritatvaparikalpanAyAM vR^ithA shramaH parikalpayituH syAtpuruShArthasAdhanavij~nAnasya tarkeNaivAdhigatatvAttasya /
tasmAdvedaprAmANyAnna shrutArthaparityAgaH /
atashcetanAvatkAraNaM jagata iti siddham //4//

START ChUp 6,3.1

#<teShAM khalv eShAM bhUtAnAM trINy eva bIjAni bhavanty ANDajaM jIvajam udbhijjam iti || ChUp_6,3.1 ||>#

ChUpBh_6,3.1 teShAM jIvAviShTAnAM khalveShAM pakShyAdInAM bhUtAnAmeShAmiti pratyakShanirdeshAnna tu tejaHprabhR^itInAM teShAM trivR^itkaraNasya vakShyamANatvAdasati trivR^itkarame pratyakShanirdeshAnupapattiH /

START ChUp 6,3.2

#<seyaM devataikShata |
hantAham imAs tisro devatA anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANIti || ChUp_6,3.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,3.2 seyaM prakR^itA sadAkhyA tejobannayonirdevatoktaikShatekShitavatI yathApUrvaM bahu syAmiti /
tadeva bahubhavanaM prayojanaM nAdyApi nirvR^ittamityata IkShAM punaH kR^itavatI bahubhavanameva prayojanamurarIkR^itya /
katham /
hantedAnImahamimA yathoktAsteja AdyAstisro devatA, anena jIveneti, svabuddhisthaM pUrvasR^iShTyanubhUtaprANadhArANamAtmAnameva smarantyAhAnena jIvenA'tmaneti /
prANadhAraNakartrA'tmaneti vacanAtsvAtmano 'vyatiriktena caitanyasvarUpatayAvishiShTenetyetaddarshayati /
anupravishya, tejobannabhUtamAtrAsaMsargeNa labdhavisheShavij~nAnA satI, nAma ca rUpaM ca nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi vispaShTamAkaravA"NyasaunAmAyamidaMrUpa"iti vyAkuryAmityarthaH /
nanu na yuktamidamasaMsAriNyAH sarvaj~nAyA devatAyA buddhipUrvakamanekashatasahasrAnarthAshrayaM dehamanupravishya duHkhamanubhaviShyAmIti saN^kalpanamanupraveshashca svAtantrye sati /

satyamevaM na yuktaM syAdyadi svenaivAvikR^itena rUpeNAnupravisheyaM duHkhamanubhaveyamiti ca saN^kalpitavatI na tvevam /
kathaM tarhi /
anena jIvenA'tmanAnupravishyeti vacanAt /
jIvo hi nAma devatAyA AbhAsamAtram /
buddhyAdibhUtamAtrAsaMsargajanita Adarsha iva praviShTaH puruShapratibimbo jalAdiShviva ca sUryAdInAm /
acintyAnantashaktimatyA devatAyA buddhyAdisambandhashcaitanyAbhAso devatAsvarUpavivekAgrahaNanimittaH sukhI duHkhI mUDha ityAdyanekavikalpapratyayahetuH /
chAyAmAtreNa jIvarUpeNAnupraviShTatvAddevatA na daihikaiH svataH sukha duHkhAdibhiH sambadhyate /
yathA puruShAdityAdaya AdarshodakAdiShu cchAyAmAtreNAnupraviShTA AdarshodakadidoShainaM sambadhyante tadvaddevatApi /
sUryo yathA sarvalokasya cakShurna lipyate cAkShuShairbAhyadoShaiH /
ekastathA sarvabhUtAntarAtmA na lipyate lokaduHkhena bAhyaH //
"AkAshavatsarvagatashca nityaH"iti ca vAjasaneyake /
nanu cchAyAmAtrashcejjIvo mR^iShaiva prAptastayA paralokehalokAdi ca tasya /
naiSha doShaH /
sadAtmanA satyatvAbhyupagamAt /
sarvaM ca nAmarUpAdi sadAtmanaiva satyaM vikArajAtaM svastvanR^itameva /
vAcA'rambhaNa vikAro nAmadheyamityukkatvAt /
tathA jIvo 'pIti /
yakShAnurUpo hi baliriti nyAyaprasiddhiH /
ataH sadAtmanA sarvavyavahArANAM sarvavikArAmAM ca satyatvaM sato 'nyatvenAnR^itatvamiti na kashciddoShastArkikairihAnuvaktuM shakyaH /
yathetaretaraviruddhadvaitavAdAH svabuddhivikalpamAtrA atattvaniShThA iti shakyaM vaktum //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 6,3.3

#<tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itam ekaikAM karavANIti |
seyaM devatemAs tisro devatA anenaiva jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkarot || ChUp_6,3.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,3.3 saivaM tisro devatA anupravishya svAtmAvasthe bIjabhUte avyAkR^ite nAmarUpe vyAkaravANItIkShitvA tAsAM ca tisR^iNAM devatAnAmekaikAM trivR^itaM trivR^itaM karavANi /
ekaikasyAsrivR^itkaraNa ekaikasyAH prAdhAnyaM dvayordvayorguNabhAvo 'nthathA hi rajjavA ivaikameva trivR^itkaraNaM syAt na tu tisR^iNAM pR^ithakpR^ithaktrivR^itkaraNamiti /
evaM hi tejobannAnAM pR^ithaÇnAmapratyayalAbhaH syAtteja idamimA Apo 'nnamidamiti ca /
sati ca pR^ithaÇnAmapratyayalAbhe devatAnAM samyagvyavahArasya prasiddhiH prayojanaM syAt /
evamIkShitvA seyaM devatemAstisro devatA anenaiva yathoktenaiva jIvena sUryabimbavadantaH pravishya vairAjaM piNDaM prathamaM devAdInAM ca piNDAnanupravishya yathAsaN^kalpameva nAmarUpe vyAkarodasaunAmAyamidaMrUpa iti //3 //

START ChUp 6,3.4

#<tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itam ekaikAm akarot |

__________


ChUpBh_6,3.4 tAsAM ca devatAnAM guNapradhAnabhAvena trivR^itaM trivR^itamekaikAmakarotkR^itavatI devatA /
tiShThatu tAvaddevatAdipiNDAnAM nAmarUpAbhyAM vyAkR^itAnAM tejobannamayatvena tridhAtvaM, yathA tu khalu bahurimAH piNDebhyastisro devatAsrivR^ittrivR^idekaikA bhavati tanme mama nigadato vijAnIhi viShTaspamavadhArayodAharaNataH //4//

START ChUp 6,4.1

#<yad agne rohitaM rUpaM tejasas tad rUpam |
yac chuklaM tad apAm |
yat kR^iShNaM tad annasya |
apAgAd agner agnitvam |
vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM trINi rUpANIty eva satyam || ChUp_6,4.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,4.1 yattaddevatAnAM trivR^itkaraNamuktaM tasyaivodAharaNamucyate /
udAharaNaM nAmaikadeshaprasiddhyarthamudAhriyata iti /
tadetadAha - yadagnesrivR^itkR^itAnAM, yatkR^iShNaM tasyaivAgne rUpaM tadannasya pR^ithivyA atrivR^itkR^itAyA iti viddhi /
tatraivaM sata rUpatrayavyatirekeNAgniriti yanmanyase tvaM tasyAgneragnitvamidAnImapAgAdapagatam /
prAgrUpatrayavivekavij~nAnAdyAgnibuddhirAsItte sAgnibuddhirapagatAgnishabdashcetyarthaH /
yathAdR^iShyamAnaraktopadhAnasaMyuktaH sphaTiko gR^ihyamANaH padmarAgo 'yamitishabdabuddhyoH prayojako bhavati prAgupadhAnasphaTikayorvivekavij~nAne tu padmarAgashabdabuddhI nivartete tadvivekavij~nAtustadvat /
nanu kimatra buddhishabdakalpanayA kriyate prAgrUpatrayavivekakaraNAdagnirevA'sIttadagneragnitvaM rohitAdirUpavivekakaraNAdapAgAditi yuktaM yathA tantvapakarShaNe paTAbhAvaH /
naivaM, buddhishabdamAtrameva hyagniryata Aha vAcA'rambhaNamagnirnAma vikAro nAmadheya nAmamAtramityarthaH /
ato 'gnibuddharapi mR^iShaiva /
kiM tarhi tatra satyaM trINi rUpANItyeva satyaM nANumAtramapi rUpatrayavyatirekeNa satyamastItyavadhAraNArthaH //1 //

START ChUp 6,4.2

#<yad Adityasya rohitaM rUpaM tejasas tad rUpam |

apAgAd AdityAd Adityatvam |
vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM trINi rUpANIty eva satyam || ChUp_6,4.2 ||>#

#<yac candramaso rohitaM rUpaM tejasas tad rUpam |

apAgAc candrAc candratvam |

#<yad vidyuto rohitaM rUpaM tejasas tad rUpam |
yac chuklaM tad apAm |
yat kR^iShNaM tad annasya |

vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM trINi rUpANIty eva satyam || ChUp_6,4.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,4.2,3,4 tathA yadAdityasya yaccandramaso yadvidyuta ityAdi samAnam /
nanu yathA nu khalu somyemAstisro devatAsrivR^ittrivR^idekaikA bhavati tanme vijAnIhityuktvA tejasa eva caturbhirapyudAharaNairagnyAdibhisrivR^itkaraNaM darshitaM nAbannayorudAharaNaM darshitaM trivR^itkaraNe /
naiSha doShaH /
abannaviShayANyapyudAharaNAnyevameva ca draShTavyAnIti manyate shrutiH /
tejasa udAharaNamupalakShaNArtham /
rUpavattvAtspaShTArthatvopapatteshca /
gandharasayoranudAharaNaM trayANAmasambhavAt /
na hi gandharasau tejasi staH /
sparshashabdayoranudAharaNaM vibhAgena darshayitumashakyatvAt /
yadi sarvaM jagattrivR^itkR^itamityagnyAdivattrINi rUpANItyeva satyamagneragnitvavadapAgAjjagato jagattvam /
tathAnnasyApyapshuN^gatvAdApa ityeva satyaM vAcArambhaNamAtramannam /
tathApAmapi tejaHshuN^gatvAdvAcArambhaNatvaM teja ityeva satyam /
tejaso 'pi sacchuN^gatvAdvAcArambhaNatvaM sadityeva satyamityeShor'tho vivakShitaH /
nanu vAyvantarikShe tvatrivR^itkR^ite tejaH prabhR^itiShvanantarbhUtatvAdavashiShyete /
evaM gandharasashabdasparshAshcAvashiShTA iti kathaM satA vij~nAtena sarvamanyadvij~nAtaM bhavettadvij~nAne vA prakArAntaraM vAcyam /
naiSha doShaH /
rUpavaddravye sarvasya darshanAt /
tejasi tAvadrUpavati shabdasparshayorapyulabhbhAdvAyvantarikShayostatra sparshashabdaguNavatoH sadbhAvo 'numIyate /
tathAbannayo rUpavato rasagandhAntabhAva iti /
rUpavatAM trayANAM tejobannAnAM trivR^itkaraNapradarshanena sarvaM tadantarbhUtaM sadvikAratvAt rUpatrayavat vij~nAtaM manyate shrutiH /
na hi mUrtaM rUpavaddravyaM pratyAkhyAya vAyvAkAshayostadguNayorgandharasayorvA grahaNamasti /
athavA rUpavatAmapi trivR^itkaraNaM pradarshanArthameva manyate shrutiH /
yathA tu trivR^itkR^ite trINi rUpANItyeva satyaM tathA paJNcIkaraNe 'pi samAno nyAya ityataH sarvasya sadvikAratvAtsatA vij~nAtena sarvamidaM vij~nAtaM syAtsadekamevAdvitIyaM satyamiti siddhameva bhavati /
tadekasminsati vij~nAte sarvamidaM vij~nAtaM bhavatIti sUktam //2-4 //

START ChUp 6,4.5

#<etad dha sma vai tadvidvAMsa AhuH pUrve mahAshAlA mahAshrotriyAH |

ChUpBh_6,4.5 etadvidvAMso viditavantaH pUrve 'tikrAntA mahAshAlA mahAshroNiyA Ahurha sma vai kila /
kimuktavanta ityAhana no 'smAkaM kule 'dyedAnIM yathoktavij~nAnavatAM kashna kashcidapyashrutamamatamavij~nAtamudAhariShyati nodAhariShyati sarvaM vij~nAtamevAsmatkulInAnAM sadvij~nAnavattvAdityAbhiprAyaH /

#<yad v avij~nAtam ivAbhUd ity etAsAm eva devatAnAM samAsa iti tad vidAM cakruH |

ChUpBh_6,4.6,7 katham /
yadanyadrUpeNa sandihyamAne kapotAdirUpe rohitamiva yadgR^ihyamANamabhUtteShAM pUrveShAM brahmavidAM tattejaso rUpamiti vidAJNcakruH tathA yacchuklamivAbhUdgR^ihyamANaM tadApAM rUpaM yatkR^iShNamiva gR^ihyamANaM tadannasyeti vidAJNcakrurevamevAtyantadurlakShyaM yadu apyavij~nAtamiva visheShato 'gR^ihyamANamabhUttadapyetAsAmeva tisR^iNAM devatAnAM samAsaH samudAya iti vidAJNcakruH /
evaM tAvadbAhyaM vastvagnyAdivavij~nAtaM tathedAnIM yathA nu khalu he somyemA yathoktAstisro devatAH puraShaM shiraHpAmyAdilakShaNaM kAryakAraNasaN^ghAtaM prApya puruSheNopayujyamAnAsrivR^ittrivR^idekaikA bhavati tanme vijAnIhi nigadata ityuktvA'ha //6-7 //

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasya caturthaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 6,5.1

#<annam ashitaM tredhA vidhIyate |
tasya yaH sthaviShTho dhAtus tat purIShaM bhavati |
yo madhyamas tan mAMsam |
yo 'NiShThas tan manaH || ChUp_6,5.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,5.1 annamashitaM bhuktaM tredhA vidhIyate jATharemAgninA pacyamAnaM tridhA vibhajyate /
kathaM, tasyAnnasya tridhA vidhIyamAnasya yaH sthaviShThaH sthUlatamo dhAtuH sthUlatamaM vastu vibhaktasya sthUloM'shastatpurIShaM bhavati /
yo madhyamoM'sho dhAturannasya tadrasAdikrameNa pariNamya mAMsaM bhavati yo 'NiShTho 'Nutamo dhAtuH sa UrdhvaM hR^idayaM prApya sUkShmAsu hitAkhyAsu nADIpvanupravisya vAgAdikaraNasaN^ghAtasya sthitimutpAdayanmano bhavati manorUpeNa vipariNamanmanasa upacayaM karoti /
tatashcAnnopacitatvAnmanaso bhautikatvameva na vaisheShikatantroktalakShaNaM nityaM niravayaM ceti gR^ihyate /
yadapi mano 'sya daivaM cakShuriti vakShyati tadapi na nityatvApekShayA kiM tarhi sUkShmavyavahitaviprakR^iShTAdisarvendriyaviShayavyApakatvApekShayA /
yaccAnyendriyaviShayApekShayA nityatvaM tadapyApekShikameveti vakShyAmaH /
sadekamevAdvitIyamiti shruteH //1 //

START ChUp 6,5.2

ChUpBh_6,5.4 yata evamannamayaM hi somya mana ApomayaH prANastejomayI vAk /
nanu kevalAnnabhakShiNa AkhuprabhR^itayo vAgminaH prANavantashca tathAMmAtrabhakShyAH sAmudrA mInamakaraprabhR^itayo manasvino vAggminashca tathA snehapAnAmapi prANavattvaM cAnumeyaM yadi santi tatra kathamannamayaM hi somya mana ityAdyucyate /
naiSha doShaH /
sarvasya trivR^itkR^itatvAtsarvatra sarvopapatteH /

ityevaM pratyAyitaH shveketurAha-bhUya eva punareva mA mAM bhagavAnannamayaM hi somya mana ityAdi vij~nApayatu dR^iShTAntenAvagamayu nAdyApi mamAsminnarthe samyaÇnishcayo jAtaH /

tamevamuktavantaM tathAstu somyeti hovAca pitA shR^iNvatra dR^iShTAntaM yathaitadupapadyate yatpR^icchasi //4//

manastvannamayamityatra naikAntena mama nishcayo jAto 'to bhUya eva mA bhagavAnmanaso 'nnamayatvaM dR^iShTAntena vij~nApayatviti /

START ChUp 6,7.1

#<ShoDashakalaH somya puruShaH |
paJNcadashAhAni mAshIH |
kAmam apaH piba |
ApomayaH prANo na pibato vicchetsyata iti || ChUp_6,7.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,7.1 annasya bhuktasya yo 'NiShTho dhAtuH sa manasi shaktimadhAt sAnnopacitA manasaH shaktiH ShoDashadhA pravibhajya puruShasya kalAtvena nirdidikShitA /
tayA manasyannopacitayA shaktyA ShoDashadhA pravibhaktayA saMyuktastadvAnkAryakaraNasaN^ghAtalakShaNo jIvavishiShTaH piNDaH puruShaH ShoDashakala ucyate yasyAM satyAM draShTA shrotA mantA boddhA kartA vij~nAtA sarvakriyAsamarthaH puruSho bhavati hIyamAnAyAM ca yasyAM sAmarthyahAniH /
vakShyati"cAthAnnasyA'yI draShTe"tyAdi /
sarvasya kAryakaraNasya sAmarthyaM manaHkR^itameva /
mAnasena hi balena sampannA balino dR^ishyante loke, dhyAnAhArAshca kecidannasya sarvAtmakatvAt /
ato 'nnakR^itaM mAnasaM vIryaM ShoDasha kalA yasya puruShasya so 'yaM ShoDashakalaH puruShaH etaccetpratyakShIkartumicchasi paJNcadashasaMkhyAkAnyahAni mAshIrashanaM mA kArShIH /
kAmamicchAto 'paH piba yasmAnnapibato 'paste prANo vicchetsyate vicchedamApatsyate yasmAdApomayo 'bvikAraH prANa ityavocAma /
na hi kAryaM svakAraNopaShTambhamantareNAvibhraMshamAnaM sthAtumutsahate //1 //

START ChUp 6,7.2

#<sa ha paJNcadashAhAni nAsha |
atha hainam upasasAda kiM bravImi bho iti |
R^icaH somya yajUMShi sAmAnIti |
sa hovAca na vai mA pratibhAnti bho iti || ChUp_6,7.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,7.2 sa haivaM shrutvA manaso 'nnamayatvaM pratyakShIkartuMmicchanpaJNcadashAhAni nA'shAshanaM na kR^itavAn /
atha ShoDashe 'hani hainaM pitaramupasasAdopagatavAnupagamya covAca kiM bravImi bho iti /
itara Aha R^icaH somya yajUMShi sAmAnyadhIShveti /
evamuktaH pitrA'ha-na vai mA mAmR^igAdIni mama manasi na dR^ishyanta ityartho he bho bhagavanniti //2//

START ChUp 6,7.3

#<taM hovAca yathA somya mahato 'bhyAhitasyaiko 'N^gAraH khadyotamAtraH parishiShTaH syAt |
tena tato 'pi na bahu dahet |
evaM somya te ShoDashAnAM kalAnAm ekA kalA atishiShTA syAt |
tayaitarhi vedAn nAnubhavasi |
ashAna |
atha me vij~nAsyasIti || ChUp_6,7.3 ||>#

ChUpBh_6,7.3 evamuktavantaM pitA'ha-shR^iNu tatra kAraNaM yena te tAnyR^igAdIni na pratibhAntIti (taM hovAca) yathA loke he somya mahato mahatparimANasyAbhyAhitasyopacitasyendhanairagnereko 'N^gAraH khadyotaparimANaH shAntasya parishiShTo 'vashiShTaH syAdbhavettenoN^gAreNa tato 'pi tatparimANAdIShadapi na bahu dahedevameva khalu somya te tavAnnopacitAnAM ShoDashAnAM kalAnAmekA kalAvayavo 'tishiShTAvashiShTA na bahu dahedevameva khalu somya te tavAnnopacitAnAM ShoDashAnAM kalAnAmekA kalAvayavo 'tishiShTA syAttayA tvaM khadyotamAtrAN^gAratulyayaitarhIdAnIM vedAnnAnubhavasi na pratipadyase, shrutvA ca me mama vAcamathAsheShaM vij~nAsyasyashAna bhuN^kShva tAvat //3 //

START ChUp 6,7.4

ChUpBh_6,7.4 sa ha tathaivA'sha bhuktavAnathAnantaraM hainaM pitaraM shushrUShurupasasAda taM hopagataM putraM yatkiJNcargAdiShu papraccha grantharUpamarthajAtaM vA pitA sa shvetaketuH sarvaM ha tatpratipede R^igAdyarthato granthatashca //4 //

START ChUp 6,7.5

#<taM hovAca |
yathA somya mahato 'bhyAhitasyaikam aN^gAraM khadyotamAtraM parishiShTaM taM tR^inair upasamAdhAya prAjvalayet tena tato 'pi bahu dahet || ChUp_6,7.5 ||>#

ChUpBh_6,7.5 taM hovAca punaH pitA yathA somya mahato 'bhyAhitAsyetyAdi samAnamekamaN^gAraM shAntasyAgneH khadyotamAtraM parishiShTaM taM tR^iNaishcUrNaishcopasamAdhAya prAjvalayedvardhayet /

#<evaM somya te ShoDashAnAM kalAnAm ekA kalAtishiShTAbhUt |

ApomayaH prANaH |
tejomayI vAg iti |

ChUpBh_6,7.6 evaM somya te ShoDashAnAmannakalAnAM sAmarthyarUpANAmekA kalAtishiShTAbhUdatishiShTA'sItpaJNcadashAhAnyabhuktavata ekaikenAhnaikaikA kalA candramasa ivAparapakShe kShINA sAtishiShTA kalA tavAnnena bhuktenopasamAhitA vardhitopacitA prAjvAli /

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasya saptamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 6,8.1

#<uddAlako hAruNiH shvetaketuM putram uvAca svapnAntaM me somya vijAnIhIti |
yatraitat puruShaH svapiti nAma satA somya tadA saMpanno bhavati |
svam apIto bhavati |
tasmAd enaM svapitIty AcakShate |
svaM hy apIto bhavati || ChUp_6,8.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,8.1 yasminmanasi jIvenA'tmanAnupraviShTA parA devatA'darsha iva puruShaH pratibimbena jalAdiviShviva ca sUryAdayaH pratibimbaiH /
tanmano 'nnamayaM tejo 'MmayAbhyAM vAkprANAbhyAM saMgatamadhigatam /
yanmayo yatsthashca jIvo mananadarshanashravaNAdivyAvahArAya kalpate taduparame ca svaM devatArUpameva pratipadyate /
taduktaM shrutyantare"dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva sadhIH svapno bhUtvemaM lokamatikrAmati""sa vA AyamAtmA brahma vij~nAnamayo manomaya"ityAdi,"svapnena shArIram" ityAdi,"prANanneva prANo nAma bhavatI"tyAdi ca /
tasyAsya manaHsthasya mana AkhyAM gatasya manaupashamadvAreNendriyaviShayebhyo nivR^ittasya yasyAM parasyAM devatAyAM svAtmabhAtAyAM yadavasthAnaM tatputrAyA'cikhyAsuruddAlako ha kilA'ruNiH shvetaketuM putramuvAcoktavAn /
svapnAntaM svapnamadhyaM svapna iti darshanavR^itteH svapnasyA'khyA tasya madhyaM svapnAntaM suShuptamityetat /
athavA svapnAntaM svapnasatattvamityarthaH tatrApyarthAtsuShuptameva bhavati /
svamapIto bhavatIti vacanAt /
na hyanyatra suShuptAtsvamapItiM jIvasyecchanti brahmavidaH /
tatra hyAdarshApanayane puruShapratibimbi Adarshagato yathA svameva puruShamapIto bhavatyevaM mana Adyuparame caitanyapratibimbarUpeNa jIvenA'tmanA manasi praviShTA nAmarUpavyAkaraNAya parA devatA sA svamevA'tmAnaM pratipadyate jIvarUpatAM mana AkhyAM hitvA /
ataH suShupta eva svapnAntashabdavAcya ityavagamyate /
yatra tu suptaH svapnAnpashyati tatsvApnaM darshanaM sukhaduHkhasaMyuktamiti puNyApuNyayorhi sukhaduHkhArambhakatvaM prasiddham /
puNyApuNyayoshcAvidyAkAmopaShTambhenaiva sukhaduHkhataddarshanakAryArambhakatvamupapadyate nAnyathetyavidyAkAmakarmabhiH saMsArahetubhiH saMyukta eva svapna iti na svamapItA bhavati /
"ananvAgataM puNyenAnanvAgataM pApena tIrNo hi tadA sarvAJNchokAnhR^idayasya bhavati" "tadvA asyaitadaticchandA" "eSha parama Ananda"ityAdishrutibhyaH /
suShupta eva svaM devatArUpaM jIvatvavinirmuktaM darshayiShyAmItyAha /
svapnAntaM me mama nigadato he somya vijAnIhi vispaShTamavadhArayetyarthaH /
kadA svapnAnto bhavatItyucyate /
yatra yasminkAla etannAma bhavati puruShasya svapsyataH /
prasiddhaM hi loke svapitIti /
gauNaM cedaM nAmetyAha /
yadA svapitItyucyate puruShastadA tasminkAle satA sacchabdavAcyayA prakR^itayA devatayA saMpanno bhavati saMgata ekIbhUto bhavati /
manasi praviShTaM mana AdisaMsargakR^itaM jIvarUpaM parityajya svaM sadrUpaM yatparamArthasatyamapIto 'pigato bhavati /
atastasmAtsvapitItyenamAcakShate lokikAH /
svamAtmAnaM hi yasmAdapIto bhavati /
tatashcA'yastAnAM karaNAnAmanekavyApAranimittaglAnAnAM svavyApArebhya uparamo bhavati /
shruteshca"shrAmyatyeva vAkshrAmyati cakShur" ityevamAdi /
tathA ca"gR^ihItA vAggR^ihItaM shrotraM gR^ihItaM mana"ityevamAdIni karaNAni prANagrastAni /
prANa eko 'shrAnto dehe kulAye yo jAgarti tadA jIvaH shramApanuttaye svaM devatArUpamAtmAnaM pratipadyate /
nAnyatra svarUpAvasthAnAcchramApanodaH syAditi yuktA prasiddhirlaukikAnAM svaM hyapIto bhavatIti /
dR^ishyate hi loke jvarAdirogagrastAnAM tadvinirnoke svAtmasthAnAM vishramaNaM tadvadihApi syAditi yuktam /
"tadyathA shyeno vA suparNo vA viparipatya shrAnta"ityAdishruteShca //1 //

START ChUp 6,8.2

#<sa yathA shakuniH sUtreNa prabaddho dishaM dishaM patitvAnyatrAyatanam alabdhvA bandhanam evopashrayate |
evam eva khalu somya tan mano dishaM dishaM patitvAnyatrAyatanam alabdhvA prANam evopashrayate |
prANabandhanaM hi somya mana iti || ChUp_6,8.2 ||>#

ChUpBh_6,8.2 tatrAyaM dR^iShTAnto yathokter'the-sa yathA shakuniH pakShI shakunighAtakasya hastagatena sUtreNa prabaddhaH pAshito dishaM dishaM bandhanamokShArthI sanpratishidishaM patitvAnyatra bandhanAdAyatanamAshrayaM vishramaNAyAlabdhvAprApya bandhanamevopashrayate /

sa mana AkhyopAdhirjIvo 'vidyAkAmakarmopadiShTAM dishaM dishaM sukhaduHkhAdilakShaNAM jAgratsvapnayoH patitvA gatvAnubhUyetyarthaH /

START ChUp 6,8.3

#<ashanApipAse me somya vijAnIhIti |
yatraitat puruSho 'shishiShati nAmApa eva tad ashitaM nayante |
tad yathA gonAyo 'shvanAyaH puruShanAya ity evaM tad apa AcakShate 'shanAyeti |
tatraitac chuN^gam utpatitaM somya vijAnIhi |
nedam amUlaM bhaviShyatIti || ChUp_6,8.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,8.3 evaM svapitinAmaprasiddhidvAreNa yajjIvasya satyasvarUpaM jagato mUlaM tatputrasya darshayitvA'hAnnAdikAryakAraNaparamparayApi jagato mUlaM saddidarshayiShuH /
ashanApipAse ashitumicchAshanA yAlopena /
pAtumicchA pipAsA te ashanApipAse ashanApipAsayoH satatvaM vijAnIhItyetat /
yatra yasminkAla etannAma puruSho bhavati /
kiM tat?ashishiShatyashitumicchatIti /
tadA tasya puruShasya kinimittaM nAma bhavatItyAha /
yattatpuruSheNAshitamannaM kaThinaM potA Apo nayante dravIkR^itya rasAdibhAvena vipariNamayante tadA bhuktamannaM jIryati /
atha ca bhavatyasya nAmAshishiShatIti gauNam /
jIrNe hyanne 'shitumicchati sarvo hi jantuH /
tat tatra apAmashitanetR^itvAdashanAyA iti nAma prasiddhamityetasminnarthe /
yathA gonAyo gAM nayatIti gonAya ityucyate gopAlaH /
tathAshvAnnayatItyashvanAyo 'shvapAla ityucyate /
puruShanAyaH puruShAnnayatIti rAjA senApatirvA /
evaM tattadApa AcakShate laukikA ashanAyeti visarjanIyalopena /
tatraivaM satyadbhI rasAdibhAvena nItenAshitenAnnena niShpAditamidaM sharIraM vaTakaNikAyAmiva shuN^go 'N^kura utpatita udgatastamimaM shuN^gaM kAryaM sharIrAkhyaM vaTAdishuN^gavadutpatitaM he sobhya vijAnIhi /
kiM tatra vij~neyamityucyate /
shuNvidaM shuN^gavatkAryatvAccharIraM nAmUlaM mUlarahitaM bhaviShyatItyukta Aha shvetaketuH //3 //

START ChUp 6,8.4

#<tasya kva mUlaM syAd anyatrAnnAt |
evam eva khalu somyAnnena shuN^genApo mUlam anviccha |
adbhiH somya shuN^gena tejo mUlam anviccha |
tejasA somya shuN^gena sanmUlam anviccha |
sanmUlAH somyemAH sarvAH prajAH sadAyatanAH satpratiShThAH || ChUp_6,8.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,8.4 yadyevaM samUlamidaM sharIraM vaTAdishuN^gavattasyAsya kva mUlaM syAdbhavedityevaM pR^iShTa Aha pitA /
tasya kva mUlaM syAdanyatrAnnAdannaM mUlamityabhiprAyaH /
katham /
ashitaM hyannamadbhirdravIkR^itaM jAThareNAgninA pacyamAnaM rasabhAvena pariNamate /
rasocchoNitaM shoNitAnmAMsaM mAMsAnmedo medaso 'sthInyasthibhyo majjA majjAyAH shukram /
tathA yoShidbhuktaM cAnnaM rasAdikrameNaivaM pariNataM lohitaM bhavati /
tAbhyAM shukrashoNitAbhyAmannakAryAbhyAM saMyuktAbhyAmannenaiva pratyahaM bhujyamAnenA'pUryamANAbhyAM kuDyamiva mR^itpiNDaiH pratyuhamupacIyamAno 'nnamUlo dehashuN^gaH pariniShpanna ityarthaH /

apAmapi vinAshotpattimattavAcchuN^gatvameveti adbhiH sImya shuN^gena kAryeNa kAraNaM tejo mUlamanviccha /
tejaso 'pi vinAshotpattimattavAcchuN^gatvamiti tejasA somya shuN^gena sanmUlamekamevAdvitIyaM paramArthasatyam /
yasminsarvamidaM vAcA'rambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyamanR^itaM rajjvAmiva sarpAdivikalpajAtamadhyastamavidyayA tadasya jagato mUlamataH sanmUlAH satkAraNA he somyemAH sthAvarajaN^gamalakShaNAH sarvAH prajA na kevalaM sanmUlA evedAnImapi sthitikAle sadAyatanAH sadAshrayA eva /
nahi mR^idamanAshritya ghaTAdeH sattvaM sthitirvAsti /
ato mR^idvatsanmUtvAtprajAnAM sadAyatanaM yAsAM tAH sadAyatanAH prajAH /
ante ca satpratiShThAH sadeva pratiShTA layaH samAptipavasAnaM parisheSho yAsAM tAH satpratiShThAH //4 //

START ChUp 6,8.5

#<atha yatraitat puruShaH pipAsati nAma teja eva tat pItaM nayate |
tad yathA gonAyo 'shvanAyaH puruShanAya ity evaM tat teja AcaShTa udanyeti |
tatraitad eva shuN^gam utpatitaM somya vijAnIhi |
nedam amUlaM bhaviShyatIti || ChUp_6,8.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,8.5 athedAnImapshuN^gadvAreNa sato mUlasyAnugamaH kArya ityAha /
yatra yasminkAla etannAma pipAsati pAtumicchatIti puruSho bhavati /
ashishiShatItivadidamapi gauNameva nAma bhavati /
dravIkR^itasyAshitasyAnnasya netrya Apo 'nnashuN^gaM dehaM kledayantyaH shithilI kuryurabbAhulyAdyadi tejasA na shoShyante /

START ChUp 6,8.6

#<tasya kva mUlaM syAd anyatrAdbhyaH |
adbhiH somya shuN^gena tejo mUlam anviccha |
tejasA somya shuN^gena sanmUlam anviccha |
sanmUlAH somyemAH sarvAH prajAH sad AyatanAH satpratiShThAH |
yathA nu khalu somyemAs tisro devatAH puruShaM prApya trivR^it trivR^id ekaikA bhavati tad uktaM purastAd eva bhavati |
asya somya puruShasya prayato vAÇ manasi saMpadyate manaH prANe prANas tejasi tejaH parasyAM devatAyAm || ChUp_6,8.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,8.6 sAmarthyAttejaso 'pyetadeva sharIrAkhyaM shuN^gam /
ato 'pshuN^gena dehenA'po mUlaM gamyate /
adbhiH shuN^gena tejo mUlaM gamyate /
tejasA shuN^gena sanmUlaM gamyate pUrvavat /
evaM hi tejobannamayasya dehashuN^gasya vAcArambhaNamAtrasyAnnAdiparamparayA paramArthasatyaM sanmUlamabhayasaMtrAsaM nirAyAsaM sanmUlamanviccheti putraM gamayitvAshishiShati pipAsatIti nAmaprasiddhidvAreNa yadanyadihAsminprakaraNe tejobannAnAM puruSheNopabhujyamAnAnAM kAryakaraNasaMghAtasya dehashuN^gasya svajAtyasAMkaryeNopacayakaratvaM vaktavyaM prAptaM tadihoktameva draShTavyamiti pUrvoktaM vyapadishati /
yathA nu khalu yena prakAreNemAstejobannAkhyAstisro devatAH puruShaM prApya trivR^ittrivR^idekaikA bhavati taduktaM purastAdeva bhavatyannamashitaM tredhA vidhIyata ityAdi /
tatraivoktamannAdInAmasitAnAM ye mavyamA dhAtavaste sAptadhAtukaM sharIramupacinvantItyuktam /
"mAMsaM bhavati lohitaM bhavati majjA bhavatyasthi bhavati ye tvaNiShThA dhAtavo manaH prANaM vAcaM dehasyAntaHkaraNasaMghAtamupacinvantI"ti coktaM"tanmano bhavati sa prANo bhavati sA vAgbhavatI"ti /
so 'yaM prANakaraNasaMghAto dehe vishIrNe dehAntaraM jIvAdhiShThito yena krameNa pUrvadehAtpracyuto gacchati tadAhAsya he somya puruShasya prayato mriyamANasya vAÇmanasi saMpadyate manasyupasaMhriyate /
atha tadA'hurj~nAtayo na vadatIti /
manaHpUrvako hi vAgvyApAraH /
"yadvai manasA dhyAyati tadvAcA vadati"iti shruteH /
vAcyupasaMhR^itAyAM manasi mano mananavyApAreNa kevalena vartate /
mano 'pi yadopasaMhriyate tadA manaH prANe saMpannaM bhavati suShuptakAla iva tadA pArshvasthA j~nAtayo na vijAnAtItyAhuH /
prANashca tadordhvocchvAsI svAtmanyupasaMhR^itabAhyakaraNaH saMvargavidyAyAM darshanAddhastapAdAdInvikShipanmarmasthAnAni nikR^intannana ivotsR^ijan krameNopasaMhR^itastejasi sampadyate /
tadA'hurj~nAtayo na calatIti mR^ito neti vA vicikitsanto dehamAlabhamAnA uShNaM copalabhamAnA deha uShNo jIvatIti yadA tadapyauShNyaliN^gaM teja upasaMhriyate tadA tattejaH parasyAM devatAyAM prashAmyati /
tadevaN^krameNopasaMhR^ite svamUlaM prApte ca manasi tatstho jIvo 'pi suShuptakAlavannimittopasaMhArAdupasaMhriyamANaH sansatyAbhisaMdhipUrvakaM cedupasaMhriyate sadeva saMpadyate na punardehAntarAya suShuptAdivottiShThati /
yathA loke sabhaye deshe vartamAnaH kathaJNcidivAbhayaM deshaM prAptastadvat /
itarastvanAtmaj~nastasmAdeva mUlAtsuShuptAdivotthAya mR^itvA punardehajAlamAvishati //6 //

START ChUp 6,8.7

#<sa ya eSho 'Nimaitad Atmyam idaM sarvam |
tat satyam |
sa AtmA |
tat tvam asi shvetaketo iti |
bhUya eva mA bhagavAn vij~nApayatv iti |
tathA somyeti hovAca || ChUp_6,8.7 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,8.7 yasmAnmUlAdutthAya dehamAvishati jIvaH sa yaH sadAkhya eSha ukto 'NimANubhAvo jagato mUlamaitadAtmyametatsadAtmA yasya sarvasya tadetadAtma tasya bhAva aitadAtmyam /
etena sadAkhyenA'tmanA'tmavatsarvamidaM jagat /
nAnyo 'styasyA'tmA saMsArI /
"nAnyadato 'ti shrotR^i"ityAdishrutyantarAt /
yena cA'tmanA'tmavatsarvamidaM jagattadeva sadAkhyaM kAraNaM satyaM paramArthasat /
ataH sa evA'tmA jagataH pratyaksvarUpaM satattvaM yAthAtmyam /
Atmashabdasya nirupapadasya pratyagAtmani gavAdishabdavannirUDhatvAt /
atastatsattvamasIti he shvetaketo ityevaM pratyAyitaH putra Aha-bhUya eva mA bhagavAnvij~nApayatu yadbhavaduktaM tatsandigdhaM mamAhanyahani sarvAH prajAH suShupte satsaMpadyanta ityetadyena tatsaMpadya na viduH satsampannA vayamiti /
ato dR^iShTontena mAM pratyAyayatvityarthaH /
evamuktastathAstu somyeti hovAca pitA //7//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasyAShTamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 6,9.1

#<yathA somya madhu madhukR^ito nistiShThanti nAnAtyayAnAM vR^ikShANAM rasAn samavahAram ekatAM rasaM gamayanti || ChUp_6,9.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,9.1 yatpR^icchasyahanyahani satsaMpadya na viduH satsaMpannAH sma iti tatkasmAdityatra shR^iNu dR^iShTAntam /
yathA loke he somya madhukR^ito madhu kurvantIti madhukR^ito madhukaramakShikA madhu nistiShThanti madhu niShpAdayanti tatparAH santaH /
katham?nAnAtyayAnAM nAnAgatInAM nAnAdikkAnAM vR^ikShANAM rasAnsamavahAraM samAhR^ityaikatAmekabhAvaM madhutvena rasAngamayanti madhutvamApAdayanti //1 //

START ChUp 6,9.2

#<te yathA tatra na vivekaM labhante 'muShyAhaM vR^ikShasya raso 'smy amuShyAhaM vR^ikShasya raso 'smIti |
evam eva khalu somyemAH sarvAH prajAH sati saMpadya na viduH sati saMpadyAmaha iti || ChUp_6,9.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,9.2 te rasA yathA madhutvenaikatAM gatAstatra madhuni vivekaM na labhante /
katham, amuShyAhamAmrasya panasasya vA vR^ikShasya raso 'smIti /
yathA hi loke bahUnAM cetanAvatAM sametAnAM prANinAM vivekalAbho bhavatyamuShyAhaM putro 'muShyAhaM naptAsmIti /
te ca labdhavivekAH santo na saMkIryante na tathehAnekaprakAravR^ikSharasAnAmapi madhurAmlatiktakaTukAdInAM madhutvenaikatAM gatAnAM madhurAdibhAvena viveko gR^ihyata ityabhiprAyaH /
yathAyaM dR^iShTAnta ityevameva khalu somyemAH sarvAH prajA ahanyahani sati saMpadya suShuptakAle maraNapralayayoshca na vidurna vijAnIyuH sati saMpadyAmaha iti saMpannA iti vA //2 //

START ChUp 6,9.3

#<ta iha vyaghro vA siMho vA vR^iko vA varAho vA kITo vA pataN^go vA daMsho vA mashako vA yad yad bhavanti tad Abhavanti || ChUp_6,9.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,9.3 yasmAccaivamAtmanaH sadrUpatAmaj~nAtvaiva satsaMpadyante /
atasta iha loke yatkarmanimittAM yAM yAM jAtiM pratipannA AsurvyAghrAdInAM vyAghro 'haM siMho 'hamityevaM te tatkarmaj~nAnavAsanAN^kitAH santaH satpraviShTA api tadbhAvenaiva punarAbhavanti punaH sata Agatya vyAghro vA siMho vA vR^iko vA varAho vA kITo vA pataN^go vA daMsho vA mashako vA yadyatpUrvamiha loke bhavanti vabhUvurityarthaH /
tadeva punarAgatya bhavanti yugasahasrakoTyantaritApi saMsAriNo jantoryA purA bhAvitA vAsanA sA na nashyatItyarthaH /
"yathApraj~naM hi saMbhavAH"iti shruttyantarAt //3 //

START ChUp 6,10.1

#<imAH somya nadyaH purastAt prAcyaH syandante pashcAt pratIcyaH |

START ChUp 6,11.1

#<asya somya mahato vR^ikShasya yo mUle 'bhyAhanyAj jIvan sraved yo madhye 'bhyAhanyAj jIvan sraved yo 'gre 'bhyAhanyAj jIvan sravet |

ChUpBh_6,11.1 shR^iNu dR^iShTAntamasya - he somya mahato 'nekashAkhAdiyuktasya vR^ikShasyAsyetyagrataH sthitaM vR^ikShaM darshayannAha /

START ChUp 6,11.2

#<asya yad ekAM shAkhAM jIvo jahAty atha sA shuShyati |
dvitIyAM jahAty atha sA shuShyati |
tR^itIyAM jahAty atha sA shuShyati |
sarvaM jahAti sarvaH shuShyati || ChUp_6,11.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,11.2 tasyAsya yadekAM shAkhAM rogagrastAmAhatAM vA jIvo jahAtyupasaMharati shAkhAyAM viprasR^itamAtmAMsham /
atha sA shuShyati /
vAÇmanaHprANakaraNagrAmAnupraviShTo hi jIva iti tadupasaMhAra upasaMhriyate /
jIvena ca prANayuktenAshitaM potaM ca rasatAM gataM jIvaccharIraM vR^ikShaM vardhayadrasarUpeNa jIvasya sadbhAve liN^gaM bhavati /
ashitapItAbhyAM hi dehe jIvastiShThati te cAshitapIte jIvakarmAnusAriNI iti /
tasyaikAN^gavaikalyanimittaM karma yadopasthitaM bhavati tadA jIva ekAM shAkhAM jahAti shAkhAyA AtmAnamupasaMharati /
atha tadA sA shAkhA shuShyati /
jIvasthitinimitto raso jIvakarmAkShipto jIvopasaMhAre na tiShThati /
rasApagame ca shAkhA shoShamupaiti /

ChUpBh_6,11.3 yathAsminvR^ikShadR^iShTAnte darshitaM jIvena yukto vR^ikSho 'shuShko rasapAnAdiyukto jAvatItyucyate tadapetashca mriyata ityucyate /

START ChUp 6,12.1

#<nyagrodhaphalam ata Ahareti |

aNvya ivemA dhAnA bhagava iti |

ChUpBh_6,12.1 yadyetatpratyakShIkartumicchasi, ato 'smAnmahato nyagrodhAtphalamekamAharetyuktastathA cakAra, sa idaM bhagava upahR^itaM phalamiti darshitavantaM pratyAha phalaM bhindhIti /

ChUpBh_6,13.1 vidyamAnamapi vastu nopalabhyate prakArAntareNa tUpalabhyata iti shR^iNvatra dR^iShTAntam yadi cemamarthaM pratyakSho sa ha pitroktamarthaM pratyakShIkartumicchaMstathA cakAra /

ChUpBh_6,13.2 yathA vilInaM lavaNaM na vettha tathApi taccakShuShA sparshanena ca piNDarUpaM lavaNamagR^ihyamANaM vidyata evApsUpalabhyate copAyAntareNetyetatputraM pratyAyayitumicchannAha-aN^gAsyodakasyAntAdupari gR^ihItvA'cAmetyuktvA putraM tathAkR^itavantamuvAca kathamitItara Aha lavaNaM svAdutaH iti /

tathAntAdadhodeshAdgR^ihItvA'cAmeti kathamiti lavaNamiti /

START ChUp 6,14.1

#<yathA somya puruShaM gandhArebhyo 'bhinaddhAkSham AnIya taM tato 'tijane visR^ijet |

ChUpBh_6,14.1 yathA loke he somya puruShaM yaM kaJNcidgandhArebhyo janapadebhyo 'bhinaddhAkShaM baddhacakShuShamAnIya dravyahartA taskarastamabhinaddhAkShameva baddhahastamaraNye tato 'pyatijane 'tigatajane 'tyantavigatajane deshe visR^ijetsa tatra digbhramopeto yathA prAÇvA prAgaJNcanaH prAÇmukho, vetyarthaH /

START ChUp 6,14.2

#<tasya yathAbhinahanaM pramucya prabrUyAd etAM dishaM gandhArA etAM dishaM vrajeti |

__________


ChUpBh_6,14.2 evaM vikroshatastasya yathAbhinahanaM yathAbandhanaM pramucya muktvA kAruNikaH kashcidetAM dishamuttarato gandhArA etAM dishaM vrajeti prabrUyAtsa evaM kAruNikena bandhanAnmokShito grAmAdgrAmAntaraM pR^icchanpaNDita upadeshavAnmedhAvo paropadiShTagrAmapraveshamArgAvadhAraNasamarthaH sangandhArAnevopasampadyeta netaro mUDhamatirdeshAntaradarshanatR^iDvA /

START ChUp 6,15.1

#<puruShaM somyotopatApinaM j~nAtayaH paryupAsate jAnAsi mAM jAnAsi mAm iti |

ChUpBh_6,15.1 puruShaM he somyotopatApinaM jvarAdyupatApavantaM j~nAtayo bAndhavAH parivAryopAsate mumUrShuM jAnAsi mAM tava pitaraM putraM bhrAtaraM veti pR^icchantastasya mumUrShoryAvanna vAÇmanasi sampadyate manaH prANe prANastejasi tejaH parasyAM devatAyAmityetaduktartham //1 //

START ChUp 6,15.2

#<atha yadAsya vAÇ manasi saMpadyate manaH prANe prANas tejasi tejaH parasyAM devatAyAm atha na jAnAti || ChUp_6,15.2 ||>#

ChUpBh_6,15.2 saMsAriNo yo maraNakramaH sa evAyaM viduSho 'pi satsampattikrama ityetadAha parasyAM devatAyAM tejasi sampanne 'tha na jAnAti /

START ChUp 6,16.1

#<puruShaM somyota hastagR^ihItam Anayanti |

ChUpBh_6,16.1 shR^iNu yathA somya puruShaM cauryakarmaNi sandihyamAnaM nigrahAya parIkShaNAya votApi hastagR^ihItaM baddhahastamAnayanti rAjapuruShAH /

(te cA'huH sandihyamAnaM steyamakArShIstvamasya dhanasyeti) /
tasmiMshcApahnavAne AhuH parashumasmai tapateti shodhayatvAtmAnamiti /
sa yadi tasya stainyasya kartA bavati bahishcApahnate sa evaMbhUtastata evAnR^itamanyathAbhUtaM santamanyathA'mAnaM kurute sa tathAnR^itAbhisandho 'nR^itenA'tmAnamantardhAya vyavahitaM kR^itvA parashuM taptaM mohAtpratigR^ihrAti sa dahyate 'tha hanyate rAjapuruShaiH svakR^itenAnR^itAbhisandhidoSheNa //1 //

START ChUp 6,16.2

#<atha yadi tasyAkartA bhavati |
tata eva satyam AtmAnaM kurute |

atha mucyate || ChUp_6,16.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_6,16.2 atha yadi tasya karmaNo 'kartA bhavati tata eva satyamAtmAnaM kurute sa satyena tayA stainyAkartR^itayA'tmAnamantardhAya parashuM taptaM pratigR^ihNAti sa satyAbhisandhaH sanna dahyate satyavyavadhAnAdatha mucyate ca mR^iShAbhiyoktR^ibhyaH /

START ChUp 6,16.3

#<sa yathA tatra nAdAhyeta |
