ChUpBh_6,16.3 sa yathA satyAbhisandhastaptaparashugrahaNakarmaNi satyavyavahitahastatalatvAnnAdAhyeta na dahyetetyetadevaM sadbrahmasatyAbhisandhItarayoH sharIrapAtakAle ca tulyAyAM satsampattau vidvAnsatsampadya na punarvyAghradevAdidehagrahaNAyA'vartate /
avidvAMstu vikArAnR^itAbhisandhaH punarvyAghrAdibhAvaM devatAdibhAvaM vA yathAkarma yathAshrutaM pratipadyate /
yadAtmAbhisandhyanabhisandhikR^ite mokShabandhane yacca mUlaM jagato yadAyatanA yatpratiShThAshca sarvAH prajA yadAtmakaM ca sarvaM yaccAjamamR^itamabhayaM shivamadvitIyaM tatsatyaM sa AtmA tavAtastattvamasi he shvetaketo ityuktArthamasakR^idvAkyam /

kaH punarasau shvetaketustvaMshabdArthaH /
yo 'haM shvetaketuruddAlakasya putra iti vedA'tmAnamAdeshaM shrutvA matvA vij~nAya cAshrutamamatamavij~nAtaM vij~nAtuM pitaraM papraccha kathaM nu bhagavaH sa Adesho bavatIti sa eSho 'dhikR^itaH shrotA mantA vij~nAtA tejobannamayaM kAryakAraNasaN^ghAtaM praviShTA paraiva devatA nAmasvarUpavyAkaraNAyA'darsha iva puruShaH sUryAduriva jalAdau pratibodhitastattvamasItidR^iShTAntairhetubhishca tatpiturasya ha kiloktaM sadevAhamasmIti vijaj~nau vij~nAtavAn /
dvirvacanamadhyAyaparisamAptyartham /
kiM punaratra ShaShThe vAkyapramANena janitaM phalam?Atmani kartR^itvabhoktR^itvayoradhikR^itatvavij~nAnanivR^ittistasya phalaM yaM vayamavocAma tvaMshabdavAcyamarthaM shrotuM mantuM cAdhikR^itamavij~nAtavij~nAnaphalArtham /
prAkcaitasmAdvij~nAnAdahamevaM kariShyAmyagnihotrAdIni karmANyahamatrAdhikR^itaH /
eShAM ca karmaNAM phalamihAmutra ca bhokShye kR^iteShu vA karmasu kR^itakartavyaH syAmityevaM kartR^itvabhoktR^itvayoradhikR^ito 'smItyAtmani yadvij~nAnamabhUttattasya yatsajjagato mUlamekamevAdvitIyaM tattvamasItyanena vAkyena pratibuddhasya nivartate /
virodhAt /
na hyekasminnadvitIya AtmanyayamahamasmIti vij~nAte mamedamanyadanena kartavyamidaM kR^itvAsya phalaM bhokShya iti vA bhedavij~nAnamupapadyate /
tasmAtsatsatyAdvitIyAtmavij~nAne vikArAnR^itajIvAtmavij~nAnaM nivartata iti yuktam /
nanu tattvamasItyatra tvaMshabdavAcyer'the sadbuddhirAdhitsyate yathA'dityamana AdiShu brahmAdibuddhiH /
yathA ca loke pratimAdiShu viShNvAdibuddhistadvannatu sadeva tvamiti, yadi sadeva shvetaketuH syAtkathamAtmAnaM na vijAnIyAdyena tasmai tattvamasItyupadishyate /
na /
AdityAdivAkyavailakShaNyAt /
Adityo brahmetyAdAvitishabdavyavadhAnAnna sAkShAdbrahmatvaM gamyate /
rUpAdimattvAccA'dityAdInAmAkAshamanasoshcetishabdavyavadhAnAdevAbrahmatvamiha tu sata eveha praveshaM darshayitvA tattvamasIti niraN^kushaM sadAtmabhAvamupadishati /
nanu parAkramAdiguNaH siMho 'si tvamitivattattvamasIti syAt /
na /
mR^idAdivatsadekamevAdvitIyaM satyamityupadeshAt /
na copacAravij~nAnAttasya tAvadeva ciramiti satsampattirUpadishyeta /
mR^iShAtvAdupacAravij~nAnasya /
tvamindro 'si yama itivat /
nApi stutiranupAsyatvAcchvetaketoH /
nApi sacchvetaketutvopadeshena stUyeta /
na hi rAjA dAsastvamiti stutyaH syAt /
nApi sataH sarvAtmana ekadeshanirodho yuktastattvamasIti deshAdhipateriva grAmAdhyakShastvamiti /
na cAnyA gatiriha sadAtmatvopadeshAdarthAntarabhUtA sambhavati /
nanu sadasmItibuddhimAtramiha kartavyatayA codyate na tvaj~nAtaM sadasIti j~nApyata iti cet /
nanvasminpakShe 'pyashrutaM shrutaM bhavatItyAdyanupapannam /
na, sadasmItibuddhividheH stutyarthatvAt /
na, AcAryavAnpuruSho veda tasya tAvadeva ciramityupadeshAt /
yadi hi sadasmIti buddhimAtraM kartavyatayA vidhIyate na tu tvaMshabdavAcyasya sadrUpatvameva tadA nA'cAryavAnvedeti j~nAnopAyopadesho vAcyaH syAt /
yathAgnihotraM juhuyAdityevamAdiShvarthaprAptamevA'cAryavattvamiti tadvat /

sadAtmatattve 'vij~nAte 'pi sakR^idbuddhimAtrakaraNe mokShaprasaN^gAt /
na ca tattvamasItyukte nAhaM saditipramANavAkyajanitA buddhIrnivartayituM shakyA notpanneti vA shakyaM vaktum /
sarvopaniShadvAkyAnAM tatparatayaivopakShayAt /
yathAgnihotrAdividhijanitAgnihotrAdikartavyatAbuddhInAmatathArthatvamanutpannatvaM vA na shakyate vaktuM tadvat /
yattUktaM sadAtmA sannAtmAnaM kathaM na jAnIyAditi /
nAsau doShaH /
kAryakaraNasaN^ghAtavyatirikto 'haM jIvaH kartA bhoktetyapi svabhAvataH prANinAM vij~nAnAdarshanAtkisu tasya sadAtmavij~nAnam /

tadvattasyApi dehAdiShvAtmabuddhitvAnna syAtsadAtmavij~nAnam /
tasmAdvikArAnR^itAdhikR^itajIvAtmavij~nAnanivartakamevedaM vAkyaM tattvamasIti siddhamiti //3 // //

START ChUp 7,1.1

#<adhIhi bhagava iti hopasasAda sanatkumAraM nAradaH |

ChUpBh_7,1.1
paramArthantattvopadeshapradhAnaparaH ShaShTho 'dhyAyaH sadAtmaikatvanirNayaparatayaivopayuktaH /
na sator'vAgvikAralakShaNAni tattvAni nirdiShTAnItyatastAni nAmAdIni prANAntAni krameNa nirdishya taddvAreNApi bhUmAkhyaM niratishayaM tattvaM nirdekShyAmIti shAkhAcandradarshanavaditInaM saptamaM prapAThakamArabhate /
anirdiShTeShu hi sator'vAktattveShu sanmAtre ca nirdiShTe 'nyadapyavij~nAtaM syAdityAshaN^kA kasyacitsyAtsA mA bhUditi vA tAni nirdidikShati /

athavA sopAnArohaNavatsthUlAdArabhya sUkShmaM sUkShamataM ca buddhiviShayaM j~nApayitvA tadatirikte svArAjye 'bhiShekShyAmIti nAmAdIni nirdidikShati /
athavA nAmAdyuttarottaravishiShTAni tattvAnyatitarAM ca teShAmutkR^iShTatamaM bhUmAkhyaM tattvamiti tatstutyarthaM nAmAdInAM krameNopanyAsaH /

AkhyAyikA tu paravidyAstutyarthA /
katham /
nArado devarShiH kR^itakartavyaH sarvavidyo 'pi sannanAtmaj~natvAcchushocaiva kimu vaktavyamanyo 'lpavijjanturakR^itapuNyAtishayo 'kR^itArtha iti /
athavA nAnyadAtmaj~nAnAnniratishayashreyaH sAdhanamastItyetatpradarshanArthaM sanatkumAranAradAkhyAyikA'rabhyate /
yena sarvavij~nAnasAdhanashaktisampannasyApi nAradasya devarSheH shreyo na babhUva yenottamAbhijanavidyAvR^ittasAdhanashaktisampattinimittAbhi mAnaM hitvA prAkR^itapuruShavatsanatkumAramupasasAda shreyaHsAdhanaprAptaye 'taH prakhyApitaM bhavati niratishayaprAptisAdhanatvamAtmavidyAyA iti /
adhIhyadhIShva bhagavA bha vinniti kilopasasAda /
adhIhi bhagava iti mantraH /
sanatkumAraM yogIshvaraM brahmiShThaM nArada upasannavAn /
taM nyAyata upasannaM hovAca yadAtmaviShaye kiJNcidvettha tena tatprakhyApanena mAmupasIdedamahaM jAna iti tato 'haM bhavato vij~nAnAtte tubyamUrdhvaM vakShyAmItyuktavati sa hovAca nAradaH //1 //

START ChUp 7,1.2

#<R^igvedaM bhagavo 'dhyemi yajurvedaM sAmavedam AtharvaNaM caturtham itihAsapurANaM paJNcamaM vedAnAM vedaM pitryaM rAshiM daivaM nidhiM vAkovAkyam ekAyanaM devavidyAM brahmavidyAM bhUtavidyAM kShatravidyAM nakShatravidyAM sarpadevajanavidyAm etad bhagavo 'dhyemi || ChUp_7,1.2 ||>#

ChUpBh_7,1.2 R^igvedaM bhagavo 'dhyemi smarAmi yadvettheti vij~nAnasya pR^iShTatvAt /
tathA yajurvedaM sAmavedamAtharvaNaM caturthaM vedaM vedashabdasya prakR^itatvAditihAsapurANaM paJNcamaM vedaM vedAnAM bhAratapaJNcamAnAM vedaM vyAkaraNamityarthaH /

vyAkaraNena hi padAdivibhAgasha R^igvedAdayo j~nAyante /
pitryaM shrAddhakalpam /
kAshiM gaNitam /
daivamutpAtaj~nAnam /

START ChUp 7,1.3

#<so 'haM bhagavo mantravid evAsmi nAtmavit |
shrutaM hy eva me bhagavaddR^ishebhyas tarati shokam Atmavid iti |
so 'haM bhagavaH shocAmi |
taM mA bhagavA¤ chokasya pAraM tArayatv iti |
taM hovAca yad vai kiMcaitad adhyagIShThA nAmaivaitat || ChUp_7,1.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,1.3 so 'haM bhagava etatsarvaM jAnannapi mantravidevAsmi shabdArthamAtravij~nAnavAnevAsmItyarthaH /
sarvo hi shabdo 'bhidhAnamAtramabhidhAnaM ca sarvaM mantreShvantarbhavati /
mantravidevAsmi mantravitkarmavidityarthaH /
'mantreShu karmANI'ti hi vakShyati nA'tmavinnA'tmAnaM vedbhi /
nanvAtmApi mantraiH prakAshyata eveti kathaM mantraviccennA'tmavit /
na /
abhidhAnAbhidheyabhedasya vikAratvAt /
na ca vikAra AtmeShyate /
nanvAtmApyAtmashabdenAbhidhIyate /
na"yato vAco nivartante" /
"yatra nAnya pashyati"ityAdishruteH /
kathaM tarhyA'tmaivAdhastAt' 'sa Atme'tyAdishabdA AtmAnaM pratyAyayanti /
naiSha doShaH /
dehavati pratyagAtmani bhedaviShaye prayujyamAnaH shabdo dehAdInAmAtmatve pratyAkhyAyamAne yatparishiShTaM sadavAcyamapi pratyAyayati /
yathA sarAjikAyAM dR^ishyamAnAyAM senAyAM chatradhvajapatAkAdivyavahite 'dR^ishyamAne 'pi rAjanyeSha rAjA dR^ishyata iti bhavati shabdaprayogastatra ko 'sau rAjeti rAjavisheShanirUpaNAyAM dR^ishyamAnetarapratyAkhyAne 'nyasminnadR^ishyamAne 'pi rAjani rAjapratItirbhavettadvat /
tasmAtsohaM mantravitkarmavidevAsmi karmakAryaM ca sarvaM vikAra iti vikAraj~na evAsmi nA'tmavinnA'tmaprakR^itisvarUpaj~na ityarthaH /
ata evokta"mAcAryavAnpuruSho vede"ti /
"yato vAco nivartante"ityAdishrutibhyashca /
shrutamAgamaj~nAnamastyeva hi yasmAnme mama bhagavaddR^ishebhyo yuShmatsadR^ishebhyastaratyatikrAmati shokaM manastApamakR^itArthabuddhitAmAtmavidityataH /
so 'hamanAtmavittvAddhe bhagavaH shocAmyakR^itArthabuddhyA santapye sarvadA taM mA mAM shokasya shokasAgarasya pAramantaM bhagavAMstArayatvAtmaj~nAnoDupena kR^itArthabuddhimApAdayatvabhayaM gamayatvityarthaH /
tamevamuktavantaM hovAca yadvai kiJNcaitadadhyagIShThA adhItavAnasi /
adhyayanena tadarthaj~nAnamupalakShyate j~nAtavAnasItyetannAmaivaitat /
"vAcA'rambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyam"iti shruteH //3 //

ChUpBh_7,4.1 saMkalpo vAva manaso bhUyAn /

ChUpBh_7,4.2 tAni ha vA etAni mana AdIni saMkalpaikAyanAni saMkalpa eko 'yanaM gamanaM pralayo yeShAM tAni saMkalpaikAyanAni saMkalpAtmakAnyutpattau saMkalpe pratiShThitAni sthitau samakÊpatAM saMkalpaM kR^itavatyAviva hi dyaushca pR^ithivI ca dyAvApR^ithivyau nishcale lakShyete /

START ChUp 7,7.2

#<sa yo vij~nAnaM brahmety upAste |
vij~nAnavato vai sa lokA¤ j~nAnavato 'bhisidhyati |

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya paJNcadashaH khaNDaH>#

7.16.1

#<eSha tu vA ativadati yaH satyenAtivadati so 'haM bhagavaH satyenAti-># #<vadAnIti satyaM tveva vijij~nAsitavyamiti satyaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti //1//>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,16.1 sa eSha nAradaH sarvAtishayaM prANaM svamAtmAnaM sarvAtmAnaM shrutvA nAtaH paramastItyupararAma /
na pUrvavatkimasti bhagavaH prANAdbhUya iti papraccha /
yatastamevaM vikArAnR^itabrahmavij~nAnena parituShTamakR^itArthaM paramArthasatyAtivAdinamAtmAnaM manyamAnaM yogyaM shiShyaM mithyAgrahavisheShAdvipracyAvayannAha bhagavAnsanatkumAraH /
eSha tu vA ativadati yamahaM vakShyAmi na prANavidativAdI paramArthataH /
nAmAdyapekShaM tu tasyAtivAditvam /
yastu bhUmAkhyaM sarvAtikrAntaM tattvaM paramArthasatyaM veda so 'tivAdItyata Aha-eSha tu vA ativadati yaH sateyana paramArthasatyavij~nAnavattayAtivadati /
so 'haM tvAM prapanno bhagavansatyenAtivadAni tathAmAM niyunaktu bhagavAnyathAhaM satyenAtivadAnItyabhiprAyaH /
yadyevaM satyenAtivaditumicchasi satyameva tu tAvadvijij~nAsitavyamityukta Aha nAradaH /
tathAstu tarhi satya bhagavo vijij~nAse visheSheNa j~nAtumiccheyaM tvatto 'hamiti //1//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya ShoDashaH khaNDaH>#


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 7,17.1

#<yadA vai vijAnAty atha satyaM vadati |
nAvijAnan satyaM vadati |
vijAnann eva satyaM vadati |
vij~nAnaM tv eva vijij~nAsitavyam iti |
vij~nAnaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti || ChUp_7,17.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,17.1 yadA vai satyaM paramArthato vijAnAtIdaM paramArthaH satyamiti, tato 'nR^itaM vikArajAtaM vAcArambhaNaM hitvA sarvavikArAvasthaM sadevaikaM satyamiti tadevAtha vadati yadvadati /
nanu vikAro 'pi satyameva /
"nAmarUpe satyaM tAbhya mayaM prANashchannaH" /
"prANA vai satyaM teShAmeSha satyam"iti shrutyantarAt /
satyamuktaM satyatvaM shrutyantare vikArasya na tu paramArthApekShamuktaM kiM tarhIndriyaviShayatvApekShaM sacca tyacceti satyamityuktaM taddvAreNa ca paramArthasatyasyopalabdhirvivakShiteti /
prANA vai satyaM teShAmeSha satyamiti coktam /
ihApi tadiShTameva /
iha tu praNaviShayAtparamArthasatyavij~nAnAbhimAnAdvyutthApya nAradaM yatsadeva satyaM paramArthato bhUmAkhyaM tadvij~nApayiShyAmItyeSha visheShato vivakShitor'thaH /
nAvijAnansatyaM vadati yastvavijAnanvadati so 'gnyAdishabdenAgnyadInparamArthasadrUpAnmanyamAno vadati na tu te rUpatrayavyatirekeNa paramArthaH santi /
tathA tAnyapi rUpANi sadapekShayA naiva santItyato nAvijAnansatyaM vadati /
vijAnanneva satyaM vadati /
na ca tatsatyavij~nAnamavijij~nAsitamaprArthitaM j~nAyata ityAha-vij~nAnaM tveva vijij~nAsitavyamiti /
yadyevaM vij~nAnaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti /
evaM satyAdInAM cottarottarANAM karotyantAnAM pUrvapUrvahetutvaM vyAkhyeyam //1//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya saptadashaH khaNDaH>#


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 7,18.1

#<yadA vai  manute 'tha vijAnAti |
nAmatvA vijAnAti |
matvaiva vijAnAti |
matis tv eva vijij~nAsitavyeti |
matiM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti || ChUp_7,18.1 ||>#

START ChUp 7,20.1

nAnistiShTha¤ chraddadhAti |

START ChUp 7,21.1

#<yadA vai karoty atha nistiShThati |
nAkR^itvA nistiShThati |
kR^itvaiva nistiShThati |
kR^itis tv eva vijij~nAsitavyeti |
kR^itiM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti || ChUp_7,21.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,21.1 yadA vai karoti /
kR^itirindriyasaMyamashcittaikAgratAkaraNaM ca /
satyAM hi tasyAM niShThAdIni yathoktAni bhavanti vij~nAnAvasAnAni //1//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasyaikaviMshaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 7,22.1

#<yadA vai sukhaM labhate 'tha karoti |
nAsukhaM labdhvA karoti |
sukham eva labdhvA karoti |
sukhaM tv eva vijij~nAsitavyam iti |
sukhaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti || ChUp_7,22.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,22.1 sApi kR^itiryadA sukhaM labhate sukhaM niratishayaM vakShyamANaM labdhavyaM mayeti manyate tadA bhavatItyarthaH /
yathA dR^iShTaphalasukhA kR^itistathehApi nAsukhaM labdhvA karoti /
bhaviShyadapi phalaM labdhvetyucyate /
taduddishya pravR^ittyupapatteH /
athedAnIM kR^ityAdiShUttarottareShu satsu satyaM svayameva pratibhAsata iti na tadvij~nAnAya pR^ithagyatnaH kArya iti prAptaM tata idamucyate /
sukhaM tveva vijij~nAsitavyamityAdi /
sukhaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa ityabhimukhIbhUtAyA'ha //1//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya dvAviMshaH khaNDaH>#


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 7,23.1

#<yo vai bhUmA tat sukham |
nAlpe sukham asti |
bhUmaiva sukham |
bhUmA tv eva vijij~nAsitavya iti |
bhUmAnaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti || ChUp_7,23.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,23.1 yo vai bhUmA mahanniratishayaM bahviti paryAyAstatsukham /
tator'vAksAtishayatvAdalpam /
atastasminnalpe sukhaM nAsti /
alpasyAdhikatR^iShNAhetutvAt /
tR^iShNA ca duHkhabIjaM /
na hi duHkhabIjaM sukhaM dR^iShTaM jvarAdi loke /
tasmAdyuktaM nAlpe sukhamastIti /
ato bhUmaiva sukham /
tR^iShNAdiduHkhabIjatvAsaMbhavAdbhUmnaH //1//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya trayoviMshaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 7,24.1

#<yatra nAnyat pashyati nAnyac chR^iNoti nAnyad vijAnAti sa bhUmA |
atha yatrAnyat pashyaty anyac chR^iNoty anyad vijAnAti tad alpam |
yo vai bhUmA tad amR^itam |
atha yad alpaM tan martyam |
sa bhagavaH kasmin pratiShThita iti |
sve mahimni yadi vA na mahimnIti || ChUp_7,24.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,24.1 kiMlakShaNo 'sau bhUmetyAha-yatra yasminbhUmni tattve nAnyaddraShTavyamanyena karaNena draShTAnyo vibhakto dR^ishyAtpashyati /
tathA nAnyacchR^iNoti /
nAmarUpayorevAntarbhAvAdviShayabhedasya tadgrAhakayoreveha darshanashravaNayorgrahaNamanyeShAM copalakShaNArthatvena /
mananaM cAtroktaM draShTavyaM nAnyanmanuta iti /
prAyasho mananapUrvakatvAdvij~nAnasya /
tathA nAnyadvijAnAti /
evaMlakShaNo yaH sa bhUmA /
kimatra prasidrAnyadarshanAbhAvo bhUmnyucyate nAnyatpashyatItyAdinA, athAnyanna pashyatyAtmAnaM pashyatItyetat /
kiJNcAtaH /
yadyanyadarshanAdyabhAvamAtramityucyate tadA dvaitasaMvyavahAravilakShaNo bhUmetyuktaM bhavati /
athAnyadrashanavisheShapratiShedhenA'tmAnaM pashyatItyucyate tadaikasminneva kriyAkArakaphalabhedo 'bhyupagato bhavet /
yadyevaM ko doShaH syAt /
nanvayameva doShaH saMsArAnivR^ittiH /
kriyAkArakaphalabhedo hi saMsAra iti /
Atmaikatva eva kriyAkArakaphalabhedaH saMsAravilakShaNa iti cet /
na /
Atmano nirvisheShaikatvAbhyupagame darshanAdikriyAkArakaphalabhedAbhyupagamasya shabdamAtratvAt /
anyadarshanAdyabhAvoktipakShe 'pi yatretyanyanna pashyatIti ca visheShaNe anarthake syAtAmiti cet /
dR^ishyate hi loke yatra shUnye gR^ihe 'nyanna pashyatItyukte stambhAdInAtmAnaM ca na na pashyatIti gamyate /
evamihApIti cet /
na /
tattvamasItyekatvopadeshAdadhikaraNAdhikartavyabhedAnupapatteH /
tathA sadekamevAdvitIyaM satyamiti ShaShThe nirdhAritatvAt /
"adR^ishye 'nAtmye" "na saMdR^ishe tiShThati rUpamasya" "vij~nAtAramare kena vijAnIyAt"ityAdishrutibhyaH svAtmani darshanAdyanupapattiH /
yatreti visheShaNamanarthakaM prAptamiti cet /
na /
avidyAkR^itabhedApekShatvAt /
yathA satyekatvAdvitIyatvabuddhiM prakR^itAmapekShya sadekamevAdvitIyamiti saMkhyAdyanarhamapyucyate /
evaM bhUmnyekasminneva yatreti visheShaNam /
avidyAvasthAyAmanyadarshanAnuvAdena ca bhUmnastadabhAvatvalakShaNasya vivakShitatvAnnAnyatpashyatIti visheShaNam /
tasmAtsaMsAravyavahAro bhUmni nAstIti samudAyArthaH /
atha yatrAvidyAviShaye 'nyo 'nyenAnyatpashyatIti tadalpamavidyAkAlabhAvItyarthaH /
yathA svapnadR^ishyaM vastu prAk prabodhAttatkAlabhAvIti tadvat /
tata eva tanmartyaM vinAshi svapnavastuvadeva tadviparoto bhUmA yastadamR^itam /
tacchabdo 'mR^itatvaparaH /
sa tarhyevaMlakShaNo bhUmA he bhagavankasminpratiShThita ityuktavantaM nAradaM pratyAha sanatkimAraH /
sve mahimnIti sva AtmIye mahimni mAhAtmye vibhUtau pratiShThito bhUmA /
yadi pratiShThAmicchasi kvacidyadi vA paramArthameva pR^icchasi na mahimnyapi pratiShThita iti brUmaH /
apratiShThito 'nAshrito bhUmA kvacidapItyarthaH //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 7,24.2

#<go 'shvam iha mahimety AcakShate hastihiraNyaM dAsabhAryaM kShetrANy AyatanAnIti |
nAham evaM bravImi |
bravImIti hovAca |
anyo hy anyasmin pratiShThita iti || ChUp_7,24.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,24.2 yadi svamahimni pratiShThito bhUmA kathaM tarhyapratiShTha ucyate /
shR^iNu /
go 'shvAdIha mahimetyAcakShate /
gAvashcAshvAshca go 'shvaM dvandvaikavadbhAvaH /
sarvatra gavAshvAdi mahimeti prasiddhaM tadAshritastatpratiShThashcaitro bhavati, yathA nAhamevaM svato 'nyaM mahimAnamAshrito bhUmA caitravaditi bravImyatra hetutvenAnyo hyanyasminpratiShThita iti vyavahitena sambandhaH /
kintvevaM bravImIti hovAca-sa evetyAdi //2//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya caturviMshaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 7,25.1

#<sa evAdhastAt sa upariShTAt sa pashcAt sa purastAt sa dakShiNataH sa uttarataH |
sa evedaM sarvam iti |
athAto 'haMkArAdesha eva |
aham evAdhastAd aham upariShTAd ahaM pashcAd ahaM purastAd ahaM dakShiNato 'ham uttarato 'ham evedaM sarvam iti || ChUp_7,25.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,25.1 kasmAtpunaH kvacinna pratiShThita ityucyate /
yasmAtsa eva bhUmAdhastAnna tadvyatirekeNAnyadvidyate yasminpratiShThitaH syAt /
tathopariShTAdityAdi samAnam /
sati bhUmno 'nyasminbhUmA hi pratiShThitaH syAnna tu tadasti /
sa eva tu sarvam /
atastasmAdasau na kvacitpratiShThitaH /
yatra nAnyatpashyatItyadhikaraNAdhikartavyatAnirdeshAtsa evAdhastAditi ca parokShanirdeshAddraShTarjIvAdanyobhUmA syAdityAshaN^kA kasyacinmA bhUdityathAto 'nantaramahaN^kArAdesho 'haN^kAreNA'dishyata ityahaN^kArAdeshaH /
draShTurananyatvadarshanArthaM bhUmaiva nirdishyate 'haN^kAreNAhamevAdhastAdityAdinA //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 7,25.2

#<athAta AtmAdesha eva |
AtmaivAdhastAd AtmopariShTAd AtmA pashcAd AtmA purastAd AtmA dakShiNata Atmottarata AtmaivedaM sarvam iti |
sa vA eSha evaM pashyann evaM manvAna evaM vijAnann Atmaratir AtmakrIDa Atmamithuna AtmAnandaH sa svarAD bhavati |
tasya sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati |
atha ye 'nyathAto vidur anyarAjAnas te kShayyalokA bhavanti |
teShAM sarveShu lokeShv akAmacAro bhavati || ChUp_7,25.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,25.2 ahaN^kAreNa dehAdisaMghAto 'pyAdishyate 'vivekibhirityatastadAshaN^kA mA bhUdityathAnantaramAtmAdesha Atmanaiva kevalena satsvarUpeNa shuddhenA'dishyate /
Atmaiva sarvataH sarvamityevamekamajaM sarvato vyomavatpUrNamanyashUnyaM pashyansa vA eSha vidvAnmananavij~nAnAbhyAmAtmaratirAtmanyeva ratI ramaNaM yasya so 'yamAtmaratiH /
tathA'tmakrIDaH /
dehamAtrasAdhanA ratirbAhyasAdhanA krIDA /
loke srIbhiH sakhibhishca krIDatIti darshanAt na tathA viduShaH kiM tarhyAtmavij~nAnanimittamevobhayaM bhavatItyarthaH /
mithunaM dvaMndvajanitaM sukhaM tadapi dvandvanirapekShaM yasya viduShaH /
tathA'tmAnandaH shabdAdinimitta Anando 'viduShAM na tathAsya viduShaH kiM tarhyAtmanimittameva sarvaM sarvadA sarvaprakAreNa ca dehajIvitabhogAdinimittabAhyavastunirapekSha ityarthaH /
sa evaMlakShaNo vidvAJNjIvanneva svArAjye 'bhiShiktaH patite 'pi dehe svarADeva bhavati /
yata evaM bhavati tata eva tasya sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati /
prANAdiShu pUrvabhUmiShu tatrAsyeti tAvanmAtraparicchinnakAmacAratvamuktamanrAjatvaM cArthaprAptaM sAtishayatvAdyathAprAptasvArAjyakAmacAratvAnuvAdena tatannivR^ittirihocyate sa svarADityAdinA /
atha punarye 'nyathAta uktadarshanAdanyathA vaiparItyena yathoktameva vA samyaÇna viduste 'nyarAjAno bhavanti anyaH paro rAjA svAmI yeShAM te 'nyarAjAnaste /
kiJNca kShayyo loko yeShAM te kShayylokAH /
bhedadarshanasyAlpaviShayatvAdalpaM ca tanmartyamityavocAma /
tasmAdye dvaitadarshinaste kShayyalokAH svadarshanAnurUpyeNaiva bhavantyata eva teShAM sarveShu lokeShvakAmacAro bhavati //2//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi saptamAdhyAyasya paJNcaviMshaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 7,26.1

#<tasya ha vA etasyaivaM pashyata evaM manvAnasyaivaM vijAnata AtmataH prANa Atmata AshAtmataH smara Atmata AkAsha Atmatas teja Atmata Apa Atmata AvirbhAvatirobhAvAv Atmato 'nnam Atmato balam Atmato vij~nAnam Atmato dhyAnam Atmatash cittam AtmataH saMkalpa Atmato mana Atmato vAg Atmato nAmAtmato mantrA AtmataH karmANy Atmata evedaM sarvam iti || ChUp_7,26.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,26.1 tasya ha vA etasyetyAdi svArAjyaM prAptasya prakR^itasya viduSha ityarthaH /
prAksadAtmavij~nAnAtsvAtmano 'nyasmAtsataH prANAdernAmAntasyotpattipralayAvabhUtAM sadAtmAvij~nAne tu satIdAnIM svAtmata eva saMvR^ittau tathA sarvo 'pyanyo vyavahAra Atmata eva viduShaH //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 7,26.2

#<tad eSha shlokaH |
na pashyo mR^ityuM pashyati na rogaM nota duHkhatAm |
sarvaM ha pashyaH pashyati sarvam Apnoti sarvashaH |
iti |
sa ekadhA bhavati tridhA bhavati paJNcadhA |
saptadhA navadhA caiva punash caikAdasha smR^itaH |
shataM ca dasha caikash ca sahasrANi ca viMshatiH |
AhArashuddhau sattvashuddhiH |
sattvashuddhau dhruvA smR^itiH |
smR^itilambhe sarvagranthInAM vipramokShaH |
tasmai mR^iditakaShAyAya tamasas pAraM darshayati bhagavAn sanatkumAraH |
taM skanda ity AcakShate || ChUp_7,26.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_7,26.2 kiJNca tadetasminnartha eSha shloko mantro 'pi bhavati /
na pashyaH pashyatIti pashyo yathoktadarshI vidvAnityarthaH /
mR^ityuM maraNaM rogaM jvarAdi duHkhatAM duHkhabhAvaM cApi na pashyati /
sarvaM ha sarvameva sa pashyaH pashyatyAtmAnameva sarvaM tataH sarvamApnoti sarvashaH sarvaprakArairiti /
kiJNca sa vidvAnprAksR^iShTiprabhedAdekadhaiva bhavatyekadhaiva ca saMsridhAdibhedairanantabhedaprakAro bhavati sR^iShTikAle /
punaH saMhArakAle mUlameva svaM pAramArthakamekadhAbhAvaM pratipadyate svatantra eveti vidyAM phalena prarocayanstauti /
athedAnIM yathoktAyA vidyAyAH samyagavabhAsakAraNaM mukhAvabhAsakAraNasyevA'darshasya vishuddhikAraNaM sAdhanamupadishyate-AhArashuddhau /
Ahriyata ityAhAraH shabdAdiviShayavij~nAnaM bhokturbhogAyA'hriyate vishuddhikAraNaM sAdhanamupadishyate-AhArashuddhau /
Ahriyata ityAharaH shabdAdiviShayavij~nAnaM bhokturbhogAyA'hriyate tasya viShayopalabdhilakShaNasya vij~nAnasya shuddhirAhArashuddhI rAgadveShamohadoShairasaMsR^iShTaM viShayavij~nAnamityarthaH /
tasyAmAhArAshuddhau satyAM tadvato 'ntaHkaraNasya sattvasya shuddhirnairmalyaM bhavati /
sattvashuddhau ca satyAM yathAvagate bhUmAtmani dhruvAvicchinnA smR^itiravismaramaM bhavati /
tasyAM ca labdhAyAM smR^itilambhe sati sarveShAmavidyAkR^itAnarthapAsharUpANAmanekajanmAntarAnubhavabhAvanAkaThinIkR^itAnAM hR^idayAkShayANAM granthInAM vipramokSho visheSheNa pramokShaNaM vinAsho bhavatIti /
yata etaduttarottaraM yathoktamAhArashuddhimUlaM tasmAtsA kAryetyarthaH /
sarvaM shAsrArthamasheShata uktvA'khyAyikAmupasaMharati shrutiH-tasmai mR^iditakaShAyAya vArkShAdiriva kaShAyo rAgadveShAdidoShaH sattvasya raJNjanArUpatvAtsa j~nAnavairAgyAbhyAsarUpakShAreNa kShAlito mR^idito vinAshito yasya nAradasya tasmai yogyAya mR^iditakaShAyAya tamaso 'vidyAlakShaNAtpAraM paramArthatattvaM darshayati darshitavAnityarthaH /
ko 'sau, bhagavAn-"utpattiM pralayaM caiva bhUtAnAmAgatiM gatim /
vetti vidyAmavidyAM ca sa vAcyo bhagavAniti //
" evandharmA sanatkumAraH /
tameva sanatkumAraM devaM skanda ityAcakShate kathayanti tadvidaH /
dvirvacanamadhyAyaparisamAptyartham //2 // //

START ChUp 8,1.1

#<atha yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma daharo 'sminn antarAkAsaH |
tasmin yad antas tad anveShTavyaM tad vAva vijij~nAsitavyam iti || ChUp_8,1.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,1.1
yadyapi digdeshakAlAdibhedashUnyaM brahma sadekamevAdvitIyamAtmaivedaM sarvamiti ShaShThasaptamayoradhigataM tathApIha mandabuddhInAM digdeshAdibhedavadvastvityevaM bhAvitA buddhirna shakyate sahasA paramArthaviShayA kartumityanadhigamya ca brahma na puruShArthasiddhiriti tadadhigamAya hR^idayapuNDarIkadesha upadeShTavyaH /
yadyapi satsamyakpratyayaikaviShayA kartumityAnadhigamya ca brahma na puruShArthasiddhiriti tadadhigamAya hR^idayapuNDarIkadesha upadeShTavyaH /
yadyapi satsamyakpratyayaikaviShayaM nirguNaM cA'tmatattvaM tathApi mandabuddhInAM guNavattvasyeShTatvAtsatyakAmAdiguNavattvaM ca vaktavyam /
tathA yadyapi brahmavidAM stryAdiviShayebhyaH svayamevoparamo bhavati tathApyanekajanmaviShayasevAbhyAsajanitA viShayaviShayA tR^iShNA na sahasA nivartayituM shakyata iti brahmacaryAdisAdhanavisheSho vidhAtavyaH /
tathA yadyapyAtmaikatvavidAM gantR^igamanagantavyAbhAvAdavidyAvisheShasthitinimittakShaye gagana iva vidyududbhUta iva vAyurdagdhendhana ivAgniH svAtmanyeva nivR^ittistathApi gantR^igamanAdivAsitabuddhInAM hR^idayadeshaguNavishiShTabrahmopAsakAnAM mUrdhanyayA nADyA gatirvaktavyetyaShTamaH prapAThaka Arabhyate /
digdeshaguNagatiphalabhedashUnyaM hi paramArthasadadvayaM brahmamandabuddhInAmasadiva pratibhAti /
sanmArgasthAstAvadbhavantu tataH shanaiH paramArthasadapi grAhayiShyAmIti manyate shrutiH /
athAnantaraM yadidaM vakShyamANaM daharamalpaM puNDarIkaM puNDarIkasadR^ishaM veshmeva veshma dvArapAlAdimattvAt /
asminbrahmapure brahmaNaH parasya puraM rAj~no 'nekaprakR^itimadyathApuraM tathedamanekendriyamanobuddhibhiH svAmyarthakAribhiryuktamiti brahmapuram /
pure ca veshma rAj~no yathA tathA tasminbrahmapure sharIre daharaM veshma brahmaNa upalabdhyadhiShThAnamityarthaH /
yathA viShNoH shAlagrAmaH /
asminhi svavikArashiN^ge dehe nAmarUpavyAkaraNAya praviShTaM sadAkhyaM braÇma jIvenA'tmanetyuktam /
tasmAdasminhR^idayapuNDarIke veshmanyupasaMhR^itakaraNairbAhyaviShayaviraktairvisheShato brahmacaryasatyasAdhanAbhyAM yuktervakShyamANaguNavaddhyAyamAnairbrahmopalabhyata iti prakaraNArthaH /
daharo 'lpataro 'smindahare veshmani veshmano 'lpatvAttadantarvartino 'lpataratvaM veshmanaH /
antarAkAsha AkAshAkhyaM brahma /
AkAsho vai nAmeti hi vakShyati /
AkAsha ivAsharIratvAtsUkShmatvasarvagatatvasAmAnyAcca /
tasminnAkAshAkhye yadantarmadhye tadanveShTavyam /
tadvAva tadeva ca visheSheNa jij~nAsitavyaM gurvAshrayashravaNAdyupAyairanviShya ca sAkShAtkaraNIyamityarthaH //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,1.2

#<taM ced brUyur yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma daharo 'sminn antarAkAshaH kiM tad atra vidyate yad anveShTavyaM yad vAva vijij~nAsitavyam iti |
sa brUyAt || ChUp_8,1.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,1.2 taM cedevamuktavantamAcAryaM yadi brUyurantevAsinashcodayeyuH, kathaM, yadidamasminbrahmapure paricchinne 'ntardaharaM puNDarIkaM veshma tato 'pyantaralpatara evA'kAshaH /
puNDarIka eva veshmani tAvatkiM syAt /
kiM tato 'lpatare khe yadbhavedityAhuH /
daharo 'sminnantarAkAshaH kiM tadatra vidyate na kiJNcana vidyata ityabhiprAyaH /
yadi nAma badaramAtraM kimapi vidyate kiM tasyAnveShaNena vijij~nAsanena vA phalaM vijij~nAsituH syAt /
ato yatttrAnveShTavyaM vijij~nAsitavyaM vA na tena prayojanamityuktavataH sa AcAryo brUyAditi shrutervacanam //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,1.3

#<yAvAn vA ayam AkAshas tAvAn eSho 'ntarhR^idaya AkAshaH |
ubhe 'smin dyAvApR^ithivI antar eva samAhite |
ubhAv agnish ca vAyush ca sUryAcandramasAv ubhau vidyun nakShatrANi |
yac cAsyehAsti yac ca nAsti sarvaM tad asmin samAhitam iti || ChUp_8,1.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,1.3 shR^iNuta /
tatra yadbrUtha puNDarIkAntaHkhasyAlpatvAttatsthamalpataraM syAditi /
tadasat /
na hi khaM puNDarIkaveshamagataM puNDarIkAdalpataraM matvAvocaM daharo 'rsminnantarAkAsha iti /
kiM tarhi puNDarIkamalpaM tadanuvidhAyi tatsthamantaHkaraNaM puNDarIkAkAshaparicchinnaM tasminvishuddhe saMhR^itakaraNAnAM yoginAM svaccha ivodake pratibimbarUpamAdarsha iva ca shuddhe svacchaM vij~nAnajyotiH svarUpAvabhAsaM tAvanmAtraM brahmopalabhyata iti daharo 'sminnantarAkAsha ityavocAmAntaHkaraNopAdhinimittam /
svatastu yAvAnvai prasiddhaH parimANato 'yamAkAsho bhautikastAvAneSho 'ntarhR^idaya AkAsho yasminnanveShTavyaM vijij~nAsitavyaM cAvocAma /
nApyAkAshatulyaparimANatvamabhipretya tAvAnityucyate /
kiM tarhi brahmaNo 'nurUpasya dR^iShTAntAntarasyAbhAvAt /
kathaM punarnA'kAshasamameva brahmetyavagamyate /
"yenA'vR^itaM khaM ca divaM mahIM ca" /
"tasmAdvA etasmAdAtmana AkAshaH saMbhUtaH" "etasminnu khalvakShare gArgyAkAshaH"ityAdishrutibhyaH /
kiJNcobhe 'smindyAvApR^ithivI brahmAkAshe buddhyupAdhivishiShTe 'ntareva samAhite samyagAhite sthite yathA vA arA nAbhAvityuktaM hi /
tathobhAvagnishca vAyushcetyAdi samAnam /
yaccAsyA'tmana AtmIyatvena dehavato 'sti vidyata iha loke /
tatA yaccA'tmIyatvena na vidyate /
naShTaM bhaviShyacca nAstItyucyate /
na tvatyantamevAsat /
tasya hR^idyAkAshe samAdhAnAnupapatteH //3 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,1.4

#<taM ced brUyur asmiMsh cedaM brahmapure sarvaM samAhitaM sarvANi ca bhUtAni sarve ca kAmA yad enaj jarA vApnoti pradhvaMsate vA kiM tato 'tishiShyata iti || ChUp_8,1.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,1.4 taM cedevamuktavantaM brUyuH punarantevAsinaH asmiMshcedyathokte cedyadi brahmapuropalakShitAntarAkAsha ityarthaH /
idaM sarvaM samAhitaM sarvANi ca bhUtAni sarve ca kAmAH /
kathamAcAryeNAnuktAH kAmA antevAsibhirucyante /
naiSha doShaH yaccAsyehAsti yacca nAstItyuktA eva hyAcAryeNa kAmAH /
api ca sarvashabdena coktA eva kAmAH /
yadA yasminkAla etaccharIraM brahmapurAkhyaM jarAvalIpalitAdilakShaNA vayohAnirvA'pnoti shasrAdinA vA vR^ikNaM pradhvaMsate visraMsate vinashyati kiM tato 'nyadatishiShyate /
ghaTAshritakShIradadhisnehAdivadghaTanAshe dehanAshe 'pi dehAshrayamuttarottaraM pUrvapUrvanAshAnnashyatItyabhiprAyaH /
evaM prApte nAshe kiM tato 'nyadyathoktAdatishiShyate 'vatiShThate na kiJNcanAvatiShThata ityabhIprAyaH //4 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,1.5

#<sa brUyAt |
nAsya jarayaitaj jIryati na vadhenAsya hanyate |
etat satyaM brahmapuram asmin kAmAH samAhitAH |
eSha AtmApahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityur vishoko vijighatso 'pipAsaH satyakAmaH satyasaMkalpaH |
yathA hy eveha prajA anvAvishanti yathAnushAsanam |
yaM yam antam abhikAmA bhavanti yaM janapadaM yaM kShetrabhAgaM taM tam evopajIvanti || ChUp_8,1.5 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,1.5 evamantevAsibhishcoditaH sa AcAryo brUyAttanmatimapanayan /
katham /
asya dehasya jarayaitadyathoktamantarAkAshAkhyaM braÇma yasminsarva samAhitaM na jIryati dehavanna vikriyata ityarthaH /
na cAsya vadhena shasrAdighAtenaitaddhanyate yathA'kAshaM kimu tato 'pi sUkShmataramashabdamasparshaM brahma dehendriyAdidoShairna spR^ishyata ityetasminnavasare vaktavyaM prAptaM tatprakR^itavyAsaN^go mA bhUditi nocyate /
indravirocanAkhyAyikAyAmupariShTAdvakShyAmo yuktitaH /
etatsatyamavitathaM brahmapuraM brahmaiva puraM brahmapuraM sharIrAkhyaM tu brahmapuraM brahmopalakShaNArthatvAt /
tattvanR^itameva /
"vAcA'rambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyam"iti shruteH /
tadvikAre 'nR^ite 'pi dehashuN^ge brahmopalabhyata iti brahmapuramityuktaM vyAvahArikam /
satyaM tu brahmapurametadeva brahma /
sarvavyavahArAspadatvAt /
ato 'sminpuNDarIkopalakShite brahmapure sarve kAmA ye bahirbhavadbhiH prArthyante te 'sminneva svAtmani samAhitAH /
atastatprAptyupAyamevAnutiShThata bAhyaviShayatR^iShmAM tyajatetyabhiprAyaH /
eSha AtmA bhavatAM svarUpam /
shR^iNuta tasya lakShaNam /
apahatapApmA /
apahataH pApmA dharmAdharmAkhyo yasya so 'yamapahatapApmA /
tathA vijaro vigatajaro vimR^ityushca /
taduktaM pUrvameva na vadhenAsya hanyata iti /
kimartha punarucyate /
yadyapi dehasaMbandhibhyAM jarAmR^ityubhyAM na saMbadhyate 'nyathApi saMbandhastAbhyAM syAdityAshaN^kAnivR^ittyartham /
vishoko vigatashokaH /
shoko nAmeShTAdiviyoganimitto mAnasaH saMtApaH /
vijighatso vigatAshanecchaH /
apipAso 'pAnecchaH /
nanvapahatapApmatvena jarAdayaH shokAntAH pratiShiddhA eva bhavanti /
kAraNapratiShedhAt /
dharmAdharmakAryA hi ta iti /
jarAdipratiShedhena vA dharmAdharmayoH kAryAbhAve vidyamAnayorapyasatsamatvamiti pR^ithakpratiShedho 'narthakaH syAt /
satyamevaM tathApi dharmakAryA nandavyatirekeNa svAbhAvikAnando yatheshvare vij~nAnamAnandaM brahmeti shruteH /
tathAdharmakAryajarAdivyatirekeNApi jarAdiduHkhasvarUpaM svAbhAvikaM syAdityAshaN^kyeta /
ato yuktastannivR^ittaye jarAdInAM dharmAdharmAbhyAM pR^ithakpratiShedhaH /
jarAdigrahaNaM sarvaduHkhopalakShaNArtham /
pApanimittAnAM tu duHkhAnAmAnantyAtpratyekaM ca tatpratiShedhasyAshakyatvAtsarvaduHkhapratiShedhArthaM yuktamevApahatapApmatvavacanam /
satyA avitathAH kAmA yasya so 'yaM satyakAmaH /
vitathA hi saMsAriNAM kAmAH /
Ishvarasya tadviparItAH /
tathA kAmahetavaH saMkalpA api satyA yasya sa satyasaMkalpaH /
saMkalpAH kAmAshca shuddhasattvopAdhinimittA Ishvarasya citraguvat /
na svato neti netItyuktatvAt /
yathoktalakShaNa evA'tmA vij~neyo gurubhyaH shAstratashcA'tmasaMvedyatayA ca svArAjyakAmaiH /
na cedvij~nAyate ko doShaH syAditi /
shR^iNutAtra doShaM dR^iShTAntena /
yathA hyeveha loke prajA anvAvishantyanuvartante /
yathAnushAsanaM yatheha prajA anyaM svAminaM manyamAnAH svasya svAmino yathA yathAnushAsanaM tathA tathAnvAvishanti /
kim /
yaM yamantaM pratyantaM janapadaM kShetrabhAgaM cAbhikAmA arthinyo bhavantyAtmabuddhyanurUpaM taM tameva ca pratyantAdimupajIvantIti /
eSha dR^iShTAnto 'svAtantryadeShaM prati puNyaphalopabhoge //5 //

START ChUp 8,1.6

#<tad yatheha karmajito lokaH kShIyata evam evAmutra puNyajito lokaH kShIyate |
tad ya ihAtmAnam ananuvidya vrajanty etAMsh ca satyAn kAmAMs teShAM sarveShu lokeShv akAmacAro bhavati |
atha ya ihAtmAnam anivudya vrajanty etaMsh ca satyAn kAmAMs teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati || ChUp_8,1.6 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,1.6 athAnyo dR^iShTAntastatkShayaM prati tadyathehetyAdiH /
tattatra yatheha loke tAsAmeva svAmyanushAsanAnuvartinInAM prajAnAM sevAdijito lokaH parAdhInopabhogaH kShIyate 'ntavAnbhavati /
athedAnIM dArShTAntikamupasaMharati-evamevAmutrAgnihotrAdipuNyaj ito lokaH parAdhInopabhogaH kShIyata evetyukto doSha eShAmiti viShayaM darshayati-tadya ityAdinA /
tattatrehAsmiMlloke j~nAnakarmaNoradhikR^itA yogyAH santa AtmAnaM yathoktalakShaNaM shAstrAcAryopadiShTamananuvidya yathopadeshamanu svasaMvedyatAmakR^itvA vrajanti dehAdasmAt prayanti ya etAMshca yathoktAn satyAn satyasaMkalpakAryAMshca svAtmasthAn kAmAnananuvidya vrajanti teShAM sarveShu lokeShvakAmacAro 'svatantratA bhavati /
yathA rAjAnushAsanAnuvartinInAM prajAnAmityarthaH /
atha ye 'nya iha loka AtmAnaM shAsrAcAryoradeshamanuvidya svAtmasaMvedyatAmApAdya vrajanti yathoktAMshca satyAnkAmAMsteShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati rAj~na iva sArvabhaumasyeha loke //6//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi aShTamAdhyAyasya prathamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 8,2.1

#<sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya pitaraH samuttiShThanti |
tena pitR^ilokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,2.1 kathaM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavatIti, ucyate-ya AtmAnaM yatoktalakShaNaM hR^idi sAkShAtkR^itavAnvakShyamANabrahmacaryAdisAdhanasaMpannaH saMstatsthAMshca satyAnkAmAnsa tyaktadeho yadi pitR^ilokakAmaH pitaro janayitArasta eva sukhahetutvena bhogyatvAllokA ucyante teShu kAmo yasya taiH pitR^ibhiH saMbandhecchA yasya bhavati tasya saMkalpamAtrAdeva pitaraH samuttiShThintyAtmasaMbandhitAmApadyante /
vishuddhasattvatayA satyasaMkalpatvAdIshvarasyeva tena pitR^ilokena bhogena saMpannaH saMpattiriShTaprAptistayA samR^iddho mahIyate pUjyate vardhate vA mahimAnamanubhavati //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,2.2-9

#<atha yadi mAtR^ilokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya mAtaraH samuttiShThanti |
tena mAtR^ilokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.2 ||>#

#<atha yadi bhrAtR^ilokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya bhrAtaraH samuttiShThanti |
tena bhrAtR^ilokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.3 ||>#

#<atha yadi svasR^ilokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya svasAraH samuttiShThanti |
tena svasR^ilokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.4 ||>#

#<atha yadi sakhilokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya sakhAyaH samuttiShThanti |
tena sakhilokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.5 ||>#

#<atha yadi gandhamAlyalokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya gandhamAlye samuttiShThataH |
tena gandhamAlyalokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.6 ||>#

#<atha yady annapAnalokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsyAnnapAne samuttiShThataH |
tenAnnapAnalokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.7 ||>#

#<atha yadi gItavAditalokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya gItavAdite samuttiShThataH |
tena gItavAditalokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.8 ||>#

#<atha yadi strIlokakAmo bhavati |
saMkalpAd evAsya striyaH samuttiShThanti |
tena strIlokena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.9 ||>#


__________


ChUpBh_8,2.2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9 samAnamanyat /
mAtaro janayitryo 'tItAH sukhahetubhUtAH sAmardhyAt /
na hi duHkhahetubhUtAsu grAmasUkarAdijanmanimittAsu mAtR^iShu vishuddhasattvasya yogina icchA tatsaMbandho vA yuktaH //2-9 //

START ChUp 8,2.10

#<yaM yam antam abhikAmo bhavati |
yaM kAmaM kAmayate |
so 'sya saMkalpAd eva samuttiShThati |
tena saMpanno mahIyate || ChUp_8,2.10 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,2.10 yaM yanamtaM pradeshamabhikAmo bhavati /
yaM ca kAmaM kAmayate yathoktavyatirekeNApi so 'syAntaH prAptumiShTaH kAmashca saMkalpAdeva samuttiShThatyasya /
tenecchAvighAtatayAbhipretArthaprAptyA ca saMpanno mahIyata ityuktArtham //10//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi aShTamAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH khaNDaH>#

=======================================================================

START ChUp 8,3.1

#<ta ime satyAH kAmA anR^itApidhAnAH |
teShAM satyAnAM satAm anR^itam apidhAnam |
yo yo hy asyetaH praiti na tam iha darshanAya labhate || ChUp_8,3.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,3.1 yathoktAtmadhyAnasAdhanAnuShThAnaM prati sAdhakAnAmutsAhajananArthamanukroshantyAha-kaShTamidaM khalu vartate yatsvAtmasthAH shakyaprApyA api ta ime satyAH kAmA anR^itApidhAnAsteShAmAtmasthAnAM svAshrayANAmeva satAmanR^itaM ba3hyaviShayeShu stryannabhojanAcchAdanAdiShu tR^iShNA tannimittaM ca svecchApracAratvaM mithyAj~nAnanimittatvAdanR^itamityucyate /
tannimittaM satyAnAM kAmAnAmaprAptirityapidhAnamivApidhAnam /
kathamanR^itApidhAnanimittaM teShAmalAbha iti, ucyate-yo yo hi yasmAdasya jantoH putro bhrAtA veShTa ito 'smAllokAtpraiti pragacchati mriyate tamiShTaM putraM bhrAtaraM vA svahR^idayAkAshe vidyamAnamapIha punardarshanAyecchannapi na labhate //1 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,3.2

#<atha ye cAsyeha jIvA ye ca pretA yac cAnyad icchan na labhate sarvaM tad atra gatvA vindate |
atra hy asyaite satyAH kAmA anR^itApidhAnAH |
tad yathApi hiraNyanidhiM nihitam akShetraj~nA upary upari saJNcaranto na vindeyuH |
evam evemAH sarvAH prajA ahar ahar gacchantya etaM brahmalokaM na vindanty anR^itena hi pratyUDhAH || ChUp_8,3.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,3.2 atha punarye cAsya viduSho jantorjIvA jIvantIha putrA bhrAtrAdayo vA ye ca pretA mR^itA iShTAH saMbandhino yaccAnyadiha loke vastrAnnapAnAdi ratnAdi vA vastvicchanna labhate tatsarvamatra hR^idayAkAshAkhye brahmaNi gatvA yathoktena vidhinA vindate labhate /
atrAsminhArdAkAshe hi yasmAdasyaite yathoktAH satyAH kAmA vartante 'natApidhAnAH /
kathamiva tadanyAyyamityucyate-tattatra yathA hiraNyanidhiM hiraNyameva punargrahaNAya nidhAtR^ibhirnidhIyata iti nidhistaM hiraNyanidhiM nihitaM bhUmeradhastAnnikShiptamakShetraj~nA nidhishAsrairnidhikShetramajAnantaste nidheruparyupari saMcaranto 'pi nidhiM na vindeyuH shakyavedanamapi /
evamevemA avidyavatyaH sarvA imAH prajA yathoktaM hR^idayAkAshAkhyaM brahmalokaM brahmaiva loko brahmalokastamaharahaH pratyahaM gacchantyo 'pi suShuptakAle na vidandanti na labhanta eSho 'haM brahmalokabhAvamApanno 'smyadyeti /

anR^itena hi yathoktena hi yasmAtpratyUDhA hR^itAH svarUpAdavidyAdidoShairbahipakR^iShTA ityarthaH /
ataH kaShTamidaM vartate jantUnAM yatsvAyattamapi brahma na labhyata ityabhiprAyaH //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,3.3

#<sa vA eSha AtmA hR^idi |
tasyaitad eva niruktaM hR^idy ayam iti tasmAd dhR^id ayam |
ahar ahar vA evaMvit svargaM lokam eti || ChUp_8,3.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,3.3 sa vai ya AtmApahatapApmeti prakR^ito vaishabdena taM smArayatyeSha vivakShita AtmA hR^idi hR^idayapuNDarIka AkAshashabdenAbhihitaH /
tasyaitasya hR^idayasyaitadeva niruktaM nirvacanaM nAnyata /
hR^idyayamAtmA vartata iti yasmAt tasmAddhR^idayaM hR^idayanAmanirvacanaprasiddhyApi svahR^idaya AtmetyavagantavyamityabhiprAyaH /
aharaharvai pratyahamevaMviddhR^idyayamAtmeti jAnansvargaM lokaM hArdaM brahmaiti pratipadyate /
nanvanevaMvidapi suShuptakAle hArdaM brahma pratipadyata eva suShuptakAle satA somya tadA saMpanna ityuktatvAt /
bADhamevaM tathApyasti visheShaH /
yathA jAnannajAnaMshca sarvo jantuH sadbrahmaiva tathApi tattvamasIti pratibodhito vidvAnsadeva nAnyo 'smIti jAnansadeva bhavati /
evameva vidvAnavidvAMshcasuShupte yadyapi satsaMpadyate tathApyevaMvideva svargaM lokametItyucyate /
dehapAte 'pi vidyAphalasyAvashyaMbhAvitvAdityeSha visheShaH //3 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,3.4

#<atha ya eSha saMprasAdo 'smAc charIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotir upasaMpadya  svena rUpenAbhiniShpadyata eSha Atmeti hovAca |
etad amR^itam abhayam etad brahmeti |
tasya ha vA etasya brahmaNo nAma satyam iti || ChUp_8,3.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,3.4 suShuptakAle svenA'manA satA saMpannaH sansamyakprasIdatIti jAgratsvapnayorviShayendriyasaMyogajAtaM kAluShyaM jahAtIti saMprasAdashabdo yadyapi sarvajantUnAM sAdhAraNastathApyevaMvitsvargaM lokametIti prakR^itatvAdeSha saMprasAda iti saMnihitavadyatnavisheShAtso 'thedaM sharIraM hitvAsmAccharIrAtsamutthAya sharIrAtmabhAvanAM parityajyetyarthaH /
na tvAsanAdiva samutthAyetIha yuktam /
svena rUpeNeti visheShaNAt /
na hyanyata utthAya svarUpaM saMpattavyam /
svarUpameva hi tanna bhavati pratipattavyaM cetsyAt /
paraM paramAtmalakShaNaM vij~naptisvabhAvaM jyotirupasaMpadya svAsthyamupagamyetyetat /
svena AtmIyena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate prAgetasyAH svarUpasaMpatteravidyayA dehamevAparaM rUpamAtmatvenopagata iti tadapekShayedamucyate svena rUpeNeti /
asharIratA hyAtmanaH svarUpaM yatsvaM paraM jyotiHsvarUpamApadye saMprasAda eSha Atmeti hovAca /
sa brUyAditi yaH shrutyA niyukto 'ntevAsibhyaH /
kiJNcaitadamR^itamavinAshi bhUmA yo vai bhUmA tadamR^itamityuktam /
ata evAbhayaM bhUmno dvitIyAbhAvAdata etadbrahmeti /
tasya ha vA etasya brahmaNo nAmAbhidhAnam /
kiM tatsatyamiti /
satyaM hyavitathaM brahma /
tatsatyaM sa Atmeti hyuktam /
atha kimarthamidaM nAma punarucyate /
tadupAsanavidhistutyartham //4//


8.3.5 #<tAni ha vA etAni trINyakSharANi satIyamiti tadyatsattdamR^itamatha yatti tanmartyamatha># #<yadyaM tenobhe yacchati yadanenobhe yacchati tasmAdyamaharaharvA evaMvitsvargaM lokameti //5//>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,3.5 tAni ha vA etAni brahmaNo nAmAkSharANi trINyetAni satIyAmati sakArastakAro yamiti ca /
takAra IkAraH uccAraNArtho 'nubandhaH /
hrasvenaivAkShareNa punaH pratinirdeshAtteShAm /
tattatra yatsatsakArastadamR^itaM sadbrahmAmR^itavAcakatvAdamR^ita eva sakArastakAranto nirdiShTaH /
atha yattitakArastanmartyam /
atha yadyamakSharaM tenAkShareNAmR^itamartyAkhye pUrve ubhe 'kShare yacchati yamayati niyamayati vashIkarotyAtmana ityarthaH /
yadyasmAdanena yamityetenobhe yacchati tasmAdyAm /
saMyate iva hyetena yamA lakShyete /
braÇmanAmAkSharasyApIdamamR^itatvAdidharmavattvaM mahAbhAgyaM kimuta nAmavata ityupAsyatvAya stUyate /
brahmanAmanirvacanenaiva nAmavato vettaivaMvit /
aharaharvA evaMvitsvargaM lokametItyuktArtham //5//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi aShTamAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 8,4.1

#<atha ya AtmA sa setur dhR^itir eShAM lokAnAm asaMbhedAya |
naitaM setum ahorAtre tarato na jarA na mR^ityur na shoko na sukR^itam |
sarve pApmAno 'to nivartante |
apahatapApmA hy eSha brahmalokaH || ChUp_8,4.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,4.1 atha ya Atmeti /
uktalakShaNo yaH saMprasAdastasya svarUpaM vakShyamANairuktaishca guNaiH punaH stUyate brahmacaryasAdhanasaMbandhArtham /
ya eSha yathoktalakShaNa AtmA sa seturiva setuH /
vidhR^itirvidharaNaH /
anena hi sarvaM jagadvarNAshramAdikriyAkArakaphalAdibhedaniyamaiH karturanurUpaM vidadhatA vidhR^itam /
adhriyamANaM hIshvareNedaM vishvaM vinashyedyatastasmAtsa seturvidhR^itiH /
kimarthaM sa seturityAha-eShAM bhUrAdInAM kartR^ikarmalAshrayANAmasaMbhedAyAvidAraNAyAvinAshAyetyetat /
kiMvishShTashcAsau seturityAha-naitam setumAtmAnamahorAtre sarvasya janimataH paricchedake satI naitaM tarataH /
yathAnye saMsAriNaH kAlenAhorAtrAdilakShaNena paricchedyA na tathAyaM kAlaparicchedya ityabhiprAyaH /
"yasmAdarvAksaMvatsaro 'hobhiH parivartata"iti shrutyantarAt /
ata evainaM na jarA tarati na prApnoti /
tathA na mR^ityurna shoko na sukR^itaM na dR^iShkR^itaM sukR^itaduShkR^ite dharmAdharmai /
prAptiratra taraNashabdenAbhipretA nAtikramaNam /
kAraNaM hyAtmA /
na shakyaM hi kAraNAtikramaNaM kartuM kAryeNa /
ahorAtrAdi ca sarvaM sataH kAryam /
anyena hyanyasya prAptiratikramaNaM vA kriyeta /
na tu tenaiva tasya /
na hi ghaTena mR^itprApyate 'tikramyate vA /
yadyapi pUrvaM ya AtmApahatapApmetyAdinA pApmAdipratiShedha ukta eva tathApIhAyaM visheSho na taratIti prAptiviShayatvaM pratiShidhyate /
tatrA visheSheNa jarAdyabhAvamAtramuktam /
ahorAtrAdyA uktA anuktAshcAnye sarve pApmAna ucyante 'to 'smAdAtmanaH setornivartante 'prApyaivetyarthaH /
apahatapApmA hyeSha brahmaiva loko brahmaloka uktaH //1 //

START ChUp 8,4.2

#<tasmAd vA etaM setuM tIrtvA andhaH sann anandho bhavati |
viddhaH sann aviddho bhavati |
upatApI sann anupatApI bhavati |
tasmAd vA etaM setuM tIrtvA api naktam ahar evAbhiniShpadyate |
sakR^id vibhAto hy evaiSha brahmalokaH || ChUp_8,4.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,4.2 yasmAcca pApmakArya mAndhyAdi sharIravataH syAnna tvasharIrasya tasmAdvA etamAtmAnaM setuM tIrvA prApyAnandho bhavati dehavattve pUrvamandho 'pi san /
tatA viddhaH sandehavattve sa dehaviyoge setuM tIrtvA prApyAnandho bhavati dehavattve pUrvamandho 'pi san /
tathA viddhaH sandehavattve sa dehaviyogo setuM prApyAviddho bhavati /
tathopatApI rogAdyupatApavAnsannanupatApI bhavati /
kiJNca yasmAdahorAtre na staH setau tasmAdvA etaM setuM tIrtvA prApya naktamapi tamorUpaM rAtrirapi sarvamaharevAbhiniShpadyate /
vij~naptyAtmajyotiH svarUpamaharivAhaH sadaikarUpaM viduShaH saMpadyata ityarthaH /
sakR^idvibhAtaH sadA vibhAtaH sadaikarUpaH svena rUpeNaiSha brahmalokaH //2 //

START ChUp 8,4.3

#<tad ya evaitaM brahmalokaM brahmacaryeNAnuvindanti teShAm evaiSha brahmalokaH |
teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati || ChUp_8,4.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,4.3 tattatraivaM satyetaM yathoktaM brahmalokaM brahmacaryeNa srIviShayatR^iShNAtyAgena shAsrAcAryopadeshamanuvindanti svAtmasaMvedyatAmApAdayanti ye teShAmeva brahmacaryasAdhanavatAM brahmavidAmeSha brahmalokaH nAnyeShAM srIviShayasaMparkajAtatR^iShNAnAM brahmavidAmapItyarthaH /
teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavatItyuktArtham /
tasmAtparamametatsAdhanaM brahmacaryaM brahmavidAmityabhiprAyaH //3//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi aShTamAdhyAyasya caturthaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 8,5.1

#<atha yad yaj~na ity AcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat |
brahmacaryeNa hy eva yo j~nAtA taM vindate |
atha yad iShTam ity AcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat |
brahmacaryeNa hy eveShTvAtmAnam anuvindate || ChUp_8,5.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,5.1 ya AtmA setutvAdiguNaiH stutastatprAptaye j~nAnasahakArisAdhanAntaraM brahmacaryAkhyaM vidAtavyamityAha /
yaj~nAdibhishca tatstauti kartavyArtham- atha yadyaj~na ityAcakShate loke paramapuruShArthasAdhanaM kathayanti shiShTAstadbrahmacaryameva /
yaj~nasyApi yatphalaM tadbrahmacaryavAllaMbhate 'to yaj~no 'pi brahmacaryaM bhavati pratipattavyam /
kathaM brahmacaryaM yaj~na ityAha-brahmacaryeNaiva hi yasmAdyo j~nAtAsa taM brahmalokaM yaj~nasyApi pAramparyeNa phalabhUtaM vindate labhate tato yaj~no 'pi brahmacaryameveti /
yo j~nAtetyakSharAnuvR^itteryaj~no brahmacaryameva /
atha yadiShTamityAcakShate brahmacaryameva tat /
katham /
brahmacaryeNaiva sAdhanena tamIshvaramiShTvA pUjayitvAthavaiShaNAmAtmaviShayAM kR^itvA tamAtmAnamanuvindate /
eShaNAdiShTamapi brahmacaryameva //1 //

START ChUp 8,5.2

#<atha yat sattrAyaNam ity AcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat |
brahmacaryeNa hy eva sata Atmanas trANaM vindate |
atha yan maunam ity AcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat |
brahmacaryeNa hy evAtmAnam anuvidya manute || ChUp_8,5.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,5.2 atha yatsattrAyaNamityAcakShate brahmacaryameva tattathA sataH parasmAdAtmana AtmanasrANaM rakShaNaM brahmacaryasAdhanena vindate /
ataH sattrAyaNashabdamapi brahmacaryameva sat /
atha yanmaunamityAcakShate brahmacaryameva tadbrahmacaryeNaiva sAdhanena yuktaH sannAtmAnaM shAsrAcAryAbhyAmanuvidya pashcAnmanute dhyAyati /
ato maunashabdamapi brahmacaryameva //2 //

START ChUp 8,5.3

#<atha yad anAshakAyanam ity AcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat |
eSha hy AtmA na nashyati yaM brahmacaryeNAnuvindate |
atha yad araNyAyanam ity AcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat |
tat arash ca ha vai Nyash cArNavau brahmaloke tR^itIyasyAm ito divi |
tad airaMmadIyaM saraH |
tad ashvatthaH somasavanaH |
tad aparAjitA pUr brahmaNaH prabhuvimitaM hiraNmayam || ChUp_8,5.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,5.3 atha yadanAshakAyanamityAcakShate brahmacaryameva tat /
yamAtmAnaM brahmacaryeNAnuvindate sa eSha hyAtmA brahmacaryasAdhanavato na nashyati tasmAdanAshakAyanamapi brahmacaryameva /
atha yadaraNyAyanamityAcakShate brahmacaryameva tat /
araNyashabdayorarNavayorbrahmacaryavato 'yanAdaraNyAyanaM brahmacaryam /
yo j~nAnAdyaj~na eShaNAdiShTaM satasrANAtsattrAyaNaM mananAnmaunamanashanAdanAshakAyanamaraNyayorgamanAdaraNyAyanamityAdibhirmahadbhiH puruShArthasAdhanaiH stutatvAdbrahmacaryaM paramaM j~nAnasya sahakArikAraNaM sAdhanamityato brahmavidA yatnato rakShaNIyamityarthaH /
tattatra hi brahmaloke 'rashca ha vai prasiddho NyashcArNavau samudropame vA sarasI tR^itIyasyAM bhuvamantarikShaM cApekShya tR^itIyA dyaustasyAM tR^itIyasyAmito 'smAllokAdArabhya gaNyamAnAyAM divi /
tattatraiva cairamirAnnaM tanmaya airo maNDastena pUrNamairaM madIyaM tadupayoginAM madakaraM harShotpAdakaM saraH /
tatraiva cAshvattho vR^ikShaH somasavano nAmataH somo 'mR^itaM tanniHsravo 'mR^itasrava iti vA /
tatraiva ca brahmaloke brahmacaryasAdhanarahitairbrahmacaryasAdhanavadbhyo 'nyairna jIyata ityaparAjitA nAma pUH purI brahmaNo hiraNyagarbhasya /
brahmaNA ca prabhuNA visheSheNa mitaM nirmitaM tacca hiraNmayaM sauvarNaM prabhuvimitaM maNDapamiti vAkyasheShaH //3 //

START ChUp 8,5.4

#<tad ya evaitAv araM ca NyaM cArNavau brahmaloke brahmacaryeNAnuvindanti teShAm evaiSha brahmalokaH |
teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati || ChUp_8,5.4 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,5.4 tattatra hi brahmaloka etAvarNavau yAvaraNyAkhyAvuktau brahmacaryeNa sAdhanenAnuvindanti ye teShAmevaiSha yo vyAkhyAto brahmalokasteShAM ca brahmacaryasAdhavanatAM brahmavidAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati /
nAnyeShAmabrahmacaryaparANAM bAhyaviShayAsaktabuddhInAM kadAcidapItyarthaH /
nanvatra tvamindrastvaM yamastvaM varuNa ityAdibhiryathA kashcitstUyate mahArha evamiShTAdibhiH shabdairna stryAdiviShayatR^iShNAnivR^ittimAtraM stutyarhaM kiM tarhi j~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatvAttadeveShTAdibhiH stUyata iti kecit /
na /
stryAdibAhyaviShayatR^iShNApahR^itacittAnAM pratyagAtmavivekavij~nAnAnupapatteH /
"parAJNci khAni vyatR^iNatsvayaMbhUstasmAtparAÇpashyati nAntarAtman"ityAdishrutismR^itishatebhyaH /
j~nAnasahakArikAraNaM stryAdiviShayatR^iShNAnivR^ittisAdhanaM vidhAtavyameveti yuktaiva tatstutiH /
nanu ca yaj~nAdibhiH stutaM brahmacaryamiti yaj~nAdInAM puruShArthasAdhanatvaM gamyate /
satyaM gamyate /
na tviha brahmalokaM prati yaj~nAdInAM sAdhanatvamabhipretya yaj~nAdibhirbrahmacaryaM stUyate kiM tarhi teShAM prasiddhaM puruShArthasAdhanatvamapekShya /
yathendrAdibhI rAjA na tu yatrendrAdInAM vyApArastatraiva rAj~na iti tadvat /
ya imer'NavAdayo brAhmalaukikAH saMkalpajAshca pitrAdayo bhogAste kiM pArthivA ApyAshca yatheha loke dR^ishyante taddhadarNavavR^ikShapUHsvarNamaNDapAnyAhosvinmAnasapratyayamAtrANIti /
kiJNcAtaH, yadi pArthivA ApyAshca sthUlAH syurhR^idyAkAshe samAdhAnAnupapattiH /
purANe ca"manomayAni brahmaloke sharIrAdInI"ti vAkyaM virudhyeta /
"ashokamahimam"ityAdyAshca shrutayaH /
nanu"samudrAH saritaH sarAMsi vApyaH kUpA yaj~nA vedA mantrAdayashca mUrtimanto brahmANamupatiShThanta"iti mAnasatvai virudhyeta purANasmR^itiH /
na /
mUrtimattve prasiddharUpANAmeva tatra gamanAnupapatteH /
tasmAtprasiddhamUrtivyatirekeNa sAgarAdInAM mUrtyantaraM sAgarAdibhirupAttaM brahmalokagantR^i kalpanAyAM yathAprasiddhA eva mAnasya AkAravatyaH puMstryAdyA mUrtayo yuktAH kalpayituM mAnasadehAnurUpyasaMbandhopapatteH /
dR^iShTA hi mAnasya evA'kAravatyaH puMstryAdyA mUrtayaH svapne /
nanu tA anR^itA eva /
ta ime satyAH kAmA iti shrutistathA sati virudhyeta /
na /
mAnasapratyayasya sattvopapatteH /
mAnasA hi pratyayAH srIpuruShAdyAkArAH svapne dR^ishyante /
nanu jAgradvAsanArUpAH svapnadR^ishyA na tu tatra stryAdayaH svapne vidyante /
atyalpamidamucyate /
jAgradviShayA api mAnasapratyayAbhinirvR^ittA eva sadIkShAbhinirvR^ittatejo 'bannamayatvAjjAgradviShayANAm /
saMkalpamUlA hi lokA iti coktam"samakÊpatAM dyAvApR^ithivI"ityatra /
sarvashrutiShu ca pratyagAtmana utpattiH pralayashca tatraiva sthitishca"yathA vA arA nAbhau"ityAdinocyate /
tasmAnmAnasAnAM bAhyAnAM ca viShayANAmitaretarakAryakAraNamiShyata eva bIjAN^kuravat /
yadyapi bAhyA eva mAnasA mAnasA eva ca bAhyA nAnR^itatvaM teShAM kadAcidapi svAtmani bhavati /
nanu svapne dR^iShTAH pratibuddhasyAnR^itA bhavanti viShayAH /
satyameva /
jAgradbodhApekShaM tu tadanR^itatvaM na svataH /
tathA svapnabodhApekShaM ca jAgraddR^iShTaviShayAnR^itatvaM na svataH /
visheShAkAramAtraM tu sarveShAM mithyApratyayanimittamiti vAcA'rambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyamanR^itaM trINi rUpANItyeva satyam /
tAnyapyAkAravisheShato 'nR^itaM svataH sanmAtrarUpatayA satyam prAksadAtmapratibodhAtsvaviShaye 'pi sarvaM styameva svapnadR^ishyA iveti na kashcidvirodhaH /
tasmAnmAnasA eva brAhmalaukikA araNyAdayaH pitrAdayaH kAmAH /
bAhyaviShayabhogavadashuddhirahitatvAcchuddhasattvasaMkalpajanyA iti niratishayasukhAH satyAshceshvarANAM bhavantItyarthaH /
satsatyAtmapratibodhe 'pi rajjvAmiva kalpitAH sarpAdayaH sadAtmasvarUpatAmeva pratipadyanta iti sadAtmanA satyA eva bhavanti //4//

#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi aShTamAdhyAyasya paJNcamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 8,6.1

#<atha yA etA hR^idayasya nADyas tAH piN^galasyANimnas tiShThanti shuklasya nIlasya pItasya lohitasyeti |
asau vAdityaH piN^gala eSha shukla eSha nIla eSha pIta eSha lohitaH || ChUp_8,6.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,6.1 yastu hR^idayapuNDarIkagataM yathoktaguNavishiShTaM brahma brahmacaryAdisAdhanasaMpannastyaktabAhyaviShayAnR^itatR^iShNaH sannupAste tasyeyaM mUrdhanyayA nADyA gatirvaktavyeti nADIkhaNDa Arabhyate- atha yA etA vakShyamANA hR^idayasya puNDarIkAkArasya brahmopAsanasthAnasya saMbandhinyo nADyo hR^idayamAMsapiNDAtsarvato viniHsR^itA AdityamaNDalAdiva rashmayastAshcaitAH piN^galasya varNavisheShavishiShTasyANimnaH sUkShmarasasya rasena pUrNAstadAkArA eva tiShThanti vartanta ityarthaH /
tathA shuklasya nIlasya pItasya lohitasya ca rasasya pUrNA iti sarvatrAdhyAhAryam /
saureNa tejasA pittAkhyena pAkAbhinirvR^ittena kaphenAlpena saMparkAtpiN^galaM bhavati sauraM tejaH pittAkhyAm tadeva ca vAtabhUyastvAnnIlaM bhavati /
tadeva ca kaphabhUyastvAcchuklam /
kaphena samatAyAM pItam /
shoNita bAhulyena lohitam /
vaidyakAdvA varNavisheShA anveShTavyAH kathaM bhavantIti /
shrutistvAhA'dityasaMbandhAdeva tattejaso nADIShvanugatasyaite varNavisheShA iti /
katham /
asau vA AdityaH piN^galo varNata eSha AdityaH shuklo 'pyeSha nIla eSha pIta eSha lohita Aditya eva //1 //

START ChUp 8,6.2

#<tad yathA mahApatha Atata ubhau grAmau gacchatImaM cAmuM caivam evaitA Adityasya rashmaya ubhau lokau gacchantImaM cAmuM ca |
amuShmAd AdityAt pratAyante tA Asu nADIShu sR^iptAH |
Abhyo nADIbhyaH pratAyante te 'muShminn Aditye sR^iptAH || ChUp_8,6.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,6.2 tasyAdhyAtmaM nADIbhiH kathaM saMbandha ityatra dR^iShTAntamAha-tattatra yathA loke mahAnvistIrNaH panthA mahApatha Atato vyApta ubhau gacchatImaM ca saMnihitamamuM ca viprakR^iShTaM dUrasthamevaM yathA dR^iShTAnto mahApatha ubhau grAmau praviShTa evamevaitA Adityasya rashmaya ubhau lokAvamuM cA'dityamaNDalamimaM ca puruShaM gacchantyubhayatra praviShTAH /
yathA mahApathaH /
katham /
amuShmAdAdityamaNDalAtpratAyante saMtatA bhavanti /
tA adhyAtmamAsu piN^galAdivarNAsu yathoktAsu nADIShu sR^iptA gatAH praviShTA ityarthaH /
Abhyo nADIbhyaH pratAyante pravR^ittAH santAnabhUtAH satyaste 'muShmin /
rashmInAmubhayaliN^gatvAtta ityucyante //2 //


_______________________________________________________________________


START ChUp 8,6.3

#<tad yatraitat suptaH samastaH saMprasannaH svapnaM na vijAnAti |
Asu tadA nADIShu sR^ipto bhavati |
taM na kashcana pApmA spR^ishati |
tejasA hi tadA saMpanno bhavati || ChUp_8,6.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,6.3 tattatraivaM sati yatra yasminkAla etatsvapanamayaM jIvaH supto bhavati /
svApasya dviprakAratvAdvisheShaNaM samasta iti /
upasaMhR^itasarvakaraNavR^ittirityetat /
ato bAhyaviShayasaMparkajanitakAluShyAbhAvAtsamyak /
prasannaH saMprasanno bhavati /
ata eva svapnaM viShayAkArAbhAsaM mAnasaM svapnapratyayaM na vijAnAti nAnubhavatItyarthaH /
yadaivaM supto bhavatyAsu sauratejaHpUrNAsu yathoktAsu nADIShu tadA sR^iptaH praviShTo nADIbhirdvArabhUtAbhirhR^idayAkAshaM gato bhavatItyarthaH /
na hyanyatra satsaMpatteH svapnAdarshanamastIti sAmarthyAnnADIShviti saptamI tR^itIyayA pariNamyate /
taM satA saMpannaM na kashcana na kashcidapi dharmAdharmarUpaH pApmA spR^ishatIti svarUpAvasthitatvAttadA'tmanaH /
dehendriyavishiShTaM hi sukhaduHkhakAryapradAnena pApmA spR^ishatIti na tu satsaMpannaM svarUpAvasthaM kashcidapi pApmA spraShTumutsahate /
aviShayatvAt /
anyo hyanyasya viShayo bhavati na tvanyatvaM kenacitkutashcidapi satsaMpannasya /
svarUpapracyavanaM tvAtmano jAgratsvapnAvasthAM prati gamanaM bAhyaviShayapratibodho 'vidyAkAmakarmabIjasya brahmavidyAhutAshAdAhanimittamityavocAma ShaShTha eva tadihApi pratyetavyam /
yadaivaM suptaH saureNa tejasA hi nADyantargatena sarvataH saMpanno vyApto bhavati /
ato visheSheNa cakShurAdinADIdvArairbAhyaviShayabhogAyAprasR^itAni karaNAnyasya tadA bhavanti /
tasmAdayaM karaNAnAM nirodhAtsvAtmanyevAvasthitaH svapnaM na vijAnAtIti yuktam //3 //

START ChUp 8,6.4

#<atha yatraitad abalimAnaM nIto bhavati |

ChUpBh_8,6.4 tatraivaM satyatha yatra yasminkAle 'balimAnamabalabhAvaM dehasya rogAdinimittaM jarAdinimittaM vA kR^ishIbhAvametannayanaM nItaH prApito devadatto bhavati mumUrSharyadA bhavatItyarthaH /

START ChUp 8,6.5

#<atha yatraitad asmAc charIrAd utkrAmati |

ChUpBh_8,6.5 atha yatra yadaitatkriyAvisheShaNamityasmAccharIrAdutkrAmati /

START ChUp 8,6.6

#<tad eSha shlokaH |

START ChUp 8,7.1

#<ya AtmA apahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityur vishoko vijighatso 'pipAsaH satyakAmaH satyasaMkalpaH so 'nveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH |

ChUpBh_8,7.1 "atha ya eSha saMprasAdo 'smAccharIrAtsamutthAya paraM jyotirupasaMpadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata eSha Atmeti hovAcaitadamR^itamabhayametadbrahma"ityuktam /

START ChUp 8,7.2

#<tad dhobhaye devAsurA anububudhire |

ChUpBh_8,7.2 taddhobhaya ityAdyAkhyAyikAprayojanamuktam /

START ChUp 8,7.3

#<tau ha dvAtriMshataM varShANi brahmacaryam UShatuH |

tau hocatur ya AtmA apahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityur vishoko vijighatso 'pipAsaH satyakAmaH satyasaMkalpaH so 'nveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH |

ChUpBh_8,7.3 tau ha gatvA dvAtriMshataM varShANi shushrUShAparau bhUtvA brahmacaryamUShaturuShitavantau /

START ChUp 8,7.4

#<tau ha prajApatir uvAca ya eSho 'kShiNi puruSho dR^iShyata eSha Atmeti hovAca |

atha yo 'yaM bhagavo 'psu parikhyAyate yash cAyam Adarshe katama eSha iti |

__________


ChUpBh_8,7.4 tAvevaM tapasvinau shuddhakalmaShau yogyAvupalabhya prajApatiruvAcaha-ya eSho 'kShiNi puruSho nivR^ittacakShurbhirmR^iditakaShAyairdR^ishyate yogibhirdraShTA, eSha AtmApahatapApmAdiguNo yamavocaM purAhaM yadvij~nAnAtsarvalokakAmAvAptiretadamR^itaM bhamAkhyamata evAbhayamata eva brahma vR^iddhatamamiti /

gR^ihItvA ca dR^iDhIkaraNAya prajApatiM pR^iShTavantau /
atha yo 'yaM he bhagavo 'psu parikhyAyate parisamantAjj~nAyate yashcAyamAdarsha AtmanaH pratibimbAkAraH parikhyAyate khaDgAdau ca katama eSha eShAM bhagavadbhiruktaH kiMvaika eva sarveShviti /
evaM pR^iShTaH prajApatiruvAca-eSha u eva yashcakShuShi draShTA mayokta iti /
etanmanasi kR^itvaiShu sarveShvanteShu madhyeShu parikhyAyata iti hovAca /
nanu kathaM yuktaM shiShyorviparItagrahaNamanuj~nAtuM prajApatervigatadoShasyA'cAryasya sataH /
satyameva, nAnuj~nAtam /
katham /
AtmanyadhyAropitapANDityamahattvaboddhR^itvau hIndravirocanau tathaiva ca prathitau loke /
tau yadi prajApatinA mUDhau yuvAM viparItagrAhiNAvityuktau syAtAM tatastastayoshcitte duHkhaM syAttajjanitAcca cittAvasAdAtpunaH prashnashravaNagrahaNAvadhAraNaM pratyutsAhavidhAtaH syAdato rakShaNIyau shiShyAviti manyate prajApatiH /
gR^ihNItAM tAvattadudasharAvadR^iShTAntenApaneShyAmIti ca /
nanu na yuktameSha u evetyanR^itaM vaktum /
na cAnR^itamuktam /
katham /

tamevAvocadeSha u evetyato nAnR^itamuktaM prajApatinA /

START ChUp 8,8.1

#<udasharAva AtmAnam avekShya yad Atmano na vijAnIthas tan me prabrUtam iti |
tau hodasharAve 'vekShAM cakrAte |
tau ha prajApatir uvAca kiM pashyatha iti |
tau hocatuH sarvam evedam AvAM bhagava AtmAnaM pashyAva A lomabhyaH A nakhebhyaH pratirUpam iti || ChUp_8,8.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,8.1 udasharAva udakapUrNe sharAvAdAvAtmAnamavekShyAnantaraM yattatrA'tmAnaM pashyantau na vijAnIthastanme mama prabrUtamAcakShIyAthAmityuktau tau ha tathaivodasharAve 'vekShAJNcakrAte 'vekShaNaM cakratuH /
tathA kR^itavantau tau ha prajApatiruvAca kiM pashyatha iti /
nanu tanme prabrUtamityuktAbhyAmudasharAve 'vekShaNaM kR^itvA prajApataye na niveditamidamAvAbhyAM na viditamityanivedite cAj~nAnahetau ha prajApatiruvAca kiM pashyatha iti tatra ko 'bhiprAya iti /
ucyate-naiva tayoridamAvayoraviditamityAshaN^kAbhUcchAyAtmanyAtmapratyayo nishcita evA'sIt /
yena vakShyati tau ha shAntahR^idayau pravavrajaturiti /
na hyanishcite 'bhipretArthe prashAntahR^idayatvamupapadyate /
tena nocaturidamAvAbhyAmaviditamiti /
viparItagrAhiNau ca shiShyAvanupekShaNIyAviti svayameSha papraccha kiM pashyatha iti, viparItanishcayApanayAya ca vakShyati sAdhvalakR^itAvityevamAdi /
tau hocatuH-sarvamevedamAvAM bhagava AtmAnaM pashyAva A lomabhya A nakhebhyaH pratirUpamiti, yathaivA'vAM he bhagavo lomanakhAdimantau sva evamevedaM lomanakhAdisahitamAvayoH pratirUpamudasharAve pashyAva iti //1 //

START ChUp 8,8.2

#<tau ha prajApatir uvAca sAdhvalaMkR^itau suvasanau pariShkR^itau bhUtvodasharAve 'vekShethAm iti |
tau ha sAdhvalaMkR^itau suvasanau pariShkR^itau bhUtvodasharAve 'vekShAM cakrAte |
tau ha prajApatir uvAca kiM pashyatha iti || ChUp_8,8.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,8.2 tau ha punaH prajApatiruvAca cchAyAtmanishcayApanayAya, sAdhvalaN^kR^itau yathA svagR^ihe suvasanau mahArhavastraparidhAnau pariShkR^itau chinnalomanakhau ca bhUtvodasharAve tayoshchAyAtmagraho 'panItaH syAt /
sAdhvalaN^kArasuvasanAdInAmAgantukAnAM chAyAkaratvamudasharAve yathA sharIrasaMbaddhAnAmevaM sharIrasyApi cchAyAkaratvaM pUrvaM babhUveti gamyate /
sharIraikadeshAnAM ca lomanakhAdInAM nityatvenAbhipretAnAmakhaNDitAnAM chAyAkaratvaM pUrvamAsIt /
chinneShu ca teShu naiva lomanakhAdicchAyA dR^ishyate 'to lomanakhAdivaccharIrasyApyAgamApAyitvaM siddhamityudasharAvAdau dR^ishyamAnasya tannimittasya ca dehasyAnAtmatvaM siddham udashArAvAdau chAyAkaratvAddehasaMbaddhAlaN^kArAdivat /
na kevalametAvadetena yAvatkiJNcidAtmIyatvAbhimataM sukhaduHkharAgadveShamohAdi ca kAdAcitkatvAnnakhalomAdivadanAtmeti pratyetavyam /
evamasheShamithyAgrahApanayanimitte sAdhvalaN^kArAdidR^iShTAnte prajApatinokte shrutvA tathA kR^itavatorapi cchAyAtmaviparItagraho nApajagAma yasmAttasmAtsvadoSheNaiva kenacitpratibaddhavivekavij~nAnAvindravirocanAvabhUtAmit i gamyate /
tau pUrvavadeva dR^iDhanishcayau papraccha kiM pashyatha iti //2 //

START ChUp 8,8.3

#<tau hocatur yathaivedam AvAM bhagavaH sAdhvalaMkR^itau suvasanau pariShkR^itau sva evam evemau bhagavaH sAdhvallaMkR^itau suvasanau pariShkR^itAv iti |
eSha Atmeti hovAca |

ChUpBh_8,8.3 tau tathaiva pratipanno yathaivedamiti pUrvavadyathA sAdhvalaN^kArAdivishiShTAvAvAM sva evamevemau chAyAtmAnAviti sutarAM viparItanishcayau babhUvatuH /

START ChUp 8,8.4

#<tau hAnvIkShya prajApatir uvAca |
anupalabhyAtmAnam ananuvidya vrajato yatara etadupaniShado bhaviShyanti devA vA asurA vA te parAbhaviShyantIti |
sa ha shAntahR^idaya eva virocano 'surA¤ jagAma |

__________


ChUpBh_8,8.4 evaM tayorgatayorindravirocanayo rAj~norbhogAsaktayoryathoktavismaraNaM syAdityAshaN^kyApratyakShaM pratyakShavacanena ca cittaduHkhaM parijihIrShustau dUraM gacchantAvanvIkShya ya AtmApahatapApmetyAdivacanavadetadapyanayoH shravaNagocaratvameShyatIti matvovAca prajApatiH /

te kiM, parAbhaviShyanti shreyomArgAtparAbhUtA bahirbhUtA vinaShTA bhaviShyantItyarthaH /
svagR^ihaM gacchatoH surAsurarAjayoryo 'surarAjaH sa ha shAntahR^idaya eva sanvirocano 'surAJNjagAma /
gatvA ca tebhyo 'surebhyaH sharIrAtmabuddhiryopaniShattAmetAmupaniShadaM provAcoktavAn /
dehamAtramevA'tmA pitrokta iti /

ihalokaparalokayoreva sarve lokAH kAmAshcAntarbhavantIti rAj~no 'bhiprAyaH //4 //

START ChUp 8,8.5

#<tasmAd apyaddyehAdadAnam ashraddadhAnam ayajamAnam Ahur Asuro bateti |

ChUpBh_8,8.5 tasmAttatsaMpradAyo 'dyApyanuvartata itIha loke 'dadAnaM dAnamakurvANamavibhAgashIlamashraddadhAnaM satkAryeShu shraddhArahitaM yathAshaktyayajamAnamayajanasvabhAvamAhurAsuraH khalvayaM yata evaMsvabhAvo bateti khidyamAnA AhuH shiShTAH /

START ChUp 8,9.1

#<atha hendro 'prApyaiva devAn etad bhayaM dadarsha |
yathaiva khalv ayam asmi¤ charIre sAdhvalaMkR^ite sAdhvalaMkR^ito bhavati suvasane suvasanaH pariShkR^ite pariShkR^ita evam evAyam asminn andhe 'ndho bhavati srAme srAmaH parivR^ikNe parivR^ikNaH |
asyaiva sharIrasya nAsham anv eSha nashyati |
nAham atra bhogyaM pashyAmIti || ChUp_8,9.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,9.1 atha ha kilendro 'prApyaiva devAndaivyAkrauryAdisaMpadA yuktatvAdgurorvacanaM punaH punaH smaranneva gacchannetadvakShyamANaM bhayaM svAtmagrahaNanimittaM dadarsha dR^iShTavAn /
udasharAvadR^iShTAntena prajApatinA yadartho nyAya uktastadekadesho maghavataH pratyabhAdbuddhau /
yena cchAyAtmagrahaNe doShaM dadarsha /
katham /
yathaiva khalvayamasmiJNcharIre sAdhvalaN^kR^ite chAyAtmApi sAdhvalaN^kR^ito bhavati suvasane ca suvasanaH pariShkR^ite pariShkR^ito yathA nakhalomAdidehAvayavApagame chAyAtmApi pariShkR^ito bhavati nakhalomAdirahito bhavati /
evamevAyaM chAyAtmApyasmiJNcharIre nakhalomAdibhirdehAvayavatvasya tulyatvAdandhe cakShuSho 'pagame 'ndho bavati srAme srAmaH /
srAmaH kilekanetrastasyAndhatvena gatatvAt /
cakShurnAsikA vA yasya sadA sravati sa srAmaH /
parivR^ikNashchinnahastashchinnapAdo vA /
srAme parivR^ikNe vA dehe chAyAtmApi tathA bhavati /
tathAsya dehasya nAshamanveSha nashyati //1 //

START ChUp 8,9.2

#<sa samitpANiH punar eyAya |
taM ha prajApatir uvAca |
maghavan yac chAntahR^idayaH prAvrAjIH sArdhaM virocanena kim icchan punar Agama iti |
sa hovAca yathA eva khalvayyaM bhagavo 'smi¤ charIre sAdhvalaMkR^ite sAdhvalaMkR^ito bhavati suvasane suvasanaH pariShkR^ite pariShkR^ita evam evAyam asminn andhe 'ndho bhavati srAme srAmaH parivR^ikNe parivR^ikNaH |
asyaiva sharIrasya nAsham anv eSha nashyati |
nAham atra bhogyaM pashyAmIti || ChUp_8,9.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,9.2 ato nAhamatrAsmiMshchAyAtmadarshane dehAtmadarshane vA bhogyaM phalaM pashyAmItyevaM doShaM dehacchAyAtmadarshane 'dhyavasya sa samitpANirbrahmacaryaM vastuM punareyAya /
taM ha prajApatiruvAca-maghavanyacchAntahR^idayaH prAvrAjIH pragatavAnasi virocanena sArdhaM kimicchanpunarAgama iti /
vijAnannapi punaH papracchendrAbhiprayAbhivyaktaye yadvettha tena mopasIdeti yadvat /
tathA ca svAbhiprayAM prakaTamakarodyathaiva khalvayamityadi, evameveti cAnvamodata prajApatiH /
nanu tulye 'kShipuruShashravame dehacchAyAmindro 'grahIdAtmeti dehameva va virocanastatkiMnimittam /
tatra manyate /
yathendrasyodasharAvAdiprajApativacanaM smarato devAnaprAptasyaivA'cAryoktabuddhyA chAyAtmagrahaNaM tatra doShadarshanaM cAbhUt /
na tathA virocanasya kiM tarhi deha evA'tmadarshanaM nApi tatra doShadarshanaM babhUva /
tadvadeva vidyAgrahaNasAmarthyapratibandhadoShAlpatvabahutvApekShamindravirocanayoshchAyAtmadehayorgrahaNam /

indro 'lpadoShatvAddR^ishyata itishrutyarthameva shraddadhAnatayA jagrAhetarashchAyAnimittaM dehaM hitvA shrutyarthaM lakShaNayA jagrAha prajApatinokto 'yamiti doShabhUyastvAt /
yathA kila nIlAnIlayorAdarshe dR^ishyamAnayorvAsasoryannIlaM tanmahArhamiti cchAyAnimittaM vAsa evocyate na cchAyA tadvaditi virocanAbhiprAyaH /
svacittaguNadoShavashAdeva hi shabdArthAvadhAraNaM tulye 'pi shravaNe khyApitaM dAmyata datta dayadhvamiti dakAramAtrashravaNAcchutyantare /
nimittAnyapi tadanuguNAnyeva sahakArINi bhavanti //2 //

START ChUp 8,9.3

#<evam evaiSha maghavann iti hovAca |
etaM tv eva te bhUyo 'nuvyAkhyAsyAmi |
vasAparANi dvAtriMshataM varShANIti |
sa hAparANi dvAtriMshataM varShANyuvAsa |
tasmai hovAca || ChUp_8,9.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,9.3 evamevaiSha maghavansamyaktvayAvagataM na cchAyAtmetyuvAca prajApatiryo mayokta AtmA prakR^ita etamevA'tmAnaM tu te bhUyaH pUrvaM vyAkhyAtamapyanuvyAkhyAsyAmi /
yasmAtsakR^idvyAkhyAtaM doSharahitAnAmavadhAraNaviShayaM prAptamapi nAgrahIrataH kenaciddoSheNa pratibaddhagrahaNasAmarthastvamatastatkShapaNAya vasAparANi dvAtriMshataM varShANItyuktvA tathoShitavate kShapitadoShAya tasmai hovAca //3//

START ChUp 8,10.1

#<ya eSha svapne mahIyamAnash caraty eSha Atmeti hovAca |
etad amR^itam abhayam etad brahmeti |
sa ha shAntahR^idayaH pravavrAja |
sa hAprApyaiva devAn etad bhayaM dadarsha |
tad yady apIdaM sharIram andhaM bhavaty anandhaH sa bhavati yadi srAmam asrAmaH |
naivaiSho 'sya doSheNa duShyati || ChUp_8,10.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,10.1 ya AtmApahatapApmAdilakShaNo ya eSho 'kShiNItyAdinA vyAkhyAta eSha saH /
ko 'sau /
yaH svapne mahIyamAnaH stryAdibhiH pUjyamAnashcaratyanekavidhAnsvapnabhogAnanubhavatItyarthaH /
eSha Atmeti hovAcetyAdi samAnam /
sa haivamukta indraH shAntahR^idayaH pravavrAja /
sa hAprApyaiva devAnpUrvavadasminnapyAtmani bhayaM dadarsha /
katham /
tadidaM sharIraM yadyapyandhaM dhavati svapnAtmA yo 'nandhaH sa bhavati /
yadi srAmamidaM sharIramasrAmashca sa bhavati naivaiSha svapnAtmAsya dehasya doSheNa duShyati //1 //

START ChUp 8,10.2-4

#<na vadhenAsya hanyate |

#<sa samitpANiH punar eyAya |

#<na vadhenAsya hanyate |
nAsya srAmyeNa srAmaH |
ghnanti tv ivainam |
vicchAdayantIva |
apriyavetteva bhavati |
api roditIva |

__________


ChUpBh_8,10.2-3-4 nApyasya vadhena sa hanyate chAyAtmavanna cAsya srAmyeNa srAmaH svapnAtmA bhavati /
yadadhyAyAdAvAgamamAtreNopanyastaM nAsya jarayaitajjIryatItyAdi tadiha nyAyenopapAdayitumupanyastam /
na tAvadayaM chAyAtmavaddehadoShayuktaH kintu dhnanti tvevainam /
evashabda ivArthe /
ghnantIvainaM kecaneti draShTavyam /
prajApatiM pramANIkurvato 'nR^itavAditvApAdanAnupapatteH /
etadamR^itamityetatprajApativacanaM kathaM mR^iShA kuryAdindrastaM pramANIkurvan /
nanu cchAyApuruShe prajApatinokte 'sya sharIrasya nAshamanveSha nashyatIti doShamabhyadhAttathehApi syAt /
naivam /
kasmAt /
ya eSho 'kShiNi puruSho dR^ishyata iti manyate tadA kathaM prajApatiM pramANIkR^itya punaH shravaNAya samitpANirgacchet /
jagAma ca /
tasmAnna cchAyAtmA prajApatinokta iti manyate /
tathA ca vyAkhyAtaM draShTAkShiNi dR^ishyata iti /
tathA vicchAdayantIva vidrAvayantIva tathA ca putrAdimaraNanimittamapriyavetteva bhavati /
api ca svayamapi roditIva /
nanvapriyaM vettyeva kathaM vetteveti /
ucyate-na amR^itAbhayatvavacanAnupapatteH /
dhyAyatIveti ca shrutyantarAt /
nanu pratyakShavirodha iti cet /
na /
sharIrAtmatvapratyakShavadbhrAntisaMbhavAt /
tiShThatu tAvadapriyavetteva na veti /
nAhamatra bhogyaM pashyAmi /
svapnAtmaj~nAne 'pIShTaM phalaM nopalabha ityabhiprAyaH. evamevaiSha tavAbhiprAyeNeti vAkyaseShaH /
Atmano 'mR^itAbhayaguNavattvasyAbhipretatvAt /
dviruktamapi nyAyato mayA yathAvannAvadhArayati /
tasmAtpUrvavadasyAdyApi pratibandhakAraNamastIti manvAnastatkShapaNAya vasAparANi dvAtriMshataM varShANi brahmacaryamityAdidesha prajApatiH /
tathoShitavate kShapitakalmaShAyA'ha //2-3-4 //
#<iti cchAndogyopaniShadi aShTamAdhyAyasya dashamaH khaNDaH>#

START ChUp 8,11.1-2

#<tad yatraitat suptaH samastaH saMprasannaH svapnaM na vijAnAtyeSha Atmeti hovAca |
etad amR^itam abhayam etad brahmeti |
sa ha shAntahR^idayaH pravavrAja |

nAha khalv ayam evaM saMpraty AtmAnaM jAnAty ayam aham asmIti |

nAham atra bhogyaM pashyAmIti || ChUp_8,11.1 ||>#

#<sa samitpANiH punar eyAya |
taM ha prajApatir uvAca - maghavan yac chAntahR^idayaH prAvrAjIH kim icchan punar Agama iti |
sa hovAca nAha khalv ayaM bhagava evaM saMpraty AtmAnaM jAnAty ayam aham asmIti |
no evemAni bhUtAni |
vinAsham evApIto bhavati |
nAham atra bhogyaM pashyAmIti || ChUp_8,11.2 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,11.1-2 pUrvavadetaM tveva ta ityAdyuktvA tadyatraitatsupta ityadi vyAkhyAtaM vAkyam /
akShiNi yo draShTA svapne ca mahIyamAnashcarati sa eSha suptaH samastaH saMprasannaH svapnaM na vijAnAtyeSha Atmeti hovAcaitadamR^itamabhayametadbrahmeti svAbhipretameva /
maghavAMstatrApi doShaM dadarsha /
katham /
nAha naiva suShuptastho 'pyAtmA khalvayaM saMprati samyagidAnIM cA'tmAnaM jAnAti naivaM jAnAti /
katham /
ayamahamasmIti no evemAni bhUtAni ceti /
yathA jAgrati svapne vA /
ato vinAshameva vinAshamiveti pUrvavaddraShTavyam /
apIto 'pigato bhavati, vinaShTa iva bhavatItyabhiprAyaH /
j~nAne hi sati j~nAtuH sadbhAvo 'vagamyate nAsati j~nAne /
na ca suShuptasya j~nAnaM dR^ishyate 'to vinaShTa ivetyabhiprAyaH na tu vinAshamevA'tmano manyate 'mR^itAbhayavacanasya prAmANyamicchan //1-2 //

START ChUp 8,11.3

#<evam evaiSha maghavann iti hovAca |
etaM tv eva te bhUyo 'nuvyAkhyAsyAmi |

sa hAparANi paJNca varShANyuvAsa |
tAny ekashataM saMpeduH |
etat tad yad AhuH |
ekashataM ha vai varShANi maghavAn prajApatau brahmacaryam uvAsa |
tasmai hovAca || ChUp_8,11.3 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,11.3 pUrvavadevamevetyuktvA yo mayoktasribhiH paryAyaistamevaitaM no evAnyatraitasmAdAtmano 'nyaM kaJNcana kiM tarhyetameva vyAkhyAsyAmi /
svalpastu doShastavAvashiShTastatkShapaNAya vasAparANyanyAni paJNca varShANItyuktaH sa tathA cakAra /
tasmai mR^iditakaShAyAdidoShAya sthAnatrayadoShasaMbandharahitamAtmanaHsvarUpamapahatapApmatvAdilakShaNaM maghavate tasmai hovAca /
tAnyekashataM varShANi saMpeduH saMpannAni babhUvuH /
yadAhurloke shiShTA ekashataM ha vai varShANi maghavAnprajApatau brahmacaryamuvAseti tadetaddvAtriMshatamityAdinA darshitamityAkhyAyikAto 'pasR^itya shrutyocyate /
evaM kilaitadindratvAdapi gurutaramindreNApi mahatA yatnenaikottaravarShashatakR^itAyAsena prAptamAtmaj~nAnamato nAtaH paraM puruShArthAntaramastItyAtmaj~nAnaM stauti //3//
