START ChUp 8,12.1

#<maghavan martyaM vA idaM sharIram AttaM mR^ityunA |
tad asyAmR^itasyAsharIrasyAtmano 'dhiShThAnam |
Atto vai sasharIraH priyApriyAbhyAm |
na vai sasharIrasya sataH priyApriyayor apahatir asti |
asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishataH || ChUp_8,12.1 ||>#

__________


ChUpBh_8,12.1 maghavanmartyaM vai maraNadharmIdaM sharIram /
yanmanyase 'kShyAdhArAdilakShaNaH saMprasAdalakShaNa AtmA mayokto vinAshamevApIto bhavatIti /
shR^iNu tatra kAraNam /
yadidaM sharIraM vai tadetanmartyaM vinAshi /
taccA'ttaM mR^ityunA grastaM satatameva /
kadAcideva mriyata iti martyamityukte na tathA saMtrAso bhavati yathA grastameva sadA vyAptameva mR^ityunetyukta iti vairAgyArthaM visheSha ityucyata AttaM mR^ityuneti /
kathaM nAma dehAbhimAnato viraktaH sannivartata iti /
sharIramityatra sahendriyamanobhirucyate /
taccharIramasya saMprasAdasya tristhAnatayA gamyamAnasyAmR^itasya maraNAdidehandriyamanodharmavarjitasyetyetat /
amR^itasyetyanenaivAsharIratve siddhe punarasharIrasyeti vacanaM vAyvAdivatsAvayavatvamUrtimattve mA bhUtAmityAtmanaH /
Atmano vA sata IkShitustejobannAdikrameNotpannamadhiShThAnam /
jIvarUpeNa pravishya sadevAdhitiShThatyasminniti vAdhiShThAnam /
yasyedamIdR^ishaM nityameva mR^ityugrastaM dharmAdharmajanitatvAtpriyApriyavadadhiShThAnaM tadadhiShThitastadvAnsasharIro bhavati /
asharIrasvabhAvasyA'tmanastadevAhaM sharIraM sharIrameva cAhamityavivekAdAtmabhAvaH sasharIratvaM ata eva sasharIraH sannAtto grastaH priyApriyAbhyAm /
prasiddhametat /
tasya ca na vai sasharIrasya sataH priyApriyayorbAhyaviShayasaMyogaviyoganimittayorbAhyaviShayasaMyogaviyogau mameti manyamAnasyApahatirvinAsha ucchedaH santatirUpayornAstIti /
taM punardehAbhimAnAdasharIrasvarUpavij~nAnena vinartitAvivekaj~nAnasharIraM santaM priyApriye na spR^ishataH /
spR^ishiH pratyekaM saMbadhyata iti priyaM na spR^ishatyapriyaM na spR^ishatIti vAkyadvayaM bhavati /
"na mlecchAshucyadhArmikaiH saha saMbhAShete"ti yadvat /
dharmAdharmakArye hi te /
asharIratA tu svarUpamiti tatra dharmAdharmayorasaMbhavAttatkAryabhAvo dUrata evetyato na priyApriye spR^ishataH /
nanu yadi priyamapyasharIraM na spR^ishatIti yanmaghavatoktaM suShuptastho vinAshamevApIto bhavatIti tadevehApyApannam /
naiSha doShaH dharmAdharmakAryayoH sharIrasaMbandhinoH priyApriyayoH pratiShedhasya vivakShitatvAt asharIraM na priyApriye spR^ishata iti /
AgamApAyinorhi sparshashabdo dR^iShTo yathA shItasparsha uShNasparsha iti na tvagneruShNaprakAshayoH svabhAvabhUtayoragninA sparsha iti bhavati tathAgneH saviturvoShNaprakAshavatsvarUpabhUtasyA'nandasya priyasyApi neha pratiShedhaH"vij~nAnamAnandaM brahma" "Anando brahma"ityAdishrutibhyaH /
ihApi bhUmaiva sukhamityuktatvAt /
nanu bhUmnaH priyasyaikatve 'saMvedyatvAtsvarUpeNa vA nityasaMvedyatvAnnirvisheShateti nendrasya tadiShTam /
"nAha khalvayaM saMpratyAtmAnaM jAnAtyayamahamasmIti no evomAni bhUtAni vinAshamevApIto bhavati nAhamatra bhogyaM pashyAmi"ityuktatvAt /
taddhondrasyeShTaM yadbhatAni cA'tmAnaM ca jAnAti na cApriyaM kiJNcidvetti sa sarvAMshca lokAnApnoti sarvAMshca kAmAnyena j~nAnena satyametadiShTamindrasyemAni bhUtAni matto 'nyAni lokAH kAmAshca sarve matto 'nye 'hameShAM svAmIti /
na tvetadindrasya hitam /
hitaM cendrasya prajApatinA vaktavyam /
vyomavadasharIrAtmatayA sarvabhUtalokakAmAtmatvopagamena yA prAptistaddhitamindrAya vaktavyamiti prajApatinAbhipretam /
na tu rAj~no rAjyAptivadanyatvena /
tatraivaM sati kaM kena vijAnIyAdAtmaikatva imAni bhUtAnyayamahamasmIti /
nanvasminpakShe"strIbhirvA yAnairvA" "sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmaH" "sa ekadhA bhavati"ityAdyaishvaryashrutayo 'nupapannAH /
na /
sarvAtmanaH sarvaphalasaMbandhopapatteravirodhAt /
mR^ida iva sarvaghacakarakakuNDAdyAptiH /
nanu sarvAtmatve duHkhasaMbandho 'pi syAditi cenna, duHkhasyApyAtmatvopagamAdavirodhaH /
AtmanyavidyAkalpanAnimittAni duHkhAni rajjvAmiva sarpAdikalpanAnimittAni /
sAcAvidyAsharIrAtmaikatvasvarUpadarshanena duHkhanimittocchinneni duHkhasaMbandhAshaN^kA na saMbhavati /
shuddhasattvasaMkalpanimittAnAM tu kAmAnAmIshvaradehasaMbandhaH sarvabhUteShu mAnasAnAM para eva sarvasattvopAdhidvAreNa bhokteti sarvAvidyAkR^itasaMvyavahArANAM para evA'tmA'spadaM nAnyo 'stIti vedAntasiddhAntaH /
ya eSho 'kShiNi puruSho dR^ishyati iti cchAyApuruSha eva prajApatinoktaH /
svapnasuShuptayoshcAnya eva /
na paro 'pahatapApmatvAdilakShaNo virodhAditi kecinmanyante /
chAyAdyAtmanAM copadeshe prayojanamAcakShate /
AdAvevocyamAne kila durvij~neyatvAtparasyA'tmano 'tyantabAhyaviShayAsaktacetaso 'tyantasUkShmavastushravaNe vyAmoho mA bhUditi /
yathA kila dvitIyAyAM sUkShmaM candraM didarshayiShurvR^ikShaM kaJNcitpratyakShamAdau darshayati pashyAmumeSha candra iti, tato 'nyaM tato 'pyanyaM girimUrdhAnaM ca candrasamIpasthaM eSha candra iti tato 'sau candraM pashyati, evametadya eSho 'kShiNItyAdyuktaM prajApatinA tribhiH paryAyairna para iti /
caturthe tu paryAye dehAnmartyAtsamutthAyAsharIratAmApanno jyotiHsvarUpam /
yasminnuttamapuruShe stryAdibhirjakShatkrIDanramamANo bhavati sa uttmaH puruShaH para ukta iti cA'huH /
satyaM, ramaNIyA tAvadiyaM vyAkhyA shrotum /
na tvartho 'sya granthasyaivaM saMbhavati /
katham /
akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyata ityupanyasya shiShyAbhyAM chAyAtmani gR^ihIte tayostadviparItagrahaNaM matvA tadapanayAyodasharAvopanyAsaH kiM pashyatha iti ca prashnaH sAdhvalaN^kAropadeshashcAnarthakaH syAt yadi cchAyAtmaiva prajApatinAkShiNi dR^ishyata ityupadiShTaH /
kiJNca yadi svayamupadiShTa iti grahaNasyApyapanayakAraNaM vaktavyaM syAt /
svapnasuShuptAtmagrahaNayorapi tadapanayakAraNaM ca svayaM brUyAt na coktaM[tenaTatena manyAmahe nAkShiNi cchAyAtmA prajApatinopadiShTaH /

kiM cAnyadakShiNi draShTA ceddR^ishyata ityupadiShTaH syAttata idaM yuktam /
etaM tveva ta ityuktvA svapne 'pi draShTurevopadeshaH /
svapne na draShTopadiShTa iti cenna /
api roditIvApriyavettevetyupadeshAt /
na ca draShTuranyaH kashcitsvapne mahIyamAnashcarati /
atrAyaM puruShaH svayaJNjyotiriti nyAyataH shrutyantare siddhatvAt /
yadyapi svapne sadhIrbhavati tathApi na dhIH svapnabhogopalabdhiM prati karaNatvaM bhajate /
kiM tarhi paTacitravajjAgradvAsanAshrayA dR^ishyaiva dhIrbhavatIti na draShTuH svayaJNjyotiShTvabAdhaH syAt /
kiJNcAnyat /
jAgratsvapnyorbhUtAni cA'tmAnaM ca jAnAtImAni bhUtAnyayamahamasmIti /
prAptau satyAM pratiShedho yuktaH syAnnAha khalvayamityAdi /
tathA cetanasyaivAvidyAnimittayoH sharIratve sati priyApriyayorapahatirnAstItyuktvA tasyaivAsharIrasya sato vidyAyAM satyAM sasharIratve prAptayoH pratiShedho yukto 'sharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishata iti /
ekashcA'tmA svapnabuddhAntayormahAmatsyavadasaN^gaH saMcaratIti shrutyantare siddham /
yaccoktaM saMprasAdaH sharIrAtsamutthAya yasminstryAdibhI ramamANo bhavati so 'nyaH saMprasAdAdadhikaraNanirdiShTa uttamaH puruSha iti /
tadapyasat /
caturthe 'pi paryAya eta tveva ta iti vacanAt /
yadi tato 'nyo 'bhipretaH syAtpUrvavadetaM tveva ta iti na brUyAnmR^iShA prajApatiH /
kiJNcAnyattejobannAdInAM sraShTuH sataH svavikAradehashuN^ge praveshaM darshayitvA praviShTAya puvastattvamasItyupadesho mR^iShA prasajyeta /
tasmiMstvaM stryAdibhI rantA bhaviShyasIti yukta upadesho 'bhaviShyadyadi saMprasAdAdanya uttamaH puruSho bhavet /
tathA bhUmnyahamevetyAdishyA'tmaivedaM sarvamiti nopasamahariShyadyadi bhUmA jIvAdanyo 'bhaviShyat /
"nAnyo 'to 'sti draShTA"ityAdishrutyantarAcca /
sarvashrutiShu ca parasminnAtmashabdaprayogo nAbhaviShyatpratyagAtmA cetsarvajantUnAM para AtmA na bhavettasmAdeka evA'tmA prakaraNI siddhaH /
na cA'tmanaH saMsAritvam /
avidyAdhyastatvAdAtmani saMsArasya /
na hi rajjushuktikAgaganAdiShu sarparajatamalAdIni mithyAj~nAnAdhyastAni teShAM bhavantIti /
etena sasharIrasya priyApriyayorapahatirnAstIti vyAkhyAtam /
yaccasthitamapriyavetteveti nApriyavettaiveti siddham /
evaM ca sati sarvaparyAyeShvetadamR^itabhayametadbrahmeti prajApatervacanam /
yadi vA prajApaticchadbharUpAyAH shrutervacanaM satyameva bhavet /
na catatkutarkabuddhyA mR^iShA kartuM yuktam /
tato gurutarasya pramANAntarasyAnupapatteH /
nanu pratyakShaM duHkhAdyapriyavettR^itvamavyabhicAryanubhUyata iti cenna /
jarAdirahito jIrNo 'haM jAto 'hamAyuShmAngauraH kR^iShNo mR^ita ityAdipratyakShAnubhavavattadupapatteH /
sarvamapyetatsatyamiti cedastyevaitadevaM duravagamaM yena devarAjo 'pyudasharAvAdidarshitAvinAshayuktirapi mumohaivAtra vinAshamevApIto bhavatIti /
tathA virocano mahAprAj~naH prAjApatyo 'pi dehamAtrAtmadarshano babhUva /
tathendrasyA'tmavinAshabhayasAgara eva vainAshikA nyamajjan /
tathA sAMkhyA draShTAraM dehAdivyatiriktamavagamyApi tyaktAgamapramANatvAnmR^ityuviShaya evAnyatvadarshane tasthuH /
tathAnye kANAdAdidarshanAH kaShAyaraktamiva kShArAdibhirvasraM navabhirAtmaguNairyuktamAtmadravyaM vishodhayituM pravR^ittAH /
tathAnye karmiNo bAhyaviShayApahR^itacetaso vedapramANA api paramArthasatyamAtmaikatvaM vinAshamivendravanmanyamAnA ghaTIyantravadArohAvarohaprakArairanishaM bambhramati /
kimanye kShudrajantavo vivekahInAH svabhAvata eva bahirviShayApahR^itacetasaH /
tasmAdidaM tyaktasarvabAhyaiShaNairananyasharaNaiH paramahaMsaparivrAjakairatyAshramibhirvedAntavij~nAnaparaireva vedanIyaM pUjyatamaiH prAjApatyaM cemaM saMpradAyamanusaradbhirupanibaddhaM prakaraNacatuShTayena /
tathAnushAsatyadyApi ta eva nAnya iti //1 //

START ChUp 8,12.2

#<asharIro vAyuH |

ChUpBh_8,12.2 tatrAsharIrasya saMprasAdasyAvidyayA sharIreNAvisheShatAM sasarIratAmeva saMprAptasya sharIrAtsamutthAya svena rUpeNa yathAbhiniShpattistathA vaktavyeti dR^iShTAnta ucyate-asharIro vAyuravidyamAnaM shiraHpANyAdimaccharIramasyetyasharIraH /

START ChUp 8,12.3

#<evam evaiSha saMprasAdo 'smAc charIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotir upasaMpadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate |
sa uttamapuruShaH |
sa tatra paryeti jakShat krIDan ramamANaH strIbhir vA yAnair vA j~nAtibhir vA nopajanaM smarann idaM sharIram |

ChUpBh_8,12.3 yathAyaM dR^iShTAnto vAyvAdInAmAkAshAdisAmyagamanavadavidyayA saMsArAvasthAyAM sharIrasAmyamApanno 'hamamuShya putro jAto jIrNo mariShya ityevaMprakAraM prajApatineva maghavAnyathoktena krameNa nAsi tvaM dehendriyAdidharmA tattvamasIti pratibodhitaH sansa eSha saMprasAdo jIvo 'smAccharIrAdAkAshAdiva vAyvAdayaH samutthAya dehAdivailakShaNyamAtmano rUpamavagamya dehAtmabhAvanAM hitvetyetat /

tatsmaraNe hi duHkhameva syAt /
duHkhAtmakatvAttasya /
nanvanubhUtaM cenna smaredasarvaj~natvaM muktasya /
naiSha doShaH /
yena mithyAj~nAnAdinA janitaM tacca mithyAj~nAnAdi vidyayoccheditamatastannAnubhUtameveti na tadasmaraNe sarvaj~natvahAniH /
na hyu nmattena grahagR^ihItena vA yadanubhUtaM tadunmAdAdyapadame 'pi smartavyaM syAttathehApi saMsAribhiravidyAdoShavadbhiryadanubhUyate tatsarvAtmAnamasharIraM na spR^ishati /
avidyAnimittAbhAvAt /
ye tUcchinnadoShairmR^iditakaShAyairmAnasAH satyAH kAmA anR^itApidhAnA anubhUyante vidyAbhivyaN^gyatvAtta eva muktena sarvAtmabhUtena saMbadhyanta ityAtmaj~nAnastutaye nirdishyante 'taH sAdhvetadvishinaShTi-ya ete brahmaloka iti /
yatra kvacana bhavanto 'pi brahmaNyeva hi te loke bhavantIti sarvAtmatvAdbrahmaNa ucyante /
nanu kathamekaH'sannAnyatpashyati nAnyadvijAnAti sa bhUmA'kAmAMshca brAhmalaukikAn'pashyan ramata'iti ca viruddham /
yathaiko yasminneva kShaNe pashyati sa tasminneva kShaNe na pashyati ceti /
naiSha doShaH /
shrutyantare parihR^itatvAt /
draShTurdR^iShTeraviparilopAtpashyanneva bhavati /
draShTuranyatvena kAmAnAmabhAvAnna pashyati ceti /
yadyapi suShupte taduktaM muktasyApi sarvaikatvAtsamAno dvitIyAbhAvaH /
kena kaM pashyediti coktameva /
asharIrasvarUpo 'pahatapApmAdilakShaNaH sankathameSha puruSho 'kShiNi dR^ishyata ityuktaH prajApatinA /
tatra yathAsAvakShiNi sAkShAddR^ishyate tadvaktavyamitIdamArabhyate /
tatra ko heturakShiNi darshana ityAha-sa dR^iShTAnto yathA prayogyaH prayogyaparo vA sashabdaH /
prayujyata iti prayogyo 'shvo balIvarde vA /
yathA loka AcaratyanenetyAcaraNo ratho 'no vA tasminnAcaraNe yuktastadAkarShaNAya, evamasmiJNcharIre rathasthAnIye prANaH paJNcavR^ittirindriyamanobuddhisaMyuktaH praj~nAtmA vij~nAnakriyAshaktidvayasaMmUrchitAtmA yuktaH svakarmaphalopabhoganimittaM niyuktaH /
kasminnvahamutkrAnta utkrAnto bhavisaShyAmi kasminvA pratiShThite pratiShThAsyAmIti /

START ChUp 8,12.4

#<atha yatraitad AkAsham anuviShaNNaM cakShuH sa cAkShuShaH puruSho darshanAya cakShuH |

START ChUp 8,12.5

#<atha yo vededaM manvAnIti sa AtmA |

ChUpBh_8,12.5 atha yo vedadaM manvAnIti mananavyApAramindriyAsaMspR^iShTaM kevalaM manvAnIti veda sa AtmA mananAya manaH /

START ChUp 8,12.6

START ChUp 8,14.1

#<AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA |
te yadantarA tad brahma tad amR^itaM sa AtmA |
prajApateH sabhAM veshma prapadye yasho 'haM bhavAmi brAhmaNAnAM yasho rAj~nAm yasho vishAm |

ChUpBh_8,14.1 AkAsho vA ityAdi brahmaNo lakShaNanirdeshArthamAdhyAnAya /
AkAsho vai nAma shrutiShu prasiddha AtmA /
AkAsha ivAsharIratvAsUkShmatvAcca /

taccA'tmA brahmAmR^itamamaraNadharmA /
ata Urdhva mantraH /
prajApatishcaturmukhastasya sabhAM veshma prabhuvimitaM veshma prapadye gaccheyam /

te 'pyadhikR^itA eveti teShAmapyAtmA bhavAmi /
tadyasho 'hamanuprApatsyanuprAptumicchAmi sa hAhaM yashasAmAtmanAM dehendriyamanobuddhilakShaNAnAmAtmA /
kimarthamahamevaM prapadya iti, ucyate-shyetaM varNataH pakvabadarasamaM rohitam /

yadevaMlakShaNaM shyetaM lindu picchilaM tanmAbhigAM mAbhigaccheyam /
dvirvacanamatyantAnarthahetutvapradarshanArtham //1//

START ChUp 8,15.1

#<tad dhaitad brahmA prajApataya uvAca prajApatir manave manuH prajAbhyaH |
AcAryakulAd vedam adhItya yathAvidhAnaM guroH karmAtisheSheNAbhisamAvR^itya kuTumbe shucau deshe svAdhyAyam adhIyAno dharmikAn vidadhad Atmani sarvendriyANi saMpratiShThApyAhiMsan sarvabhUtAny anyatra tIrthebhyaH |

ChUpBh_8,15.1 taddhaitadAtmaj~nAnaM sopakaraNamomityetadakSharamityAdyaiH sahopAsanaistadvAcakena granthenAShTAdhyAyIlakShaNena saha brahmA hiraNyagarbhaH parameshvaro vA taddvAreNa prajApataye kashyapAyovAca /
asAvapi manave svaputrAya /
manuH prajAbhya ityevaM shrutyarthasaMpradAyaparamparayA'gatamupaniShadvij~nAnamadyApi vidvatsvavagamyate /
yatheha ShaShThAdyadhyAyatraye prakAshitAtmavidyA saphalAvagamyate tathA karmaNAM na kashcanArtha iti prApte tadAnarthakyaprAptiparijihIrShayedaM karmaNo vidvadbhiranuShThIyamAnasya vishiShTaphalavattvenArthavattvamucyate-AcAryakulAdvedamadhItya sahArthato 'dhyayanaM kR^itvA yathAvidhAnaM yathAsmR^ityuktairniyamairyuktaH sannityarthaH /

evaM hi niyamavatAdhIto vedaH karmaj~nAnaphalaprAptaye bhavati nAnyathetyabhiprAyaH /
abhisamAvR^itya dharmajij~nAsAM samApayitvA gurukulannivR^itya nyAyato dArAnAhR^itya kuTumbe sthitvA gArhatthve vihite karmaNi tiShThannityarthaH /
tatrApi gArhasthyavihitAnAM karmaNAM svAdhyAyasya prAdhAnyapradarshanArthamucyate-shucau vivikte 'medhyAdirahite deshe yatAvadAsInaH svAdhyAyamadhIyAno naityakamadhikaM ca yathAshakti R^igAdyabhyAsaM ca kurvandhArmikAnputrA¤shiShyAMshca dharmayuktAnvidadhaddhArmikatvena tAnniyamayannAtmani svahR^idaye hArde brahmaNi sarvendriyANi saMpratiShThApyopasaMhR^ityendriyagrahaNAtkarmANi ca saMnyasyAhiMsahiMnsAM parapIDAmakurvansarvabhUtAni sthAvarajaN^gamAni bhUtAnyapIDayannityarthaH /
bhikShAnimittamaTanAdinApi parapIDA syAdityata Aha-anyatra tIrthebhyaH /
tIrthaM nAma shAsrAnuj~nAviShayastato 'nyatretyarthaH /
sarvAshramiNAM caitatsamAnam tIrthebhyo 'nyatrahiMsaiveti /
anye varNayanti kuTumba evaitatsarvaM kurvansa khalvadhikR^ito yAvadAyuShaM yAvajjIvamevaMyathoktena prakAreNaiva vartayanbrahmalokamabhisaMpadyatedehAnte /
na ca punarAvartate sharIragrahaNAya /
punarAvR^itteH prAptAyAH pratiShedhAt /
arcirAdinA mArgeNa kAryabrahmalokabhisaMpadya yAvadbrahmalokasthitistAvattatraiva tiShThati prAktato nA'vartata ityarthaH /
dvirabhyAsa upaniShadvidyAparisamAptyarthaH //1 // //
